* ‚ùå **Robot Answer:** "‡§∏‡§∞, ‡§®‡§ø‡§Ø‡§Æ ‡§§‡•ã ‡§®‡§ø‡§Ø‡§Æ ‡§π‡•à‡•§ ‡§Æ‡•à‡§Ç ‡§ï‡•Å‡§õ ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç ‡§ï‡§∞ ‡§∏‡§ï‡§§‡§æ‡•§" (Inhumane).
* ‚úÖ **The Officer Answer (Compassionate Discretion):**
> "Sir, ‡§Æ‡•à‡§Ç ‡§â‡§∏‡•á ‡§≠‡•Ç‡§ñ‡§æ ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç ‡§∞‡§π‡§®‡•á ‡§¶‡•Ç‡§Ç‡§ó‡§æ, ‡§≤‡•á‡§ï‡§ø‡§® ‡§Æ‡•à‡§Ç ‡§∏‡§ø‡§∏‡•ç‡§ü‡§Æ ‡§ï‡•á ‡§®‡§ø‡§Ø‡§Æ ‡§≠‡•Ä ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç ‡§§‡•ã‡§°‡§º‡•Ç‡§Ç‡§ó‡§æ‡•§
> 1. **Immediate Relief:** ‡§Æ‡•à‡§Ç ‡§Ö‡§™‡§®‡•á **'Discretionary Fund'** (‡§µ‡§ø‡§µ‡•á‡§ï‡§æ‡§ß‡§ø‡§ï‡§æ‡§∞ ‡§ï‡•ã‡§∑) ‡§Ø‡§æ ‡§Ö‡§™‡§®‡•Ä ‡§ú‡•á‡§¨ ‡§∏‡•á ‡§§‡•Å‡§∞‡§Ç‡§§ ‡§â‡§∏‡§ï‡•á ‡§≠‡•ã‡§ú‡§® ‡§ï‡•Ä ‡§µ‡•ç‡§Ø‡§µ‡§∏‡•ç‡§•‡§æ ‡§ï‡§∞‡•Ç‡§Å‡§ó‡§æ‡•§
> 2. **Systemic Fix:** ‡§Æ‡•à‡§Ç ‡§§‡•Å‡§∞‡§Ç‡§§ ‡§∏‡§Ç‡§¨‡§Ç‡§ß‡§ø‡§§ ‡§Ö‡§ß‡§ø‡§ï‡§æ‡§∞‡•Ä ‡§ï‡•ã ‡§¨‡•Å‡§≤‡§æ‡§ï‡§∞ ‡§â‡§∏‡§ï‡§æ ‡§Ü‡§ß‡§æ‡§∞/‡§∞‡§æ‡§∂‡§® ‡§ï‡§æ‡§∞‡•ç‡§° ‡§¨‡§®‡§µ‡§æ‡§®‡•á ‡§ï‡•Ä ‡§™‡•ç‡§∞‡§ï‡•ç‡§∞‡§ø‡§Ø‡§æ ‡§∂‡•Å‡§∞‡•Ç ‡§ï‡§∞‡§µ‡§æ‡§ä‡§Ç‡§ó‡§æ‡•§
> ‡§Æ‡•á‡§∞‡§æ ‡§≤‡§ï‡•ç‡§∑‡•ç‡§Ø ‡§®‡§ø‡§Ø‡§Æ ‡§§‡•ã‡§°‡§º‡§®‡§æ ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç, ‡§¨‡§≤‡•ç‡§ï‡§ø ‡§®‡§ø‡§Ø‡§Æ ‡§ï‡•á ‡§¶‡§æ‡§Ø‡§∞‡•á ‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç ‡§â‡§∏‡§ï‡•Ä ‡§Æ‡§¶‡§¶ ‡§ï‡§∞‡§®‡§æ ‡§π‡•à‡•§"
> 
> 



#### **Scenario 3: The "Rioting Mob" (Women & Children)**

**Question:** *"A mob is attacking a police station. There are women and children in the front row as shields. Will you order firing?"*

* ‚ùå **Hesitant Answer:** "‡§∏‡§∞, ‡§¨‡§ö‡•ç‡§ö‡•á ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç... ‡§Æ‡•à‡§Ç ‡§ó‡•ã‡§≤‡•Ä ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç ‡§ö‡§≤‡§æ ‡§∏‡§ï‡§§‡§æ‡•§" (Station ‡§ú‡§≤ ‡§ú‡§æ‡§è‡§ó‡§æ).
* ‚úÖ **The Officer Answer (SOP Based):**
> "Sir, ‡§Æ‡•á‡§∞‡•Ä ‡§™‡•ç‡§∞‡§æ‡§•‡§Æ‡§ø‡§ï‡§§‡§æ ‡§ú‡§æ‡§®-‡§Æ‡§æ‡§≤ ‡§ï‡•Ä ‡§∞‡§ï‡•ç‡§∑‡§æ ‡§î‡§∞ 'Rule of Law' ‡§π‡•à‡•§
> ‡§Æ‡•à‡§Ç **Standard Operating Procedure (SOP)** ‡§ï‡§æ ‡§™‡§æ‡§≤‡§® ‡§ï‡§∞‡•Ç‡§Å‡§ó‡§æ:
> 1. Public Announcement (‡§ö‡•á‡§§‡§æ‡§µ‡§®‡•Ä)‡•§
> 2. Water Cannon / Tear Gas (‡§≠‡•Ä‡§°‡§º ‡§§‡§ø‡§§‡§∞-‡§¨‡§ø‡§§‡§∞ ‡§ï‡§∞‡§®‡•á ‡§ï‡•á ‡§≤‡§ø‡§è)‡•§
> 3. Lathi Charge (‡§ï‡§Æ‡§∞ ‡§∏‡•á ‡§®‡•Ä‡§ö‡•á)‡•§
> ‡§Ö‡§ó‡§∞ ‡§´‡§ø‡§∞ ‡§≠‡•Ä ‡§∏‡•ç‡§•‡§ø‡§§‡§ø ‡§¨‡•á‡§ï‡§æ‡§¨‡•Ç ‡§π‡•ã‡§§‡•Ä ‡§π‡•à ‡§î‡§∞ ‡§™‡•Å‡§≤‡§ø‡§∏ ‡§¨‡§≤ ‡§ï‡•Ä ‡§ú‡§æ‡§® ‡§ï‡•ã ‡§ñ‡§§‡§∞‡§æ ‡§π‡•à, ‡§§‡•ã **Last Resort** ‡§ï‡•á ‡§∞‡•Ç‡§™ ‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç 'Minimum Force' ‡§ï‡§æ ‡§Ü‡§¶‡•á‡§∂ ‡§¶‡•Ç‡§Ç‡§ó‡§æ, ‡§≤‡•á‡§ï‡§ø‡§® Firing ‡§π‡§µ‡§æ ‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç ‡§Ø‡§æ ‡§™‡•à‡§∞‡•ã‡§Ç ‡§™‡§∞ ‡§π‡•ã‡§ó‡•Ä‡•§ ‡§π‡§ø‡§Ç‡§∏‡§æ ‡§ï‡•ã ‡§∞‡•ã‡§ï‡§®‡§æ ‡§Æ‡•á‡§∞‡•Ä ‡§°‡•ç‡§Ø‡•Ç‡§ü‡•Ä ‡§π‡•à‡•§"
> 
> 



#### **Scenario 4: The "Bribe" (Indirect Offer)**

**Question:** *"A contractor visits your home on Diwali with a generic 'Gift Box' (Sweets + Gold Coin). He has a tender pending with you. What will you do?"*

* ‚ùå **Angry Answer:** "‡§Æ‡•à‡§Ç ‡§â‡§∏‡•á ‡§ß‡§ï‡•ç‡§ï‡•á ‡§Æ‡§æ‡§∞‡§ï‡§∞ ‡§¨‡§æ‡§π‡§∞ ‡§®‡§ø‡§ï‡§æ‡§≤ ‡§¶‡•Ç‡§Ç‡§ó‡§æ‡•§" (Over-reaction).
* ‚úÖ **The Officer Answer:**
> "Sir, ‡§Æ‡•à‡§Ç ‡§Æ‡§ø‡§†‡§æ‡§à ‡§∏‡•ç‡§µ‡•Ä‡§ï‡§æ‡§∞ ‡§ï‡§∞ ‡§∏‡§ï‡§§‡§æ ‡§π‡•Ç‡§Å (‡§∂‡§∑‡•ç‡§ü‡§æ‡§ö‡§æ‡§∞ ‡§µ‡§∂), ‡§≤‡•á‡§ï‡§ø‡§® ‡§ï‡§ø‡§∏‡•Ä ‡§≠‡•Ä ‡§ï‡•Ä‡§Æ‡§§‡•Ä ‡§â‡§™‡§π‡§æ‡§∞ (Gold Coin) ‡§ï‡•ã ‡§µ‡§ø‡§®‡§Æ‡•ç‡§∞‡§§‡§æ‡§™‡•Ç‡§∞‡•ç‡§µ‡§ï ‡§Ö‡§∏‡•ç‡§µ‡•Ä‡§ï‡§æ‡§∞ (Refuse) ‡§ï‡§∞ ‡§¶‡•Ç‡§Ç‡§ó‡§æ‡•§
> ‡§Æ‡•à‡§Ç ‡§â‡§∏‡•á ‡§∏‡•ç‡§™‡§∑‡•ç‡§ü ‡§ï‡§∞ ‡§¶‡•Ç‡§Ç‡§ó‡§æ ‡§ï‡§ø ‡§Æ‡•á‡§∞‡•á ‡§µ‡•ç‡§Ø‡§ï‡•ç‡§§‡§ø‡§ó‡§§ ‡§∏‡§Ç‡§¨‡§Ç‡§ß ‡§î‡§∞ ‡§Æ‡•á‡§∞‡§æ ‡§ï‡§æ‡§∞‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ‡§≤‡§Ø (Office) ‡§Ö‡§≤‡§ó-‡§Ö‡§≤‡§ó ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç‡•§ ‡§Æ‡•à‡§Ç ‡§∏‡•Å‡§®‡§ø‡§∂‡•ç‡§ö‡§ø‡§§ ‡§ï‡§∞‡•Ç‡§Å‡§ó‡§æ ‡§ï‡§ø ‡§ü‡•á‡§Ç‡§°‡§∞ ‡§™‡•ç‡§∞‡§ï‡•ç‡§∞‡§ø‡§Ø‡§æ ‡§™‡•Ç‡§∞‡•Ä ‡§§‡§∞‡§π ‡§™‡§æ‡§∞‡§¶‡§∞‡•ç‡§∂‡•Ä (Transparent) ‡§∞‡§π‡•á ‡§§‡§æ‡§ï‡§ø ‡§ï‡•ã‡§à ‡§∏‡§Ç‡§¶‡•á‡§π ‡§® ‡§π‡•ã‡•§"



#### **Scenario 5: The "Personal vs Professional" Conflict**

**Question:** *"Your own brother is caught in a drunk & drive case in your district. Police calls you. What will you do?"*

* ‚ùå **Corrupt Answer:** "‡§õ‡•ã‡§ü‡§æ ‡§Æ‡§æ‡§Æ‡§≤‡§æ ‡§π‡•à, ‡§õ‡•Å‡§°‡§º‡§µ‡§æ ‡§¶‡•Ç‡§Ç‡§ó‡§æ‡•§"
* ‚ùå **Show-off Answer:** "‡§Æ‡•à‡§Ç ‡§™‡•Å‡§≤‡§ø‡§∏ ‡§ï‡•ã ‡§¨‡•ã‡§≤‡•Ç‡§Ç‡§ó‡§æ ‡§â‡§∏‡•á ‡§∏‡§¨‡§∏‡•á ‡§ú‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ‡§¶‡§æ ‡§∏‡§ú‡§æ ‡§¶‡•á‡§Ç‡•§" (Unnatural).
* ‚úÖ **The Officer Answer:**
> "Sir, ‡§Æ‡•à‡§Ç ‡§™‡•Å‡§≤‡§ø‡§∏ ‡§Ö‡§ß‡§ø‡§ï‡§æ‡§∞‡•Ä ‡§∏‡•á ‡§ï‡§π‡•Ç‡§Ç‡§ó‡§æ ‡§ï‡§ø ‡§µ‡•ã ‡§ï‡§æ‡§®‡•Ç‡§® ‡§ï‡•á ‡§Ö‡§®‡•Å‡§∏‡§æ‡§∞ (As per law) ‡§ï‡§æ‡§∞‡•ç‡§∞‡§µ‡§æ‡§à ‡§ï‡§∞‡•á‡§Ç‡•§
> ‡§Æ‡•à‡§Ç ‡§® ‡§§‡•ã ‡§â‡§∏‡•á ‡§¨‡§ö‡§æ‡§®‡•á ‡§ï‡•á ‡§≤‡§ø‡§è ‡§∏‡§ø‡§´‡§æ‡§∞‡§ø‡§∂ ‡§ï‡§∞‡•Ç‡§Å‡§ó‡§æ, ‡§î‡§∞ ‡§® ‡§π‡•Ä ‡§â‡§∏‡•á ‡§è‡§ï‡•ç‡§∏‡•ç‡§ü‡•ç‡§∞‡§æ ‡§∏‡§ú‡§æ ‡§¶‡§ø‡§≤‡§µ‡§æ‡§®‡•á ‡§ï‡•á ‡§≤‡§ø‡§è ‡§ï‡§π‡•Ç‡§Ç‡§ó‡§æ‡•§
> ‡§Æ‡•à‡§Ç ‡§ñ‡•Å‡§¶ ‡§ï‡•ã ‡§á‡§∏ ‡§Æ‡§æ‡§Æ‡§≤‡•á ‡§∏‡•á **'Recuse'** (‡§Ö‡§≤‡§ó) ‡§ï‡§∞ ‡§≤‡•Ç‡§Ç‡§ó‡§æ ‡§§‡§æ‡§ï‡§ø ‡§ú‡§æ‡§Ç‡§ö ‡§®‡§ø‡§∑‡•ç‡§™‡§ï‡•ç‡§∑ ‡§π‡•ã‡•§"



---

### **3. Potential Board Questions (Dilemma Specific)**

‡§á‡§® ‡§∏‡§µ‡§æ‡§≤‡•ã‡§Ç ‡§ï‡•á ‡§ú‡§µ‡§æ‡§¨ **"Hierarchy of Duty"** (‡§∏‡§Ç‡§µ‡§ø‡§ß‡§æ‡§® > ‡§ú‡§®‡§§‡§æ > ‡§Ü‡§¶‡•á‡§∂) ‡§ï‡•á ‡§Ü‡§ß‡§æ‡§∞ ‡§™‡§∞ ‡§§‡•à‡§Ø‡§æ‡§∞ ‡§ï‡§∞‡•á‡§Ç‡•§

**Type A: Corruption & Integrity**

1. *"‡§ï‡§π‡§æ ‡§ú‡§æ‡§§‡§æ ‡§π‡•à ‡§ï‡§ø ‡§≠‡§æ‡§∞‡§§ ‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç ‡§¨‡§ø‡§®‡§æ ‡§™‡•à‡§∏‡•á ‡§¶‡§ø‡§è ‡§´‡§æ‡§á‡§≤ ‡§Ü‡§ó‡•á ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç ‡§¨‡§¢‡§º‡§§‡•Ä‡•§ ‡§Ü‡§™ ‡§è‡§ï ‡§à‡§Æ‡§æ‡§®‡§¶‡§æ‡§∞ ‡§Ö‡§ß‡§ø‡§ï‡§æ‡§∞‡•Ä ‡§ï‡•á ‡§∞‡•Ç‡§™ ‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç ‡§á‡§∏ 'System' ‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç ‡§ï‡•à‡§∏‡•á ‡§ï‡§æ‡§Æ ‡§ï‡§∞‡•á‡§Ç‡§ó‡•á?"*
* *(Hint: Focus on digitization, transparency, and personal example. Don't fight everyone, just keep your table clean).*


2. *"‡§ï‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ ‡§µ‡•ç‡§π‡§ø‡§∏‡§≤‡§¨‡•ç‡§≤‡•ã‡§Ö‡§∞ (Whistleblower) ‡§¨‡§®‡§®‡§æ ‡§∏‡§π‡•Ä ‡§π‡•à, ‡§≠‡§≤‡•á ‡§π‡•Ä ‡§á‡§∏‡§∏‡•á ‡§µ‡§ø‡§≠‡§æ‡§ó ‡§ï‡•Ä ‡§¨‡§¶‡§®‡§æ‡§Æ‡•Ä ‡§π‡•ã?"*

**Type B: Social Pressure**
3.  *"‡§Ü‡§™‡§ï‡•á ‡§∏‡§Æ‡§æ‡§ú/‡§ú‡§æ‡§§‡§ø ‡§ï‡•á ‡§≤‡•ã‡§ó ‡§Ü‡§™‡§∏‡•á ‡§â‡§Æ‡•ç‡§Æ‡•Ä‡§¶ ‡§ï‡§∞‡•á‡§Ç‡§ó‡•á ‡§ï‡§ø ‡§Ü‡§™ ‡§â‡§®‡§ï‡•á ‡§≤‡§ø‡§è '‡§´‡•á‡§µ‡§∞' ‡§ï‡§∞‡•á‡§Ç‡•§ ‡§Ü‡§™ ‡§â‡§®‡•ç‡§π‡•á‡§Ç ‡§ï‡•à‡§∏‡•á ‡§Æ‡§®‡§æ ‡§ï‡§∞‡•á‡§Ç‡§ó‡•á ‡§¨‡§ø‡§®‡§æ ‡§∏‡§Ç‡§¨‡§Ç‡§ß ‡§ñ‡§∞‡§æ‡§¨ ‡§ï‡§ø‡§è?"*
* *(Hint: "‡§Æ‡•à‡§Ç ‡§â‡§®‡•ç‡§π‡•á‡§Ç ‡§∏‡§Æ‡§ù‡§æ‡§ä‡§Ç‡§ó‡§æ ‡§ï‡§ø ‡§Æ‡•à‡§Ç ‡§∏‡§Æ‡§æ‡§ú ‡§ï‡§æ ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç, ‡§∏‡§Ç‡§µ‡§ø‡§ß‡§æ‡§® ‡§ï‡§æ ‡§∏‡•á‡§µ‡§ï ‡§π‡•Ç‡§Å‡•§ ‡§Æ‡•à‡§Ç ‡§â‡§®‡§ï‡•Ä ‡§≤‡•Ä‡§ó‡§≤ ‡§Æ‡§¶‡§¶ ‡§ï‡§∞‡•Ç‡§Å‡§ó‡§æ, ‡§á‡§≤‡•Ä‡§ó‡§≤ ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç‡•§")*

**Type C: Crisis Management**
4.  *"Fake Encounter (‡§´‡§∞‡•ç‡§ú‡•Ä ‡§Æ‡•Å‡§†‡§≠‡•á‡§°‡§º) ‡§ï‡•á ‡§¨‡§æ‡§∞‡•á ‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç ‡§Ü‡§™‡§ï‡•Ä ‡§ï‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ ‡§∞‡§æ‡§Ø ‡§π‡•à? ‡§ï‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ ‡§§‡•ç‡§µ‡§∞‡§ø‡§§ ‡§®‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ‡§Ø (Instant Justice) ‡§ï‡•á ‡§≤‡§ø‡§è ‡§Ø‡§π ‡§ï‡§≠‡•Ä-‡§ï‡§≠‡•Ä ‡§ú‡§∞‡•Ç‡§∞‡•Ä ‡§π‡•à?"*
* *(Warning: Never support fake encounters. It is murder. Always support 'Due Process of Law').*

---

### **4. How to Prepare (The Perfect Way: Dilemma Training)**

Ethical situations ‡§ï‡•á ‡§≤‡§ø‡§è ‡§≤‡§Ç‡§¨‡•á answers ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç ‡§ö‡§æ‡§π‡§ø‡§è‡•§ ‡§Ü‡§™‡§ï‡•ã **"Decision"** ‡§≤‡•á‡§®‡§æ ‡§Ü‡§®‡§æ ‡§ö‡§æ‡§π‡§ø‡§è‡•§

#### **Drill 1: The "One-Line Decision" (Rapid Fire)**

* **Task:** ‡§Ö‡§™‡§®‡•á ‡§¶‡•ã‡§∏‡•ç‡§§ ‡§∏‡•á ‡§ï‡§π‡•á‡§Ç ‡§ï‡§ø ‡§µ‡•ã ‡§Ü‡§™‡§ï‡•ã situation ‡§¶‡•á, ‡§î‡§∞ ‡§Ü‡§™ 5 ‡§∏‡•á‡§ï‡§Ç‡§° ‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç ‡§´‡•à‡§∏‡§≤‡§æ ‡§∏‡•Å‡§®‡§æ‡§è‡§Ç‡•§
* **Example:**
* *Friend:* "‡§¶‡§Ç‡§ó‡§æ ‡§π‡•ã ‡§∞‡§π‡§æ ‡§π‡•à, ‡§ó‡•ã‡§≤‡•Ä ‡§ö‡§≤‡§æ‡§ì‡§ó‡•á?"
* *You:* "Only as a last resort after SOP."
* *Friend:* "‡§∏‡•Ä‡§®‡§ø‡§Ø‡§∞ ‡§®‡•á ‡§ù‡•Ç‡§†‡•á ‡§¨‡§ø‡§≤ ‡§™‡§∞ ‡§∏‡§æ‡§á‡§® ‡§ï‡§∞‡§®‡•á ‡§ï‡•ã ‡§ï‡§π‡§æ‡•§"
* *You:* "Refuse politely, ask for written order."



#### **Drill 2: The "Written Order" Visualization**

* **Task:** ‡§ï‡§≤‡•ç‡§™‡§®‡§æ ‡§ï‡§∞‡•á‡§Ç ‡§ï‡§ø ‡§è‡§ï ‡§Æ‡§Ç‡§§‡•ç‡§∞‡•Ä ‡§Ü‡§™ ‡§™‡§∞ ‡§ö‡§ø‡§≤‡•ç‡§≤‡§æ ‡§∞‡§π‡§æ ‡§π‡•à‡•§
* **Action:** ‡§∂‡•Ä‡§∂‡•á ‡§ï‡•á ‡§∏‡§æ‡§Æ‡§®‡•á ‡§ñ‡§°‡§º‡•á ‡§π‡•ã‡§ï‡§∞ ‡§Ø‡§π ‡§µ‡§æ‡§ï‡•ç‡§Ø (Sentence) ‡§¨‡•ã‡§≤‡§®‡•á ‡§ï‡•Ä ‡§™‡•ç‡§∞‡•à‡§ï‡•ç‡§ü‡§ø‡§∏ ‡§ï‡§∞‡•á‡§Ç:
* *"Sir, I respect your authority, but I cannot violate the rules. Please give this to me in writing, and I will execute it instantly."*
* (‡§á‡§∏‡•á ‡§µ‡§ø‡§®‡§Æ‡•ç‡§∞‡§§‡§æ (Politeness) ‡§î‡§∞ ‡§¶‡•É‡§¢‡§º‡§§‡§æ (Firmness) ‡§ï‡•á ‡§∏‡§æ‡§• ‡§¨‡•ã‡§≤‡•á‡§Ç‡•§)



---

### **5. Neuro-Interrogation (Self-Reflection)**

1. **Fear Check:** *"‡§ï‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ ‡§Æ‡•à‡§Ç 'Transfer' ‡§Ø‡§æ 'Suspension' ‡§∏‡•á ‡§°‡§∞‡§§‡§æ ‡§π‡•Ç‡§Å?"*
* (‡§è‡§ï Officer ‡§ï‡•ã ‡§™‡§§‡§æ ‡§π‡•ã‡§§‡§æ ‡§π‡•à ‡§ï‡§ø ‡§ü‡•ç‡§∞‡§æ‡§Ç‡§∏‡§´‡§∞ ‡§®‡•å‡§ï‡§∞‡•Ä ‡§ï‡§æ ‡§π‡§ø‡§∏‡•ç‡§∏‡§æ ‡§π‡•à‡•§ ‡§Ö‡§ó‡§∞ ‡§Ü‡§™ ‡§°‡§∞ ‡§ó‡§è, ‡§§‡•ã ‡§Ü‡§™ ‡§ï‡§æ‡§Æ ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç ‡§ï‡§∞ ‡§™‡§æ‡§è‡§Ç‡§ó‡•á‡•§)


2. **Anger Check:** *"‡§Ö‡§ó‡§∞ ‡§ï‡•ã‡§à ‡§Æ‡•Å‡§ù‡•á ‡§∞‡§ø‡§∂‡•ç‡§µ‡§§ ‡§ë‡§´‡§∞ ‡§ï‡§∞‡•á, ‡§§‡•ã ‡§ï‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ ‡§Æ‡•Å‡§ù‡•á ‡§ó‡•Å‡§∏‡•ç‡§∏‡§æ ‡§Ü‡§§‡§æ ‡§π‡•à?"*
* (‡§ó‡•Å‡§∏‡•ç‡§∏‡§æ ‡§Æ‡§§ ‡§ï‡•Ä‡§ú‡§ø‡§è‡•§ ‡§Ø‡§π ‡§è‡§ï professional hazard ‡§π‡•à‡•§ ‡§á‡§∏‡•á professional ‡§§‡§∞‡•Ä‡§ï‡•á ‡§∏‡•á handle ‡§ï‡§∞‡•á‡§Ç‡•§)



---

### **6. Overall Effect on Interview**

‡§ú‡§¨ ‡§Ü‡§™ Ethical Stress Tests ‡§ï‡•ã ‡§™‡§æ‡§∏ ‡§ï‡§∞ ‡§≤‡•á‡§§‡•á ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç:

1. **Reliability:** Board ‡§ï‡•ã ‡§≤‡§ó‡§§‡§æ ‡§π‡•à‚Äî *"‡§Ø‡§π ‡§µ‡•ç‡§Ø‡§ï‡•ç‡§§‡§ø ‡§¶‡§¨‡§æ‡§µ ‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç ‡§ü‡•Ç‡§ü‡§§‡§æ ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç ‡§π‡•à‡•§"*
2. **Safety:** ‡§â‡§®‡•ç‡§π‡•á‡§Ç ‡§™‡§§‡§æ ‡§π‡•à ‡§ï‡§ø ‡§Ü‡§™ ‡§ï‡§≤ ‡§ï‡•ã ‡§µ‡§ø‡§≠‡§æ‡§ó (Department) ‡§ï‡•á ‡§≤‡§ø‡§è ‡§∂‡§∞‡•ç‡§Æ‡§ø‡§Ç‡§¶‡§ó‡•Ä (Embarrassment) ‡§ï‡§æ ‡§ï‡§æ‡§∞‡§£ ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç ‡§¨‡§®‡•á‡§Ç‡§ó‡•á‡•§
3. **Maturity:** ‡§Ü‡§™ ‡§¶‡§ø‡§ñ‡§æ‡§§‡•á ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç ‡§ï‡§ø ‡§Ü‡§™ "‡§ï‡§ø‡§§‡§æ‡§¨‡•Ä ‡§Ü‡§¶‡§∞‡•ç‡§∂‡§µ‡§æ‡§¶‡•Ä" (Bookish Idealist) ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç, ‡§¨‡§≤‡•ç‡§ï‡§ø "‡§µ‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ‡§µ‡§π‡§æ‡§∞‡§ø‡§ï ‡§™‡•ç‡§∞‡§∂‡§æ‡§∏‡§ï" (Practical Administrator) ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç‡•§

---

### **Today's Action Plan (‡§Ü‡§ú ‡§ï‡§æ ‡§π‡•ã‡§Æ‡§µ‡§∞‡•ç‡§ï)**

1. **Visualize:** ‡§Ü‡§Ç‡§ñ‡•á‡§Ç ‡§¨‡§Ç‡§¶ ‡§ï‡§∞‡•á‡§Ç ‡§î‡§∞ ‡§∏‡•ã‡§ö‡•á‡§Ç ‡§ï‡§ø ‡§Ü‡§™ SP ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç ‡§î‡§∞ ‡§Ü‡§™‡§ï‡•á ‡§∏‡§æ‡§Æ‡§®‡•á ‡§≠‡•Ä‡§°‡§º ‡§¨‡§∏ ‡§ú‡§≤‡§æ ‡§∞‡§π‡•Ä ‡§π‡•à‡•§ ‡§Ü‡§™ ‡§ï‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ ‡§ë‡§∞‡•ç‡§°‡§∞ ‡§¶‡•á‡§Ç‡§ó‡•á? (Step-by-step ‡§∏‡•ã‡§ö‡•á‡§Ç)‡•§
2. **Draft:** *"Fake Encounter"* ‡§µ‡§æ‡§≤‡•á ‡§∏‡§µ‡§æ‡§≤ ‡§ï‡§æ 3-‡§≤‡§æ‡§á‡§® ‡§ï‡§æ ‡§ú‡§µ‡§æ‡§¨ ‡§≤‡§ø‡§ñ‡•á‡§Ç ‡§ú‡•ã 100% ‡§ï‡§º‡§æ‡§®‡•Ç‡§®‡•Ä ‡§π‡•ã‡•§
3. **Practice:** "‡§®‡§æ" (No) ‡§¨‡•ã‡§≤‡§®‡•á ‡§ï‡•Ä ‡§™‡•ç‡§∞‡•à‡§ï‡•ç‡§ü‡§ø‡§∏ ‡§ï‡§∞‡•á‡§Ç‡•§ ‡§µ‡§ø‡§®‡§Æ‡•ç‡§∞‡§§‡§æ ‡§∏‡•á, ‡§≤‡•á‡§ï‡§ø‡§® ‡§Æ‡§ú‡§¨‡•Ç‡§§‡•Ä ‡§∏‡•á‡•§

**Chapter Mantra:**

> *"‡§à‡§Æ‡§æ‡§®‡§¶‡§æ‡§∞‡•Ä (Integrity) ‡§ï‡§æ ‡§Æ‡§§‡§≤‡§¨ ‡§Ø‡§π ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç ‡§π‡•à ‡§ï‡§ø ‡§Ü‡§™ '‡§∏‡§Ç‡§§' ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç‡•§ ‡§á‡§∏‡§ï‡§æ ‡§Æ‡§§‡§≤‡§¨ ‡§π‡•à ‡§ï‡§ø ‡§Ü‡§™ '‡§¶‡§¨‡§æ‡§µ' (Pressure) ‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç ‡§≠‡•Ä ‡§®‡§ø‡§Ø‡§Æ‡•ã‡§Ç ‡§ï‡•á ‡§∏‡§æ‡§• ‡§ñ‡§°‡§º‡•á ‡§∞‡§π‡§§‡•á ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç‡•§"*

---

**Next:** **Chapter 12 (The Clean Miss Protocol)** ‚Äî ‡§ú‡§¨ ‡§ú‡§µ‡§æ‡§¨ *‡§®* ‡§Ü‡§§‡§æ ‡§π‡•ã, ‡§§‡•ã "Sorry" ‡§ï‡•à‡§∏‡•á ‡§¨‡•ã‡§≤‡•á‡§Ç ‡§ï‡§ø Board impress ‡§π‡•ã ‡§ú‡§æ‡§è‡•§ (The Art of saying No).





---



## Chapter 12: The "Clean Miss" Protocol (‡§®‡§æ ‡§ï‡§π‡§®‡•á ‡§ï‡•Ä ‡§ï‡§≤‡§æ)
This chapter teaches you the most underrated skill in an interview: **How to be "Ignorant" with Confidence.** (‡§Ö‡§ú‡•ç‡§û‡§æ‡§®‡§§‡§æ ‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç ‡§≠‡•Ä ‡§Ü‡§§‡•ç‡§Æ‡§µ‡§ø‡§∂‡•ç‡§µ‡§æ‡§∏ ‡§ï‡•à‡§∏‡•á ‡§¶‡§ø‡§ñ‡§æ‡§è‡§Ç).
**Core Focus:** Intellectual Honesty > Bluffing (‡§à‡§Æ‡§æ‡§®‡§¶‡§æ‡§∞‡•Ä ‡§§‡•Å‡§ï‡•ç‡§ï‡•á‡§¨‡§æ‡§ú‡•Ä ‡§∏‡•á ‡§¨‡§°‡§º‡•Ä ‡§π‡•à).
**The Strategy:** The Art of saying "No" confidently without looking weak.

---

### **Namaskar Future Officer.**

Interview ‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç ‡§è‡§ï ‡§ê‡§∏‡§æ moment ‡§ú‡§∞‡•Ç‡§∞ ‡§Ü‡§è‡§ó‡§æ ‡§ú‡§¨ Board ‡§Ü‡§™‡§∏‡•á ‡§ê‡§∏‡§æ ‡§∏‡§µ‡§æ‡§≤ ‡§™‡•Ç‡§õ‡•á‡§ó‡§æ ‡§ú‡§ø‡§∏‡§ï‡§æ ‡§ú‡§µ‡§æ‡§¨ ‡§Ü‡§™‡§ï‡•ã **‡§¨‡§ø‡§≤‡•ç‡§ï‡•Å‡§≤ ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç ‡§™‡§§‡§æ**‡•§

* *"What is the GDP contribution of the handloom sector in Bhagalpur?"*
* *"Tell us the 3rd clause of Article 371-D."*

‡§á‡§∏ moment ‡§™‡§∞ 90% students ‡§ò‡§¨‡§∞‡§æ ‡§ú‡§æ‡§§‡•á ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç‡•§ ‡§â‡§®‡•ç‡§π‡•á‡§Ç ‡§≤‡§ó‡§§‡§æ ‡§π‡•à‚Äî *"‡§Ö‡§ó‡§∞ ‡§Æ‡•à‡§Ç‡§®‡•á '‡§®‡§æ' ‡§¨‡•ã‡§≤‡§æ, ‡§§‡•ã ‡§Æ‡•á‡§∞‡•á ‡§®‡§Ç‡§¨‡§∞ ‡§ï‡§ü ‡§ú‡§æ‡§è‡§Ç‡§ó‡•á‡•§"*
‡§á‡§∏ ‡§°‡§∞ ‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç ‡§µ‡•ã **"Bluff" (‡§§‡•Å‡§ï‡•ç‡§ï‡§æ)** ‡§Æ‡§æ‡§∞‡§®‡§æ ‡§∂‡•Å‡§∞‡•Ç ‡§ï‡§∞‡§§‡•á ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç: *"Sir... I think... maybe 10%... not sure but..."*

‡§Ø‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç ‡§µ‡•ã ‡§Ö‡§™‡§®‡§æ Interview ‡§¨‡§∞‡•ç‡§¨‡§æ‡§¶ ‡§ï‡§∞ ‡§≤‡•á‡§§‡•á ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç‡•§

**Golden Rule:**

> *"Board ‡§ï‡•ã 'Google' ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç ‡§ö‡§æ‡§π‡§ø‡§è‡•§ ‡§â‡§®‡•ç‡§π‡•á‡§Ç ‡§è‡§ï ‡§ê‡§∏‡§æ Officer ‡§ö‡§æ‡§π‡§ø‡§è ‡§ú‡•ã ‡§Ö‡§™‡§®‡•Ä ‡§ï‡§Æ‡§ø‡§Ø‡•ã‡§Ç ‡§ï‡•ã ‡§∏‡•ç‡§µ‡•Ä‡§ï‡§æ‡§∞ ‡§ï‡§∞ ‡§∏‡§ï‡•á‡•§ ‡§ó‡§≤‡§§ ‡§ú‡§µ‡§æ‡§¨ ‡§¶‡•á‡§®‡§æ (Misinformation) ‡§™‡§æ‡§™ ‡§π‡•à, ‡§≤‡•á‡§ï‡§ø‡§® '‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç ‡§™‡§§‡§æ' ‡§¨‡•ã‡§≤‡§®‡§æ (Ignorance) ‡§ï‡•á‡§µ‡§≤ ‡§è‡§ï ‡§∏‡§ö‡•ç‡§ö‡§æ‡§à ‡§π‡•à‡•§"*

‡§ú‡•à‡§∏‡•á ‡§ï‡•ç‡§∞‡§ø‡§ï‡•á‡§ü ‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç, ‡§Ö‡§ó‡§∞ ‡§ó‡•á‡§Ç‡§¶ ‡§∏‡§Æ‡§ù ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç ‡§Ü‡§è, ‡§§‡•ã ‡§â‡§∏‡•á **"Clean Miss"** ‡§ï‡§∞ ‡§¶‡•á‡§®‡§æ (‡§õ‡•ã‡§°‡§º ‡§¶‡•á‡§®‡§æ) ‡§¨‡•á‡§π‡§§‡§∞ ‡§π‡•à‡•§ ‡§Ö‡§ó‡§∞ ‡§Ü‡§™ ‡§ú‡§¨‡§∞‡§¶‡§∏‡•ç‡§§‡•Ä ‡§¨‡§≤‡•ç‡§≤‡§æ ‡§ò‡•Å‡§Æ‡§æ‡§è‡§Ç‡§ó‡•á, ‡§§‡•ã **"Catch Out"** ‡§π‡•ã ‡§ú‡§æ‡§è‡§Ç‡§ó‡•á‡•§

---

### **1. The Core Mechanics: Types of "No"**

"‡§®‡§æ" ‡§¨‡•ã‡§≤‡§®‡•á ‡§ï‡•á ‡§≠‡•Ä ‡§§‡§∞‡•Ä‡§ï‡•á ‡§π‡•ã‡§§‡•á ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç‡•§ ‡§Ü‡§™‡§ï‡•ã Situation ‡§ï‡•á ‡§π‡§ø‡§∏‡§æ‡§¨ ‡§∏‡•á ‡§∏‡§π‡•Ä ‡§§‡§∞‡•Ä‡§ï‡§æ ‡§ö‡•Å‡§®‡§®‡§æ ‡§π‡•à:

#### **Type 1: The Direct Miss (‡§¨‡§ø‡§≤‡•ç‡§ï‡•Å‡§≤ ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç ‡§™‡§§‡§æ)**

* **Situation:** Factual ‡§∏‡§µ‡§æ‡§≤ (Data, Name, Date) ‡§ú‡•ã ‡§Ø‡§æ‡§¶ ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç ‡§π‡•à‡•§
* **Action:** ‡§∏‡•Ä‡§ß‡§æ ‡§Æ‡§®‡§æ ‡§ï‡§∞‡•á‡§Ç‡•§ ‡§ò‡•Å‡§Æ‡§æ‡§è‡§Ç ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç‡•§
* **Phrase:** *"Sorry Sir, I am not aware of this specific fact right now."* (‡§Æ‡§æ‡§´‡•Ä ‡§∏‡§∞, ‡§Æ‡•Å‡§ù‡•á ‡§Ö‡§≠‡•Ä ‡§á‡§∏ ‡§§‡§•‡•ç‡§Ø ‡§ï‡•Ä ‡§ú‡§æ‡§®‡§ï‡§æ‡§∞‡•Ä ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç ‡§π‡•à‡•§)

#### **Type 2: The Partial Miss (‡§ß‡•Å‡§Ç‡§ß‡§≤‡§æ ‡§Ø‡§æ‡§¶ ‡§π‡•à)**

* **Situation:** ‡§™‡§¢‡§º‡§æ ‡§•‡§æ, ‡§≤‡•á‡§ï‡§ø‡§® ‡§Ö‡§≠‡•Ä 100% sure ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç‡•§
* **Action:** ‡§Ö‡§®‡•Å‡§Æ‡§§‡§ø (Permission) ‡§≤‡•á‡§ï‡§∞ guess ‡§ï‡§∞‡•á‡§Ç‡•§
* **Phrase:** *"Sir, I am not entirely sure, but if you permit, I can make an educated guess?"* (‡§∏‡§∞, ‡§Æ‡•à‡§Ç ‡§™‡•Ç‡§∞‡•Ä ‡§§‡§∞‡§π ‡§Ü‡§∂‡•ç‡§µ‡§∏‡•ç‡§§ ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç ‡§π‡•Ç‡§Å, ‡§≤‡•á‡§ï‡§ø‡§® ‡§Ö‡§ó‡§∞ ‡§Ü‡§™ ‡§Ö‡§®‡•Å‡§Æ‡§§‡§ø ‡§¶‡•á‡§Ç ‡§§‡•ã ‡§Æ‡•à‡§Ç ‡§Ö‡§®‡•Å‡§Æ‡§æ‡§® ‡§≤‡§ó‡§æ ‡§∏‡§ï‡§§‡§æ ‡§π‡•Ç‡§Å?)
* *Note:* ‡§Ö‡§ó‡§∞ ‡§µ‡•ã "No" ‡§¨‡•ã‡§≤‡•á‡§Ç, ‡§§‡•ã ‡§ö‡•Å‡§™ ‡§π‡•ã ‡§ú‡§æ‡§è‡§Ç‡•§



#### **Type 3: The "Context" Miss (Topic ‡§™‡§§‡§æ ‡§π‡•à, Detail ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç)**

* **Situation:** Topic ‡§™‡§§‡§æ ‡§π‡•à, ‡§™‡§∞ ‡§µ‡•ã specific detail ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç ‡§™‡§§‡§æ ‡§ú‡•ã ‡§â‡§®‡•ç‡§π‡•ã‡§Ç‡§®‡•á ‡§™‡•Ç‡§õ‡•Ä‡•§
* **Action:** ‡§Ö‡§™‡§®‡•Ä ‡§ú‡§æ‡§®‡§ï‡§æ‡§∞‡•Ä ‡§ï‡•Ä ‡§∏‡•Ä‡§Æ‡§æ (Limit) ‡§¨‡§§‡§æ‡§è‡§Ç‡•§
* **Phrase:** *"Sir, I know about the general framework of this scheme, but I don't recall the exact budgetary allocation."*

---

### **2. The 5 Examples: Wrong vs. Clean Miss**

‡§®‡•Ä‡§ö‡•á 5 situations ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç‡•§ ‡§¶‡•á‡§ñ‡§ø‡§è ‡§ï‡•à‡§∏‡•á ‡§è‡§ï "Bluffer" ‡§´‡§Ç‡§∏‡§§‡§æ ‡§π‡•à ‡§î‡§∞ ‡§è‡§ï "Officer" ‡§á‡§ú‡•ç‡§ú‡§§ ‡§ï‡§Æ‡§æ‡§§‡§æ ‡§π‡•à‡•§

#### **Scenario 1: The "Data" Question**

**Question:** *"What is the exact Child Mortality Rate (CMR) of Purnia district?"*

* ‚ùå **The Bluffer:** "Sir... it is around 40... maybe 42... actually situation is improving..."
* *(Effect: Board ‡§ï‡•ã ‡§™‡§§‡§æ ‡§ö‡§≤ ‡§ó‡§Ø‡§æ ‡§Ü‡§™ ‡§´‡•á‡§Ç‡§ï ‡§∞‡§π‡•á ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç‡•§ Trust finished.)*


* ‚úÖ **The Clean Miss:**
* (Smile & Eye Contact)
* "Sorry Sir, I do not recall the exact data for Purnia district at this moment. I will read up on it."
* *(Effect: Honest. Precise. Confident.)*



#### **Scenario 2: The "Technical" Question (Out of Syllabus)**

**Question:** *(To a History Student)* *"How does Quantum Computing affect Encryption?"*

* ‚ùå **The Bluffer:** "Sir, Quantum is very fast computer... it encrypts better..." (Vague nonsense).
* ‚úÖ **The Clean Miss:**
* "Sir, since my background is in Humanities, I have limited technical understanding of Quantum Computing's impact on encryption. I apologize."
* *(Effect: You know your boundaries. Self-aware.)*



#### **Scenario 3: The "Quote" Question**

**Question:** *"Who said: 'Swaraj is my birthright'?"* (Suppose you genuinely forgot/blanked out).

* ‚ùå **The Panic:** (Looking at ceiling) "Umm... Gandhi ji? No... Nehru ji... umm..."
* ‚úÖ **The Clean Miss:**
* "I am sorry Sir. It is a very famous quote by Tilak ji, but my mind just went blank. I apologize for this lapse."
* *(Effect: ‡§à‡§Æ‡§æ‡§®‡§¶‡§æ‡§∞‡•Ä ‡§∏‡•á "Brain Fade" ‡§Æ‡§æ‡§®‡§®‡§æ ‡§ï‡•ã‡§à ‡§ó‡•Å‡§®‡§æ‡§π ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç ‡§π‡•à‡•§ ‡§π‡§Æ ‡§∏‡§¨ ‡§á‡§Ç‡§∏‡§æ‡§® ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç‡•§)*



#### **Scenario 4: The "Trap" Question (Fake Fact)**

**Question:** *"Why is the 'Red River' of Bihar called the sorrow of Bengal?"* (Trick: There is no Red River, and sorrow of Bengal is Damodar, not in Bihar).

* ‚ùå **The Bluffer:** "Sir... because it floods a lot... and soil is red..." (Caught!).
* ‚úÖ **The Intelligent Miss:**
* "Sir, I am aware that Kosi is called the Sorrow of Bihar and Damodar was the Sorrow of Bengal. I am not able to recall any river named 'Red River' in this context. Could you please correct me?"
* *(Effect: ‡§Ü‡§™‡§®‡•á ‡§µ‡§ø‡§®‡§Æ‡•ç‡§∞‡§§‡§æ ‡§∏‡•á Board ‡§ï‡•ã correct ‡§ï‡§∞ ‡§¶‡§ø‡§Ø‡§æ‡•§ Big marks for confidence.)*



#### **Scenario 5: The "Consecutive" Miss (Back to Back No)**

**Question:** *(Board asks 3 tough questions in a row, and you know NONE of them).*

* ‚ùå **The Meltdown:** (Sweating, losing confidence, voice shaking) "Sorry sir... sorry sir..."
* ‚úÖ **The Clean Miss:**
* **Q1:** "Sorry Sir, I don't know."
* **Q2:** "I am unaware of this too, Sir."
* **Q3:** "Sir, I seem to be reading less on this specific topic. I will definitely brush up my knowledge."
* *(Effect: ‡§ö‡•á‡§π‡§∞‡•á ‡§™‡§∞ ‡§∂‡§ø‡§ï‡§® ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç‡•§ ‡§Ü‡§™‡§®‡•á 3 ‡§¨‡§æ‡§â‡§Ç‡§∏‡§∞ ‡§õ‡•ã‡§°‡§º‡•Ä‡§Ç, ‡§Ö‡§¨ ‡§ö‡•å‡§•‡•Ä ‡§¨‡•â‡§≤ ‡§ï‡§æ ‡§á‡§Ç‡§§‡§ú‡§º‡§æ‡§∞ ‡§ï‡§∞ ‡§∞‡§π‡•á ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç‡•§ You are unbreakable.)*



---

### **3. Potential Board Questions (Stress Testing)**

Board ‡§ú‡§æ‡§®‡§¨‡•Ç‡§ù‡§ï‡§∞ ‡§ê‡§∏‡•á ‡§∏‡§µ‡§æ‡§≤ ‡§™‡•Ç‡§õ‡•á‡§ó‡§æ ‡§ú‡•ã ‡§Ü‡§™‡§ï‡•ã ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç ‡§Ü‡§§‡•á ‡§π‡•ã‡§Ç‡§ó‡•á‡•§

**Type A: Obscure Trivia**

1. *"‡§Ü‡§™‡§ï‡•á ‡§ú‡§ø‡§≤‡•á ‡§ï‡•á ‡§§‡•Ä‡§∏‡§∞‡•á DM ‡§ï‡§æ ‡§®‡§æ‡§Æ ‡§ï‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ ‡§•‡§æ?"*
* *(Impossible to know. Just say No.)*



**Type B: Deep Technicals**
2.  *"‡§Ü‡§™‡§®‡•á Sociology ‡§™‡§¢‡§º‡§æ ‡§π‡•à, ‡§¨‡§§‡§æ‡§á‡§è 'Parson's Pattern Variables' ‡§ï‡§æ ‡§ö‡•å‡§•‡§æ variable ‡§ï‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ ‡§π‡•à?"*
* *(‡§Ö‡§ó‡§∞ ‡§Ø‡§æ‡§¶ ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç, ‡§§‡•ã guess ‡§Æ‡§§ ‡§ï‡§∞‡•á‡§Ç‡•§ Academic questions ‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç guess ‡§ï‡§∞‡§®‡§æ ‡§ñ‡§§‡§∞‡§®‡§æ‡§ï ‡§π‡•à‡•§)*

**Type C: "Are you sure?" Trap**
3.  *(After you give a correct answer)* **Board:** *"Are you sure? Think again. I think you are wrong."*
* **Response:** ‡§Ö‡§ó‡§∞ ‡§Ü‡§™ 100% sure ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç, ‡§§‡•ã stick ‡§ï‡§∞‡•á‡§Ç: *"Sir, to the best of my knowledge, this is correct."*
* ‡§Ö‡§ó‡§∞ ‡§•‡•ã‡§°‡§º‡§æ ‡§≠‡•Ä doubt ‡§π‡•à, ‡§§‡•ã ‡§ï‡§π‡•á‡§Ç: *"Sir, I might be mistaken, I will re-verify it."* (Rigid ‡§® ‡§¨‡§®‡•á‡§Ç‡•§)

---

### **4. How to Prepare (The Perfect Way: The "No" Drill)**

"‡§®‡§æ" ‡§¨‡•ã‡§≤‡§®‡§æ ‡§Ü‡§∏‡§æ‡§® ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç ‡§π‡•à, ‡§á‡§∏‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç Ego hurt ‡§π‡•ã‡§§‡§æ ‡§π‡•à‡•§ ‡§á‡§∏‡§ï‡•Ä practice ‡§ï‡§∞‡•á‡§Ç‡•§

#### **Drill 1: The "Poker Face No"**

* **Task:** ‡§∂‡•Ä‡§∂‡•á ‡§ï‡•á ‡§∏‡§æ‡§Æ‡§®‡•á ‡§ñ‡§°‡§º‡•á ‡§π‡•ã‡§Ç‡•§
* **Action:** ‡§ú‡•ã‡§∞ ‡§∏‡•á ‡§¨‡•ã‡§≤‡•á‡§Ç: *"Sorry Sir, I don't know."*
* **Check:**
* ‡§ï‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ ‡§Ü‡§™ ‡§Æ‡•Å‡§∏‡•ç‡§ï‡•Å‡§∞‡§æ ‡§∞‡§π‡•á ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç? (Good)
* ‡§ï‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ ‡§Ü‡§™‡§ï‡•Ä ‡§®‡§ú‡§∞‡•á‡§Ç ‡§ù‡•Å‡§ï ‡§ó‡§à‡§Ç? (Bad)
* ‡§ï‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ ‡§Ü‡§™‡§ï‡•Ä ‡§Ü‡§µ‡§æ‡§ú ‡§ß‡•Ä‡§Æ‡•Ä ‡§π‡•ã ‡§ó‡§à? (Bad)


* **Goal:** "No" ‡§¨‡•ã‡§≤‡§§‡•á ‡§µ‡§ï‡•ç‡§§ ‡§Ü‡§™‡§ï‡•Ä Body Language ‡§µ‡•à‡§∏‡•Ä ‡§π‡•Ä ‡§π‡•ã‡§®‡•Ä ‡§ö‡§æ‡§π‡§ø‡§è ‡§ú‡•à‡§∏‡•Ä "Yes" ‡§¨‡•ã‡§≤‡§§‡•á ‡§µ‡§ï‡•ç‡§§ ‡§π‡•ã‡§§‡•Ä ‡§π‡•à‡•§

#### **Drill 2: The "Permission" Practice**

* **Task:** ‡§ï‡•ã‡§à ‡§ê‡§∏‡§æ topic ‡§≤‡•á‡§Ç ‡§ú‡§ø‡§∏ ‡§™‡§∞ ‡§Ü‡§™ sure ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç‡•§
* **Action:** ‡§Ø‡§π phrase ‡§¨‡•ã‡§≤‡§®‡•á ‡§ï‡•Ä practice ‡§ï‡§∞‡•á‡§Ç:
* *"Sir, exact data yaad nahi hai, par anuman (guess) ke mutabik..."*
* *"Sir, if you allow me to apply logic here..."*



---

### **5. Neuro-Interrogation (Self-Reflection)**

1. **Ego Check:** *"‡§ï‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ ‡§Æ‡•Å‡§ù‡•á ‡§≤‡§ó‡§§‡§æ ‡§π‡•à ‡§ï‡§ø '‡§®‡§æ' ‡§¨‡•ã‡§≤‡§®‡•á ‡§∏‡•á ‡§Æ‡•à‡§Ç ‡§¨‡•á‡§µ‡§ï‡•Ç‡§´ ‡§≤‡§ó‡•Ç‡§Ç‡§ó‡§æ?"*
* (‡§Ø‡§æ‡§¶ ‡§∞‡§ñ‡•á‡§Ç: Google ‡§ï‡•á CEO ‡§ï‡•ã ‡§≠‡•Ä ‡§∏‡§¨ ‡§ï‡•Å‡§õ ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç ‡§™‡§§‡§æ ‡§π‡•ã‡§§‡§æ‡•§ Officer ‡§ï‡•ã '‡§∏‡§¨ ‡§ï‡•Å‡§õ' ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç, '‡§∏‡§π‡•Ä ‡§ö‡•Ä‡§ú‡§º‡•á‡§Ç' ‡§™‡§§‡§æ ‡§π‡•ã‡§®‡•Ä ‡§ö‡§æ‡§π‡§ø‡§è‡•§)


2. **Panic Check:** *"‡§Ö‡§ó‡§∞ ‡§Æ‡•à‡§Ç ‡§≤‡§ó‡§æ‡§§‡§æ‡§∞ 4 ‡§∏‡§µ‡§æ‡§≤‡•ã‡§Ç ‡§ï‡•á ‡§ú‡§µ‡§æ‡§¨ ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç ‡§¶‡•á ‡§™‡§æ‡§Ø‡§æ, ‡§§‡•ã ‡§ï‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ ‡§Æ‡•à‡§Ç 5‡§µ‡•á‡§Ç ‡§∏‡§µ‡§æ‡§≤ ‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç nervous ‡§π‡•ã ‡§ú‡§æ‡§ä‡§Ç‡§ó‡§æ?"*
* (‡§π‡§∞ ‡§∏‡§µ‡§æ‡§≤ ‡§è‡§ï ‡§®‡§Ø‡§æ ‡§Æ‡•à‡§ö ‡§π‡•à‡•§ ‡§™‡§ø‡§õ‡§≤‡•á ‡§∏‡§µ‡§æ‡§≤ ‡§ï‡§æ failure ‡§Ö‡§ó‡§≤‡•á ‡§∏‡§µ‡§æ‡§≤ ‡§™‡§∞ ‡§π‡§æ‡§µ‡•Ä ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç ‡§π‡•ã‡§®‡§æ ‡§ö‡§æ‡§π‡§ø‡§è‡•§)



---

### **6. Overall Effect on Interview**

‡§ú‡§¨ ‡§Ü‡§™ "Clean Miss" Protocol ‡§Ö‡§™‡§®‡§æ‡§§‡•á ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç:

1. **Integrity:** Board ‡§ï‡•ã ‡§≠‡§∞‡•ã‡§∏‡§æ ‡§π‡•ã ‡§ú‡§æ‡§§‡§æ ‡§π‡•à ‡§ï‡§ø ‡§Ø‡§π ‡§µ‡•ç‡§Ø‡§ï‡•ç‡§§‡§ø ‡§ï‡§≠‡•Ä ‡§ù‡•Ç‡§† ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç ‡§¨‡•ã‡§≤‡•á‡§ó‡§æ‡•§ ‡§™‡•ç‡§∞‡§∂‡§æ‡§∏‡§® ‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç ‡§Ø‡§π ‡§∏‡§¨‡§∏‡•á ‡§¨‡§°‡§º‡§æ ‡§ó‡•Å‡§£ ‡§π‡•à‡•§
2. **Time Saving:** ‡§Ü‡§™ Board ‡§ï‡§æ time waste ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç ‡§ï‡§∞‡§§‡•á‡•§ ‡§µ‡•ã ‡§ñ‡•Å‡§∂ ‡§π‡•ã‡§§‡•á ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç ‡§ï‡§ø *"‡§ö‡§≤‡•ã, ‡§Ö‡§¨ ‡§Ö‡§ó‡§≤‡§æ ‡§∏‡§µ‡§æ‡§≤ ‡§™‡•Ç‡§õ ‡§∏‡§ï‡§§‡•á ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç‡•§"*
3. **Accuracy:** ‡§ú‡§¨ ‡§Ü‡§™ ‡§Ö‡§ó‡§≤‡•á ‡§∏‡§µ‡§æ‡§≤ ‡§ï‡§æ ‡§ú‡§µ‡§æ‡§¨ ‡§¶‡•á‡§§‡•á ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç, ‡§§‡•ã Board ‡§â‡§∏‡•á ‡§ó‡§Ç‡§≠‡•Ä‡§∞‡§§‡§æ ‡§∏‡•á ‡§∏‡•Å‡§®‡§§‡§æ ‡§π‡•à ‡§ï‡•ç‡§Ø‡•ã‡§Ç‡§ï‡§ø ‡§â‡§®‡•ç‡§π‡•á‡§Ç ‡§™‡§§‡§æ ‡§π‡•à ‡§ï‡§ø *"‡§Ö‡§ó‡§∞ ‡§Ø‡§π ‡§¨‡•ã‡§≤ ‡§∞‡§π‡§æ ‡§π‡•à, ‡§§‡•ã ‡§á‡§∏‡•á ‡§™‡§§‡§æ ‡§π‡•ã‡§ó‡§æ‡•§"*

---

### **Today's Action Plan (‡§Ü‡§ú ‡§ï‡§æ ‡§π‡•ã‡§Æ‡§µ‡§∞‡•ç‡§ï)**

1. **Draft:** 3 ‡§Ö‡§≤‡§ó-‡§Ö‡§≤‡§ó ‡§§‡§∞‡•Ä‡§ï‡•á (Phrases) ‡§≤‡§ø‡§ñ‡•á‡§Ç "I don't know" ‡§¨‡•ã‡§≤‡§®‡•á ‡§ï‡•á‡•§ (Direct, Polite, Curious).
2. **Record:** ‡§Ö‡§™‡§®‡•á ‡§¶‡•ã‡§∏‡•ç‡§§ ‡§∏‡•á ‡§ï‡§π‡•á‡§Ç ‡§ï‡§ø ‡§µ‡•ã ‡§Ü‡§™‡§∏‡•á Physics ‡§Ø‡§æ Medicine ‡§ï‡•á ‡§ï‡§†‡§ø‡§® ‡§∏‡§µ‡§æ‡§≤ ‡§™‡•Ç‡§õ‡•á (‡§ú‡•ã ‡§Ü‡§™‡§ï‡§æ subject ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç ‡§π‡•à)‡•§
* ‡§π‡§∞ ‡§∏‡§µ‡§æ‡§≤ ‡§™‡§∞ ‡§¨‡§ø‡§®‡§æ ‡§π‡§ø‡§ö‡§ï‡§ø‡§ö‡§æ‡§è, ‡§Æ‡•Å‡§∏‡•ç‡§ï‡•Å‡§∞‡§æ‡§§‡•á ‡§π‡•Å‡§è "Sorry" ‡§¨‡•ã‡§≤‡•á‡§Ç‡•§


3. **Visualize:** ‡§Ü‡§Ç‡§ñ‡•á‡§Ç ‡§¨‡§Ç‡§¶ ‡§ï‡§∞‡•á‡§Ç ‡§î‡§∞ imagine ‡§ï‡§∞‡•á‡§Ç ‡§ï‡§ø Board ‡§®‡•á ‡§Ü‡§™‡§ï‡•ã ‡§´‡§Ç‡§∏‡§æ ‡§¶‡§ø‡§Ø‡§æ ‡§π‡•à‡•§ ‡§ó‡§π‡§∞‡•Ä ‡§∏‡§æ‡§Ç‡§∏ ‡§≤‡•á‡§Ç ‡§î‡§∞ imagine ‡§ï‡§∞‡•á‡§Ç ‡§ï‡§ø ‡§Ü‡§™ calm ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç‡•§

**Chapter Mantra:**

> *"‡§ó‡§≤‡§§ ‡§ú‡§µ‡§æ‡§¨ ‡§¶‡•á‡§®‡•á ‡§∏‡•á '‡§Æ‡•Ç‡§∞‡•ç‡§ñ' (Fool) ‡§∏‡§æ‡§¨‡§ø‡§§ ‡§π‡•ã‡§®‡•á ‡§∏‡•á ‡§¨‡•á‡§π‡§§‡§∞ ‡§π‡•à ‡§ï‡§ø '‡§®‡§æ' ‡§¨‡•ã‡§≤‡§ï‡§∞ '‡§à‡§Æ‡§æ‡§®‡§¶‡§æ‡§∞' (Honest) ‡§∏‡§æ‡§¨‡§ø‡§§ ‡§π‡•ã ‡§ú‡§æ‡§ì‡•§"*

---

**Next:** **Chapter 13 (Handling Stress, Silence & Provocation)** ‚Äî ‡§ú‡§¨ Board ‡§ö‡•Å‡§™ ‡§π‡•ã ‡§ú‡§æ‡§è ‡§î‡§∞ ‡§Ü‡§™‡§ï‡•ã ‡§ò‡•Ç‡§∞‡§§‡§æ ‡§∞‡§π‡•á, ‡§Ø‡§æ ‡§Ü‡§™‡§ï‡•Ä ‡§¨‡•á‡§á‡§ú‡•ç‡§ú‡§§‡•Ä (Insult) ‡§ï‡§∞‡§®‡•á ‡§ï‡•Ä ‡§ï‡•ã‡§∂‡§ø‡§∂ ‡§ï‡§∞‡•á, ‡§§‡•ã "Poker Face" ‡§ï‡•à‡§∏‡•á ‡§∞‡§ñ‡§®‡§æ ‡§π‡•à‡•§





---



## Chapter 13: Handling Stress, Silence & Provocation (‡§§‡§®‡§æ‡§µ ‡§î‡§∞ ‡§â‡§ï‡§∏‡§æ‡§µ‡•á ‡§ï‡§æ ‡§∏‡§æ‡§Æ‡§®‡§æ)
This chapter prepares you for the "Psychological Warfare" inside the interview room. This is where they stop testing your knowledge and start testing your **Nerves**.

**Core Focus:** Emotional Regulation (‡§≠‡§æ‡§µ‡§®‡§æ‡§ì‡§Ç ‡§™‡§∞ ‡§ï‡§æ‡§¨‡•Ç).
**The Weapon:** **The "Poker Face" & "Follow-Up Anticipation."**

---

### **Namaskar Future Officer.**

Interview Board ‡§ï‡§≠‡•Ä-‡§ï‡§≠‡•Ä "Good Cop, Bad Cop" ‡§ï‡§æ ‡§ñ‡•á‡§≤ ‡§ñ‡•á‡§≤‡§§‡§æ ‡§π‡•à‡•§
‡§è‡§ï ‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç‡§¨‡§∞ ‡§™‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ‡§∞ ‡§∏‡•á ‡§¨‡§æ‡§§ ‡§ï‡§∞‡•á‡§ó‡§æ, ‡§î‡§∞ ‡§¶‡•Ç‡§∏‡§∞‡§æ ‡§Ö‡§ö‡§æ‡§®‡§ï ‡§Ü‡§™ ‡§™‡§∞ ‡§ö‡§ø‡§≤‡•ç‡§≤‡§æ ‡§∏‡§ï‡§§‡§æ ‡§π‡•à ‡§Ø‡§æ ‡§Ü‡§™‡§ï‡•Ä ‡§¨‡•á‡§á‡§ú‡•ç‡§ú‡§§‡•Ä (Insult) ‡§ï‡§∞ ‡§∏‡§ï‡§§‡§æ ‡§π‡•à‡•§

‡§µ‡•ã ‡§ï‡§π‡•á‡§Ç‡§ó‡•á:

* *"‡§Ö‡§∞‡•á, ‡§Ü‡§™‡§ï‡•ã ‡§á‡§§‡§®‡§æ ‡§≠‡•Ä ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç ‡§™‡§§‡§æ? ‡§Ü‡§™‡§®‡•á Mains ‡§ï‡•à‡§∏‡•á ‡§™‡§æ‡§∏ ‡§ï‡§ø‡§Ø‡§æ?"*
* *"‡§¨‡§ø‡§π‡§æ‡§∞ ‡§§‡•ã ‡§¨‡§∞‡•ç‡§¨‡§æ‡§¶ ‡§∞‡§æ‡§ú‡•ç‡§Ø ‡§π‡•à, ‡§Ü‡§™ ‡§á‡§∏‡•á ‡§ï‡§≠‡•Ä ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç ‡§∏‡•Å‡§ß‡§æ‡§∞ ‡§∏‡§ï‡§§‡•á‡•§"*

‡§Ø‡§æ ‡§´‡§ø‡§∞... ‡§µ‡•ã ‡§è‡§ï ‡§∏‡§µ‡§æ‡§≤ ‡§™‡•Ç‡§õ‡§ï‡§∞ **‡§¨‡§ø‡§≤‡•ç‡§ï‡•Å‡§≤ ‡§ö‡•Å‡§™ (Silent)** ‡§π‡•ã ‡§ú‡§æ‡§è‡§Ç‡§ó‡•á ‡§î‡§∞ ‡§¨‡§∏ ‡§Ü‡§™‡§ï‡•ã ‡§ò‡•Ç‡§∞‡§§‡•á ‡§∞‡§π‡•á‡§Ç‡§ó‡•á‡•§

90% students ‡§Ø‡§π‡§æ‡§Å ‡§ü‡•Ç‡§ü ‡§ú‡§æ‡§§‡•á ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç‡•§ ‡§µ‡•ã ‡§Ø‡§æ ‡§§‡•ã:

1. **Defensive** ‡§π‡•ã ‡§ú‡§æ‡§§‡•á ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç (‡§∞‡•ã‡§®‡•á ‡§ú‡•à‡§∏‡§æ ‡§ö‡•á‡§π‡§∞‡§æ)‡•§
2. **Aggressive** ‡§π‡•ã ‡§ú‡§æ‡§§‡•á ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç (‡§¨‡§π‡§∏ ‡§ï‡§∞‡§®‡•á ‡§≤‡§ó‡§§‡•á ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç)‡•§
3. **Blabbering** ‡§ï‡§∞‡§®‡•á ‡§≤‡§ó‡§§‡•á ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç (‡§ö‡•Å‡§™ ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç ‡§∞‡§π ‡§™‡§æ‡§§‡•á, ‡§´‡§æ‡§≤‡§§‡•Ç ‡§¨‡•ã‡§≤‡§®‡•á ‡§≤‡§ó‡§§‡•á ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç)‡•§

‡§Ø‡§æ‡§¶ ‡§∞‡§ñ‡§ø‡§è: **‡§Ø‡§π "Personal" ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç ‡§π‡•à‡•§ ‡§Ø‡§π ‡§è‡§ï "Simulation" ‡§π‡•à‡•§**
‡§µ‡•ã ‡§¶‡•á‡§ñ‡§®‡§æ ‡§ö‡§æ‡§π‡§§‡•á ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç ‡§ï‡§ø ‡§ï‡§≤ ‡§ï‡•ã ‡§Ö‡§ó‡§∞ ‡§Ü‡§™‡§ï‡•á ‡§ú‡§ø‡§≤‡•á ‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç ‡§¶‡§Ç‡§ó‡§æ (Riot) ‡§π‡•ã ‡§ú‡§æ‡§è ‡§î‡§∞ ‡§≠‡•Ä‡§°‡§º ‡§Ü‡§™‡§ï‡•ã ‡§ó‡§æ‡§≤‡§ø‡§Ø‡§æ‡§Ç ‡§¶‡•á ‡§∞‡§π‡•Ä ‡§π‡•ã, ‡§§‡•ã ‡§ï‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ ‡§Ü‡§™ ‡§µ‡§π‡§æ‡§Ç ‡§≠‡•Ä ‡§∞‡•ã‡§®‡•á ‡§≤‡§ó‡•á‡§Ç‡§ó‡•á?

‡§è‡§ï **Officer** ‡§ï‡§æ ‡§∏‡§¨‡§∏‡•á ‡§¨‡§°‡§º‡§æ ‡§π‡§•‡§ø‡§Ø‡§æ‡§∞ ‡§â‡§∏‡§ï‡•Ä "‡§†‡§Ç‡§°‡•Ä ‡§ñ‡•ã‡§™‡§°‡§º‡•Ä" (Cool Head) ‡§π‡•ã‡§§‡•Ä ‡§π‡•à‡•§

---

### **1. The Core Mechanics: The 3 Traps**

#### **Trap 1: The "Awkward Silence" (‡§ñ‡§æ‡§Æ‡•ã‡§∂‡•Ä ‡§ï‡§æ ‡§ú‡§æ‡§≤)**

* **The Situation:** ‡§Ü‡§™‡§®‡•á ‡§ú‡§µ‡§æ‡§¨ ‡§ñ‡§§‡•ç‡§Æ ‡§ï‡§ø‡§Ø‡§æ, ‡§≤‡•á‡§ï‡§ø‡§® Board Member ‡§ï‡•Å‡§õ ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç ‡§¨‡•ã‡§≤‡•á‡•§ ‡§µ‡•ã ‡§¨‡§∏ ‡§Ü‡§™‡§ï‡•ã ‡§¶‡•á‡§ñ ‡§∞‡§π‡•á ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç‡•§
* **Student Reaction:** ‡§ò‡§¨‡§∞‡§æ‡§π‡§ü ‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç ‡§î‡§∞ ‡§¨‡•ã‡§≤‡§®‡•á ‡§≤‡§ó‡§§‡§æ ‡§π‡•à‡•§ *"Sir, aur bhi points hain..."* (‡§î‡§∞ ‡§Ø‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç ‡§µ‡•ã ‡§ó‡§≤‡§§‡•Ä ‡§ï‡§∞‡§§‡§æ ‡§π‡•à)‡•§
* **Officer Reaction:** ‡§Ü‡§™ ‡§ú‡§µ‡§æ‡§¨ ‡§ñ‡§§‡•ç‡§Æ ‡§ï‡§∞‡•á‡§Ç‡•§ ‡§è‡§ï "Full Stop" ‡§µ‡§æ‡§≤‡•Ä ‡§Æ‡•Å‡§∏‡•ç‡§ï‡§æ‡§® ‡§¶‡•á‡§Ç‡•§ ‡§î‡§∞ ‡§ö‡•Å‡§™‡§ö‡§æ‡§™ ‡§¨‡•à‡§†‡•á‡§Ç‡•§
* *Message:* "‡§Æ‡•à‡§Ç ‡§Ö‡§™‡§®‡•á ‡§ú‡§µ‡§æ‡§¨ ‡§∏‡•á ‡§∏‡§Ç‡§§‡•Å‡§∑‡•ç‡§ü ‡§π‡•Ç‡§Å‡•§ ‡§Ö‡§¨ ‡§Ü‡§™‡§ï‡•Ä ‡§¨‡§æ‡§∞‡•Ä ‡§π‡•à‡•§" (Confidence).



#### **Trap 2: The "Provocation" (‡§â‡§ï‡§∏‡§æ‡§µ‡§æ)**

* **The Situation:** *"‡§Ü‡§™‡§ï‡§æ ‡§ú‡§µ‡§æ‡§¨ ‡§è‡§ï‡§¶‡§Æ ‡§¨‡§ï‡§µ‡§æ‡§∏ ‡§π‡•à‡•§"* ‡§Ø‡§æ *"‡§Ü‡§™ Officer ‡§¨‡§®‡§®‡•á ‡§≤‡§æ‡§Ø‡§ï ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç ‡§≤‡§ó‡§§‡•á‡•§"*
* **Officer Reaction:** **Emotional Decoupling.** (‡§Ö‡§™‡§®‡•á Ego ‡§ï‡•ã ‡§ï‡§Æ‡§∞‡•á ‡§ï‡•á ‡§¨‡§æ‡§π‡§∞ ‡§õ‡•ã‡§°‡§º ‡§¶‡•á‡§Ç)‡•§
* ‡§Æ‡•Å‡§∏‡•ç‡§ï‡•Å‡§∞‡§æ‡§è‡§Ç ‡§î‡§∞ ‡§ï‡§π‡•á‡§Ç: *"Sir, I respect your opinion, but my perspective is based on..."*



#### **Trap 3: The "Rapid Fire" (‡§¨‡•å‡§õ‡§æ‡§∞)**

* **The Situation:** ‡§Ü‡§™ ‡§è‡§ï ‡§ú‡§µ‡§æ‡§¨ ‡§™‡•Ç‡§∞‡§æ ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç ‡§ï‡§∞ ‡§™‡§æ‡§§‡•á, ‡§µ‡•ã ‡§¶‡•Ç‡§∏‡§∞‡§æ ‡§¶‡§æ‡§ó ‡§¶‡•á‡§§‡•á ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç‡•§
* **Officer Reaction:** ‡§Ö‡§™‡§®‡•Ä speed ‡§Æ‡§§ ‡§¨‡§¢‡§º‡§æ‡§á‡§è‡•§ ‡§Ö‡§™‡§®‡•Ä pace maintain ‡§ï‡§∞‡•á‡§Ç‡•§ ‡§Ö‡§ó‡§∞ ‡§µ‡•ã ‡§¨‡•Ä‡§ö ‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç ‡§ï‡§æ‡§ü‡•á‡§Ç, ‡§§‡•ã ‡§∞‡•Å‡§ï ‡§ú‡§æ‡§è‡§Ç‡•§

---

### **2. New Addition: "Follow-Up Anticipation"**

Board ‡§ï‡•á ‡§π‡§Æ‡§≤‡•á ‡§ï‡•ã ‡§∞‡•ã‡§ï‡§®‡•á ‡§ï‡§æ ‡§∏‡§¨‡§∏‡•á ‡§Ö‡§ö‡•ç‡§õ‡§æ ‡§§‡§∞‡•Ä‡§ï‡§æ ‡§π‡•à‚Äî **‡§π‡§Æ‡§≤‡•á ‡§ï‡•ã ‡§™‡§π‡§≤‡•á ‡§∏‡•á ‡§≠‡§æ‡§Ç‡§™ ‡§≤‡•á‡§®‡§æ (Predicting the Attack).**

‡§ú‡§¨ ‡§Ü‡§™ ‡§ï‡•ã‡§à ‡§∂‡§¨‡•ç‡§¶ ‡§¨‡•ã‡§≤‡§§‡•á ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç, ‡§§‡•ã ‡§Ü‡§™ Board ‡§ï‡•ã ‡§Ö‡§ó‡§≤‡§æ ‡§∏‡§µ‡§æ‡§≤ "‡§™‡§∞‡•ã‡§∏" ‡§∞‡§π‡•á ‡§π‡•ã‡§§‡•á ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç‡•§

* ‡§Ö‡§ó‡§∞ ‡§Ü‡§™‡§®‡•á ‡§¨‡•ã‡§≤‡§æ **"MSP"**, ‡§§‡•ã ‡§§‡•à‡§Ø‡§æ‡§∞ ‡§∞‡§π‡•á‡§Ç ‡§Ö‡§ó‡§≤‡§æ ‡§∏‡§µ‡§æ‡§≤ **"Fiscal Deficit"** ‡§™‡§∞ ‡§π‡•ã‡§ó‡§æ‡•§
* ‡§Ö‡§ó‡§∞ ‡§Ü‡§™‡§®‡•á ‡§¨‡•ã‡§≤‡§æ **"Reservation"**, ‡§§‡•ã ‡§§‡•à‡§Ø‡§æ‡§∞ ‡§∞‡§π‡•á‡§Ç ‡§Ö‡§ó‡§≤‡§æ ‡§∏‡§µ‡§æ‡§≤ **"Merit"** ‡§™‡§∞ ‡§π‡•ã‡§ó‡§æ‡•§

**The Strategy:** ‡§ú‡§µ‡§æ‡§¨ ‡§¶‡•á‡§§‡•á ‡§µ‡§ï‡•ç‡§§ ‡§π‡•Ä ‡§∏‡•ã‡§ö ‡§≤‡•á‡§Ç ‡§ï‡§ø *"‡§á‡§∏ ‡§ú‡§µ‡§æ‡§¨ ‡§™‡§∞ ‡§µ‡•ã ‡§Æ‡•Å‡§ù‡•á ‡§ï‡§π‡§æ‡§Ç ‡§´‡§Ç‡§∏‡§æ ‡§∏‡§ï‡§§‡•á ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç?"*

---

### **3. The 5 Examples: Handling the Heat**

‡§®‡•Ä‡§ö‡•á 5 "Stress Scenarios" ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç‡•§ ‡§¶‡•á‡§ñ‡§ø‡§è ‡§ï‡•à‡§∏‡•á ‡§è‡§ï ‡§∏‡§æ‡§ß‡§æ‡§∞‡§£ ‡§ï‡•à‡§Ç‡§°‡§ø‡§°‡•á‡§ü "Melt" ‡§π‡•ã ‡§ú‡§æ‡§§‡§æ ‡§π‡•à ‡§î‡§∞ ‡§è‡§ï Officer "Solid" ‡§∞‡§π‡§§‡§æ ‡§π‡•à‡•§

#### **Scenario 1: The "Insult" Trap**

**Board Member (Aggressively):** *"Mr. [Name], ‡§Ü‡§™‡§®‡•á ‡§á‡§Ç‡§ú‡•Ä‡§®‡§ø‡§Ø‡§∞‡§ø‡§Ç‡§ó ‡§ï‡•Ä ‡§π‡•à ‡§î‡§∞ ‡§Ö‡§¨ ‡§π‡§ø‡§∏‡•ç‡§ü‡•ç‡§∞‡•Ä ‡§≤‡•á ‡§∞‡§π‡•á ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç‡•§ ‡§Ü‡§™ ‡§ú‡•à‡§∏‡•á ‡§≤‡•ã‡§ó ‡§∏‡§ø‡§∞‡•ç‡§´ 'Job Hopper' ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç‡•§ ‡§Ü‡§™ ‡§¶‡•á‡§∂ ‡§ï‡•á ‡§∏‡§Ç‡§∏‡§æ‡§ß‡§® (Resources) ‡§¨‡§∞‡•ç‡§¨‡§æ‡§¶ ‡§ï‡§∞ ‡§∞‡§π‡•á ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç‡•§"*

* ‚ùå **Defensive Answer:** "‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç ‡§∏‡§∞, ‡§ê‡§∏‡§æ ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç ‡§π‡•à... ‡§µ‡•ã ‡§¶‡§∞‡§Ö‡§∏‡§≤..." (‡§ò‡§¨‡§∞‡§æ ‡§ó‡§è)‡•§
* ‚úÖ **The Poker Face Answer:**
* (Maintain Smile. Do not look down.)
* "Sir, I understand your concern regarding resource utilization.
* However, education is never wasted. My engineering skills (Logic/Tech) combined with History (Perspective) make me a more multidimensional administrator.
* It is not 'hopping', it is 'evolving' towards a role where I can contribute best."
* *(Effect: ‡§Ü‡§™‡§®‡•á ‡§Ö‡§™‡§®‡•Ä ‡§¨‡•á‡§á‡§ú‡•ç‡§ú‡§§‡•Ä ‡§ï‡•ã "Evolution" ‡§ï‡§æ ‡§®‡§æ‡§Æ ‡§¶‡•á‡§ï‡§∞ ‡§∏‡§Æ‡•ç‡§Æ‡§æ‡§® ‡§∏‡•á ‡§ú‡§µ‡§æ‡§¨ ‡§¶‡§ø‡§Ø‡§æ‡•§)*



#### **Scenario 2: The "Silent Stare" Trap**

**You:** "...and that is why Women Reservation is necessary." (Answer finished).
**Board:** (Pin drop silence for 10 seconds. Just staring at you).

* ‚ùå **Panic Answer:** "Umm... Sir, aur bhi reasons hain... jaise ki... umm... Bihar mein bhi..." (Blabbering).
* ‚úÖ **The Officer Action:**
* (Sit comfortably. Keep hands in Steeple position. Maintain eye contact and smile gently.)
* (After 5-6 seconds, if they still don't speak): *"Sir, is there any specific aspect of this topic you would like me to elaborate on?"*
* *(Effect: ‡§Ü‡§™‡§®‡•á ‡§ö‡•Å‡§™‡•ç‡§™‡•Ä ‡§§‡•ã‡§°‡§º‡•Ä ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç, ‡§â‡§∏‡•á 'Manage' ‡§ï‡§ø‡§Ø‡§æ‡•§)*



#### **Scenario 3: The "Contradiction" Trap**

**Board:** *"‡§Ö‡§≠‡•Ä ‡§Ü‡§™‡§®‡•á ‡§ï‡§π‡§æ ‡§ï‡§ø ‡§∂‡§∞‡§æ‡§¨‡§¨‡§Ç‡§¶‡•Ä (Liquor Ban) ‡§Ö‡§ö‡•ç‡§õ‡•Ä ‡§π‡•à, ‡§î‡§∞ ‡§Ö‡§¨ ‡§ï‡§π ‡§∞‡§π‡•á ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç ‡§ï‡§ø Revenue loss ‡§π‡•ã ‡§∞‡§π‡§æ ‡§π‡•à‡•§ ‡§Ü‡§™ ‡§§‡•ã Confused ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç!"*

* ‚ùå **Scared Answer:** "Sorry Sir, wo galti ho gayi..."
* ‚úÖ **The Balanced Answer:**
* "Sir, there is no contradiction.
* Socially (‡§∏‡§æ‡§Æ‡§æ‡§ú‡§ø‡§ï ‡§∞‡•Ç‡§™ ‡§∏‡•á), it is a success (Violence down).
* Economically (‡§Ü‡§∞‡•ç‡§•‡§ø‡§ï ‡§∞‡•Ç‡§™ ‡§∏‡•á), there is a short-term revenue loss.
* An administrator must acknowledge *both* realities to find a holistic solution."
* *(Effect: ‡§Ü‡§™‡§®‡•á ‡§∏‡§æ‡§¨‡§ø‡§§ ‡§ï‡§ø‡§Ø‡§æ ‡§ï‡§ø ‡§Ü‡§™ Confused ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç, ‡§¨‡§≤‡•ç‡§ï‡§ø Comprehensive (‡§µ‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ‡§™‡§ï) ‡§∏‡•ã‡§ö ‡§∞‡§ñ‡§§‡•á ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç‡•§)*



#### **Scenario 4: The "Gaslighting" (You Look Nervous)**

**Board:** *"‡§Ü‡§™ ‡§¨‡§π‡•Å‡§§ ‡§ò‡§¨‡§∞‡§æ‡§è ‡§π‡•Å‡§è ‡§≤‡§ó ‡§∞‡§π‡•á ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç‡•§ ‡§™‡§æ‡§®‡•Ä ‡§™‡§ø‡§è‡§Ç‡§ó‡•á? ‡§Ü‡§™‡§ï‡•á ‡§™‡•à‡§∞ ‡§ï‡§æ‡§Ç‡§™ ‡§∞‡§π‡•á ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç‡•§"* (Even if you are not nervous).

* ‚ùå **Reaction:** (Touching face, checking legs) "Nahi Sir... main theek hoon..." (Now you actually become nervous).
* ‚úÖ **The Officer Action:**
* "Thank you for your concern, Sir. But I am feeling perfectly calm and eager to interact with the board."
* *(Effect: ‡§Ü‡§™‡§®‡•á ‡§â‡§®‡§ï‡•á Frame ‡§ï‡•ã reject ‡§ï‡§∞ ‡§¶‡§ø‡§Ø‡§æ ‡§î‡§∞ ‡§Ö‡§™‡§®‡§æ Frame set ‡§ï‡§ø‡§Ø‡§æ‡•§)*



#### **Scenario 5: The "Political Bait" (Bihar is Worst)**

**Board:** *"Bihar is the burden of India. It drags the national GDP down. Do you agree?"*

* ‚ùå **Emotional Answer:** "‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç ‡§∏‡§∞, ‡§¨‡§ø‡§π‡§æ‡§∞ ‡§Æ‡§π‡§æ‡§® ‡§π‡•à... ‡§π‡§Æ‡§æ‡§∞‡§æ ‡§á‡§§‡§ø‡§π‡§æ‡§∏ ‡§¶‡•á‡§ñ‡§ø‡§è..." (Sentimental).
* ‚úÖ **The Objective Answer:**
* "Sir, while it is true that Bihar's current contribution to GDP is low compared to its population, calling it a 'burden' might be overlooking its potential.
* Bihar provides the 'Human Capital' (Young Workforce) that drives India's industry.
* With recent growth rates being double-digit, Bihar is transitioning from a 'Challenge' to an 'Opportunity'."
* *(Effect: Data ‡§î‡§∞ Logic ‡§ï‡•á ‡§∏‡§æ‡§• ‡§∞‡§æ‡§ú‡•ç‡§Ø ‡§ï‡§æ ‡§¨‡§ö‡§æ‡§µ ‡§ï‡§ø‡§Ø‡§æ, ‡§≠‡§æ‡§µ‡§®‡§æ‡§ì‡§Ç ‡§∏‡•á ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç‡•§)*



---

### **4. Potential Board Questions (Stress Specific)**

‡§Ø‡•á ‡§∏‡§µ‡§æ‡§≤ ‡§Ü‡§™‡§ï‡•ã "Trigger" ‡§ï‡§∞‡§®‡•á ‡§ï‡•á ‡§≤‡§ø‡§è ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç‡•§

**Type A: Testing Patience**

1. *"‡§Æ‡•Å‡§ù‡•á ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç ‡§≤‡§ó‡§§‡§æ ‡§Ü‡§™ SDM ‡§¨‡§®‡§®‡•á ‡§≤‡§æ‡§Ø‡§ï ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç‡•§ ‡§Ü‡§™ ‡§§‡•ã ‡§è‡§ï simple ‡§∏‡§µ‡§æ‡§≤ ‡§ï‡§æ ‡§ú‡§µ‡§æ‡§¨ ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç ‡§¶‡•á ‡§™‡§æ‡§è‡•§ ‡§π‡§Æ ‡§Ü‡§™‡§ï‡•ã ‡§ï‡•ç‡§Ø‡•ã‡§Ç ‡§≤‡•á‡§Ç?"*
* *(Hint: "Sir, one missing fact does not define my capability. My track record shows consistency and learning ability.")*


2. *(Cutting you off repeatedly)* *"Next... Next... Next..."*
* *(Hint: Don't get frustrated. Keep answering with same energy.)*



**Type B: Testing Ego**
3.  *"‡§Ü‡§™‡§ï‡•Ä ‡§â‡§Æ‡•ç‡§∞ (Age) ‡§ú‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ‡§¶‡§æ ‡§π‡•ã ‡§ó‡§à ‡§π‡•à‡•§ ‡§ï‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ ‡§Ü‡§™‡§ï‡•ã ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç ‡§≤‡§ó‡§§‡§æ ‡§Ö‡§¨ ‡§Ü‡§™‡§ï‡•ã ‡§∂‡§æ‡§¶‡•Ä ‡§ï‡§∞ ‡§≤‡•á‡§®‡•Ä ‡§ö‡§æ‡§π‡§ø‡§è ‡§î‡§∞ ‡§∏‡•á‡§ü‡§≤ ‡§π‡•ã ‡§ú‡§æ‡§®‡§æ ‡§ö‡§æ‡§π‡§ø‡§è?"*
* *(Hint: This is personal. Reply professionally about focus on career goals first.)*

**Type C: "I Don't Believe You"**
4.  *"‡§Ü‡§™ ‡§ù‡•Ç‡§† ‡§¨‡•ã‡§≤ ‡§∞‡§π‡•á ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç‡•§ DAF ‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç ‡§Ø‡§π ‡§π‡•â‡§¨‡•Ä ‡§¨‡§∏ ‡§á‡§Ç‡§™‡•ç‡§∞‡•á‡§∏ ‡§ï‡§∞‡§®‡•á ‡§ï‡•á ‡§≤‡§ø‡§è ‡§≤‡§ø‡§ñ‡•Ä ‡§π‡•à ‡§®?"*
* *(Hint: Smile. "No Sir, I genuinely pursue it. Ask me anything about it.")*

---

### **5. How to Prepare (The Perfect Way: Stress Drills)**

‡§†‡§Ç‡§°‡•á ‡§ï‡§Æ‡§∞‡•á ‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç ‡§¨‡•à‡§†‡§ï‡§∞ Stress ‡§ï‡•Ä ‡§™‡•ç‡§∞‡•à‡§ï‡•ç‡§ü‡§ø‡§∏ ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç ‡§π‡•ã ‡§∏‡§ï‡§§‡•Ä‡•§ ‡§Ü‡§™‡§ï‡•ã **"Artificial Heat"** create ‡§ï‡§∞‡§®‡•Ä ‡§π‡•ã‡§ó‡•Ä‡•§

#### **Drill 1: The "Heckler" Simulation (‡§¶‡•ã‡§∏‡•ç‡§§ ‡§ï‡•Ä ‡§Æ‡§¶‡§¶ ‡§≤‡•á‡§Ç)**

* **Task:** ‡§Ö‡§™‡§®‡•á ‡§¶‡•ã‡§∏‡•ç‡§§ ‡§∏‡•á ‡§ï‡§π‡•á‡§Ç ‡§ï‡§ø ‡§µ‡•ã Interviewer ‡§¨‡§®‡•á‡•§
* **Action:** ‡§Ü‡§™ ‡§ú‡§µ‡§æ‡§¨ ‡§¶‡•á‡§®‡§æ ‡§∂‡•Å‡§∞‡•Ç ‡§ï‡§∞‡•á‡§Ç, ‡§î‡§∞ ‡§¶‡•ã‡§∏‡•ç‡§§ ‡§ï‡§æ ‡§ï‡§æ‡§Æ ‡§π‡•à:
* ‡§Ü‡§™‡§ï‡•ã ‡§¨‡•Ä‡§ö ‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç ‡§ü‡•ã‡§ï‡§®‡§æ‡•§
* ‡§Ü‡§™‡§ï‡§æ ‡§Æ‡§ú‡§æ‡§ï ‡§â‡§°‡§º‡§æ‡§®‡§æ ("‡§ï‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ ‡§¨‡§ï‡§µ‡§æ‡§∏ ‡§π‡•à!").
* ‡§ü‡•á‡§¨‡§≤ ‡§™‡§∞ ‡§ú‡•ã‡§∞ ‡§∏‡•á ‡§™‡•á‡§® ‡§™‡§ü‡§ï‡§®‡§æ‡•§


* **Goal:** ‡§ö‡§æ‡§π‡•á ‡§µ‡•ã ‡§ï‡•Å‡§õ ‡§≠‡•Ä ‡§ï‡§∞‡•á, ‡§Ü‡§™‡§ï‡•Ä **"Smile"** ‡§î‡§∞ **"Voice Tone"** ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç ‡§¨‡§¶‡§≤‡§®‡•Ä ‡§ö‡§æ‡§π‡§ø‡§è‡•§

#### **Drill 2: The "Staring Contest" (Tratak)**

* **Task:** ‡§∂‡•Ä‡§∂‡•á ‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç ‡§Ö‡§™‡§®‡•Ä ‡§Ü‡§Ç‡§ñ‡•ã‡§Ç ‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç ‡§¶‡•á‡§ñ‡•á‡§Ç‡•§
* **Action:** 1 ‡§Æ‡§ø‡§®‡§ü ‡§§‡§ï ‡§¨‡§ø‡§®‡§æ ‡§™‡§≤‡§ï ‡§ù‡§™‡§ï‡§æ‡§è (‡§Ø‡§æ ‡§ï‡§Æ ‡§ù‡§™‡§ï‡§æ‡§è) ‡§¶‡•á‡§ñ‡•á‡§Ç ‡§î‡§∞ ‡§ö‡•á‡§π‡§∞‡•á ‡§™‡§∞ ‡§è‡§ï ‡§π‡§≤‡•ç‡§ï‡•Ä ‡§Æ‡•Å‡§∏‡•ç‡§ï‡§æ‡§® ‡§∞‡§ñ‡•á‡§Ç‡•§
* **Goal:** ‡§ú‡§¨ Board ‡§ö‡•Å‡§™ ‡§π‡•ã‡§ï‡§∞ ‡§ò‡•Ç‡§∞‡•á, ‡§§‡•ã ‡§Ü‡§™‡§ï‡•ã ‡§®‡§ú‡§∞‡•á‡§Ç ‡§ö‡•Å‡§∞‡§æ‡§®‡•á ‡§ï‡•Ä ‡§Ü‡§¶‡§§ ‡§® ‡§π‡•ã‡•§

#### **Drill 3: The "Next Question" Anticipation**

* **Task:** ‡§ï‡•ã‡§à ‡§≠‡•Ä ‡§ü‡•â‡§™‡§ø‡§ï ‡§≤‡•á‡§Ç (e.g., Dowry System).
* **Action:** ‡§è‡§ï ‡§≤‡§æ‡§á‡§® ‡§¨‡•ã‡§≤‡•á‡§Ç ‡§î‡§∞ ‡§∏‡•ã‡§ö‡•á‡§Ç‚Äî *"‡§Ö‡§¨ ‡§µ‡•ã ‡§ï‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ ‡§™‡•Ç‡§õ‡•á‡§Ç‡§ó‡•á?"*
* *You:* "Dowry is a social evil..." -> *Next:* "Why laws failed?"
* *You:* "Laws failed due to lack of social will..." -> *Next:* "How will YOU generate social will?"


* **Goal:** ‡§∂‡§§‡§∞‡§Ç‡§ú (Chess) ‡§ï‡•Ä ‡§§‡§∞‡§π 2 ‡§ö‡§æ‡§≤ ‡§Ü‡§ó‡•á ‡§∏‡•ã‡§ö‡§®‡§æ‡•§

---

### **6. Neuro-Interrogation (Self-Reflection)**

1. **Face Check:** *"‡§ú‡§¨ ‡§ï‡•ã‡§à ‡§Æ‡•á‡§∞‡•Ä ‡§Ü‡§≤‡•ã‡§ö‡§®‡§æ (Criticism) ‡§ï‡§∞‡§§‡§æ ‡§π‡•à, ‡§§‡•ã ‡§ï‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ ‡§Æ‡•á‡§∞‡§æ ‡§ö‡•á‡§π‡§∞‡§æ ‡§≤‡§æ‡§≤ ‡§π‡•ã ‡§ú‡§æ‡§§‡§æ ‡§π‡•à?"*
2. **Voice Check:** *"‡§ú‡§¨ ‡§Æ‡•à‡§Ç ‡§¶‡§¨‡§æ‡§µ ‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç ‡§π‡•ã‡§§‡§æ ‡§π‡•Ç‡§Å, ‡§§‡•ã ‡§ï‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ ‡§Æ‡•á‡§∞‡•Ä ‡§Ü‡§µ‡§æ‡§ú‡§º ‡§™‡§§‡§≤‡•Ä (Shrill) ‡§Ø‡§æ ‡§§‡•á‡§ú‡§º ‡§π‡•ã ‡§ú‡§æ‡§§‡•Ä ‡§π‡•à?"*
* (‡§Ü‡§µ‡§æ‡§ú‡§º ‡§ï‡•ã ‡§™‡•á‡§ü ‡§∏‡•á ‡§®‡§ø‡§ï‡§æ‡§≤‡•á‡§Ç - Deep Voice, not Throat Voice).


3. **Defensive Trigger:** *"‡§ï‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ 'Why?' ‡§∏‡•Å‡§®‡§§‡•á ‡§π‡•Ä ‡§Æ‡•Å‡§ù‡•á ‡§≤‡§ó‡§§‡§æ ‡§π‡•à ‡§ï‡§ø ‡§Æ‡•à‡§Ç‡§®‡•á ‡§ï‡•Å‡§õ ‡§ó‡§≤‡§§ ‡§ï‡§∞ ‡§¶‡§ø‡§Ø‡§æ?"*
* ('Why' ‡§ï‡§æ ‡§Æ‡§§‡§≤‡§¨ ‡§ó‡§≤‡§§‡•Ä ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç, ‡§µ‡•ã ‡§¨‡§∏ ‡§ï‡§æ‡§∞‡§£ ‡§ú‡§æ‡§®‡§®‡§æ ‡§ö‡§æ‡§π‡§§‡•á ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç‡•§)



---

### **7. Overall Effect on Interview**

‡§ú‡§¨ ‡§Ü‡§™ Stress ‡§ï‡•ã "Poker Face" ‡§∏‡•á ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç‡§°‡§≤ ‡§ï‡§∞‡§§‡•á ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç:

1. **Unshakeable:** Board ‡§ï‡•ã ‡§≤‡§ó‡§§‡§æ ‡§π‡•à‚Äî *"‡§Ø‡§π ‡§ö‡§ü‡•ç‡§ü‡§æ‡§® ‡§π‡•à‡•§ ‡§á‡§∏‡•á ‡§π‡§ø‡§≤‡§æ‡§Ø‡§æ ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç ‡§ú‡§æ ‡§∏‡§ï‡§§‡§æ‡•§"*
2. **Crisis Ready:** ‡§µ‡•ã ‡§∏‡§Æ‡§ù ‡§ú‡§æ‡§§‡•á ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç ‡§ï‡§ø ‡§¶‡§Ç‡§ó‡•á ‡§Ø‡§æ ‡§Ü‡§™‡§¶‡§æ (Disaster) ‡§ï‡•á ‡§∏‡§Æ‡§Ø ‡§Ø‡§π ‡§ë‡§´‡§ø‡§∏‡§∞ panic ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç ‡§ï‡§∞‡•á‡§ó‡§æ‡•§
3. **Respect:** ‡§ú‡•ã ‡§á‡§Ç‡§∏‡§æ‡§® ‡§Ö‡§™‡§Æ‡§æ‡§® (Insult) ‡§∏‡§π‡§ï‡§∞ ‡§≠‡•Ä ‡§Æ‡•Å‡§∏‡•ç‡§ï‡•Å‡§∞‡§æ‡§§‡§æ ‡§∞‡§π‡•á, ‡§µ‡•ã ‡§∏‡§¨‡§∏‡•á ‡§ú‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ‡§¶‡§æ ‡§§‡§æ‡§ï‡§§‡§µ‡§∞ ‡§π‡•ã‡§§‡§æ ‡§π‡•à‡•§

---

### **Today's Action Plan (‡§Ü‡§ú ‡§ï‡§æ ‡§π‡•ã‡§Æ‡§µ‡§∞‡•ç‡§ï)**

1. **Simulation:** ‡§Ö‡§™‡§®‡•á ‡§ò‡§∞ ‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç ‡§ï‡§ø‡§∏‡•Ä ‡§ï‡•ã ‡§¨‡•ã‡§≤‡•á‡§Ç ‡§ï‡§ø ‡§µ‡•ã ‡§Ü‡§™‡§ï‡•ã ‡§≤‡§ó‡§æ‡§§‡§æ‡§∞ 2 ‡§Æ‡§ø‡§®‡§ü ‡§§‡§ï "Insult" ‡§ï‡§∞‡•á ‡§Ø‡§æ "Discourage" ‡§ï‡§∞‡•á‡•§
* ‡§Ü‡§™ ‡§∏‡§ø‡§∞‡•ç‡§´ ‡§Æ‡•Å‡§∏‡•ç‡§ï‡•Å‡§∞‡§æ‡§ï‡§∞ "Thank you for your feedback" ‡§¨‡•ã‡§≤‡•á‡§Ç‡•§


2. **Draft:** *"Why is Bihar backward?"* ‡§∏‡§µ‡§æ‡§≤ ‡§ï‡§æ ‡§è‡§ï ‡§ê‡§∏‡§æ ‡§ú‡§µ‡§æ‡§¨ ‡§≤‡§ø‡§ñ‡•á‡§Ç ‡§ú‡•ã ‡§® ‡§§‡•ã Defensive ‡§π‡•ã ‡§î‡§∞ ‡§® ‡§π‡•Ä ‡§∏‡§∞‡§ï‡§æ‡§∞ ‡§µ‡§ø‡§∞‡•ã‡§ß‡•Ä‡•§ (Fact + Hope).

**Chapter Mantra:**

> *"‡§Ü‡§ó ‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç ‡§§‡§™‡§ï‡§∞ ‡§π‡•Ä ‡§∏‡•ã‡§®‡§æ '‡§ï‡•Å‡§Ç‡§¶‡§®' ‡§¨‡§®‡§§‡§æ ‡§π‡•à‡•§ Board ‡§ï‡§æ ‡§ó‡•Å‡§∏‡•ç‡§∏‡§æ (Anger) ‡§Ü‡§™‡§ï‡•Ä ‡§™‡§∞‡•Ä‡§ï‡•ç‡§∑‡§æ ‡§π‡•à, ‡§â‡§∏‡•á '‡§Æ‡•Å‡§∏‡•ç‡§ï‡§æ‡§®' (Smile) ‡§∏‡•á ‡§π‡§∞‡§æ‡§ì‡•§"*

---

**Next:** **Chapter 14 (Crisis Management - War Room SRTs)** ‚Äî ‡§Ö‡§¨ ‡§π‡§Æ ‡§Ü‡§™‡§ï‡•ã ‡§∏‡•Ä‡§ß‡•á "‡§Æ‡•à‡§¶‡§æ‡§®" ‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç ‡§â‡§§‡§æ‡§∞‡•á‡§Ç‡§ó‡•á‡•§ *"‡§Ü‡§™ DM ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç, ‡§î‡§∞ ‡§¨‡§æ‡§¢‡§º ‡§Ü ‡§ó‡§à ‡§π‡•à..."* ‚Äî Step-by-step SOP ‡§ï‡•à‡§∏‡•á ‡§¨‡§®‡§æ‡§®‡§æ ‡§π‡•à‡•§

# üìò THE INTERVIEW MASTERY PROTOCOL
This chapter is the **Ultimate Test**. This is where the Board stops treating you like a candidate and starts testing you like a **Commander**.
**From "Mains Candidate" to "Commissioned Officer"**

## Chapter 14: Crisis Management (War Room SRTs - ‡§ú‡§¨ ‡§Ü‡§™ DM ‡§ï‡•Ä ‡§ï‡•Å‡§∞‡•ç‡§∏‡•Ä ‡§™‡§∞ ‡§π‡•ã‡§Ç)

**Core Focus:** "Action" under Pressure (‡§¶‡§¨‡§æ‡§µ ‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç ‡§∏‡§π‡•Ä ‡§®‡§ø‡§∞‡•ç‡§£‡§Ø).
**The Framework:** **The CCR Model (Containment \rightarrow Communication \rightarrow Resolution).**

---

### **Namaskar Future Officer.**

Interview Board ‡§Ü‡§™‡§ï‡•ã ‡§è‡§ï "Hypothetical Fire" (‡§ï‡§æ‡§≤‡•ç‡§™‡§®‡§ø‡§ï ‡§Ü‡§ó) ‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç ‡§´‡•á‡§Ç‡§ï‡•á‡§ó‡§æ‡•§ ‡§µ‡•ã ‡§ï‡§π‡•á‡§Ç‡§ó‡•á:

* *"Imagine you are the SDM. A communal riot has broken out during a procession. Stone pelting has started. What will you do?"*

‡§Ø‡§π‡§æ‡§Å Board ‡§ï‡•ã "‡§∏‡§π‡•Ä ‡§ú‡§µ‡§æ‡§¨" ‡§∏‡•á ‡§ú‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ‡§¶‡§æ ‡§Ü‡§™‡§ï‡•Ä **"Process"** ‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç ‡§¶‡§ø‡§≤‡§ö‡§∏‡•ç‡§™‡•Ä ‡§π‡•à‡•§

‡§¶‡•ã ‡§§‡§∞‡§π ‡§ï‡•á Candidates ‡§´‡•á‡§≤ ‡§π‡•ã‡§§‡•á ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç:

1. **The Singham (Film Hero):** *"‡§∏‡§∞, ‡§Æ‡•à‡§Ç ‡§Æ‡•å‡§ï‡•á ‡§™‡§∞ ‡§ú‡§æ‡§ï‡§∞ ‡§∏‡§¨‡§ï‡•ã ‡§Æ‡§æ‡§∞‡•Ç‡§Ç‡§ó‡§æ ‡§î‡§∞ ‡§ó‡•ã‡§≤‡•Ä ‡§ö‡§≤‡§æ ‡§¶‡•Ç‡§Ç‡§ó‡§æ‡•§"* (Result: You will trigger a massacre. Rejected.)
2. **The Panic Master (Darpok):** *"‡§∏‡§∞, ‡§Æ‡•à‡§Ç SP ‡§∏‡§∞ ‡§ï‡•ã ‡§´‡•ã‡§® ‡§ï‡§∞‡•Ç‡§Å‡§ó‡§æ... ‡§Æ‡•à‡§Ç ‡§∏‡•Ä‡§®‡§ø‡§Ø‡§∞ ‡§∏‡•á ‡§™‡•Ç‡§õ‡•Ç‡§Ç‡§ó‡§æ..."* (Result: You are indecisive. Rejected.)

‡§è‡§ï **Officer** "Hero" ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç ‡§π‡•ã‡§§‡§æ, ‡§µ‡•ã "Administrator" ‡§π‡•ã‡§§‡§æ ‡§π‡•à‡•§ ‡§µ‡•ã **SOP (Standard Operating Procedure)** ‡§∏‡•á ‡§ö‡§≤‡§§‡§æ ‡§π‡•à‡•§

---

### **1. The Core Mechanics: The CCR Model**

‡§ï‡§ø‡§∏‡•Ä ‡§≠‡•Ä Crisis (‡§¶‡§Ç‡§ó‡§æ, ‡§¨‡§æ‡§¢‡§º, ‡§Ü‡§ó) ‡§ï‡•ã handle ‡§ï‡§∞‡§®‡•á ‡§ï‡§æ ‡§è‡§ï ‡§π‡•Ä Universal Formula ‡§π‡•à‡•§ ‡§á‡§∏‡•á ‡§∞‡§ü ‡§≤‡•á‡§Ç:

1. **Containment (‡§∞‡•ã‡§ï‡§•‡§æ‡§Æ - Immediate Action):**
* ‡§∏‡§¨‡§∏‡•á ‡§™‡§π‡§≤‡•á "Bleeding" ‡§∞‡•ã‡§ï‡•á‡§Ç‡•§ (e.g., ‡§≠‡•Ä‡§°‡§º ‡§ï‡•ã ‡§§‡§ø‡§§‡§∞-‡§¨‡§ø‡§§‡§∞ ‡§ï‡§∞‡§®‡§æ, ‡§™‡§æ‡§®‡•Ä ‡§∞‡•ã‡§ï‡§®‡§æ, ‡§Ü‡§ó ‡§¨‡•Å‡§ù‡§æ‡§®‡§æ)‡•§
* Goal: ‡§ú‡§æ‡§®-‡§Æ‡§æ‡§≤ ‡§ï‡§æ ‡§®‡•Å‡§ï‡§∏‡§æ‡§® ‡§ï‡§Æ ‡§ï‡§∞‡§®‡§æ‡•§


2. **Communication (‡§∏‡•Ç‡§ö‡§®‡§æ - Information Flow):**
* ‡§∏‡§π‡•Ä ‡§≤‡•ã‡§ó‡•ã‡§Ç ‡§ï‡•ã inform ‡§ï‡§∞‡§®‡§æ (Seniors, Media, Control Room) ‡§§‡§æ‡§ï‡§ø ‡§Ö‡§´‡§µ‡§æ‡§π (Rumors) ‡§® ‡§´‡•à‡§≤‡•á‡•§


3. **Resolution (‡§∏‡§Æ‡§æ‡§ß‡§æ‡§® - Long Term):**
* ‡§ú‡§æ‡§Ç‡§ö (Inquiry) ‡§î‡§∞ ‡§≠‡§µ‡§ø‡§∑‡•ç‡§Ø ‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç ‡§ê‡§∏‡§æ ‡§® ‡§π‡•ã, ‡§â‡§∏‡§ï‡•Ä ‡§™‡•ç‡§≤‡§æ‡§®‡§ø‡§Ç‡§ó‡•§



**Golden Rule:**

> *"Crisis ‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç 'Emotion' ‡§ï‡•ã ‡§ò‡§∞ ‡§™‡§∞ ‡§õ‡•ã‡§°‡§º ‡§Ü‡§è‡§Ç‡•§ ‡§Ü‡§™‡§ï‡•ã 'Rule of Law' ‡§î‡§∞ 'Public Safety' ‡§ï‡•ã ‡§∏‡§¨‡§∏‡•á ‡§ä‡§™‡§∞ ‡§∞‡§ñ‡§®‡§æ ‡§π‡•à‡•§"*

---

### **2. The 5 Examples: War Room Scenarios (SRTs)**

‡§®‡•Ä‡§ö‡•á 5 ‡§∏‡§¨‡§∏‡•á common Situations ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç ‡§ú‡•ã Board ‡§™‡•Ç‡§õ‡§§‡§æ ‡§π‡•à‡•§ ‡§¶‡•á‡§ñ‡§ø‡§è ‡§è‡§ï Officer ‡§ï‡•à‡§∏‡•á ‡§∏‡•ã‡§ö‡§§‡§æ ‡§π‡•à‡•§

#### **Scenario 1: The Communal Riot (‡§∏‡§æ‡§Ç‡§™‡•ç‡§∞‡§¶‡§æ‡§Ø‡§ø‡§ï ‡§¶‡§Ç‡§ó‡§æ)**

**Question:** *"You are SDM. During a religious procession (‡§ú‡•Å‡§≤‡•Ç‡§∏), stone pelting starts. The mob is getting violent. Will you order firing?"*

* ‚ùå **Wrong Answer:** "‡§π‡§æ‡§Å ‡§∏‡§∞, ‡§≠‡•Ä‡§°‡§º ‡§ï‡•ã ‡§∞‡•ã‡§ï‡§®‡•á ‡§ï‡•á ‡§≤‡§ø‡§è ‡§ó‡•ã‡§≤‡•Ä ‡§ö‡§≤‡§æ‡§®‡•Ä ‡§™‡§°‡§º‡•á‡§ó‡•Ä‡•§" (Too Aggressive).
* ‚úÖ **The SOP Answer (CCR Model):**
> **Containment:** "Sir, ‡§Æ‡•á‡§∞‡•Ä ‡§™‡§π‡§≤‡•Ä ‡§™‡•ç‡§∞‡§æ‡§•‡§Æ‡§ø‡§ï‡§§‡§æ (Priority) ‡§π‡§ø‡§Ç‡§∏‡§æ ‡§ï‡•ã ‡§§‡•Å‡§∞‡§Ç‡§§ ‡§∞‡•ã‡§ï‡§®‡§æ ‡§π‡•à‡•§
> 1. ‡§Æ‡•à‡§Ç ‡§Æ‡•å‡§ï‡•á ‡§™‡§∞ ‡§™‡§π‡•Å‡§Ç‡§ö‡§ï‡§∞ **Force Multiplier** (Loudspeaker) ‡§∏‡•á ‡§ö‡•á‡§§‡§æ‡§µ‡§®‡•Ä ‡§¶‡•Ç‡§Ç‡§ó‡§æ‡•§
> 2. ‡§´‡§ø‡§∞ **Graded Force** ‡§ï‡§æ ‡§™‡•ç‡§∞‡§Ø‡•ã‡§ó ‡§ï‡§∞‡•Ç‡§Å‡§ó‡§æ: Tear Gas \rightarrow Water Cannon \rightarrow Lathi Charge.
> 3. ‡§Ö‡§ó‡§∞ ‡§ú‡§æ‡§® ‡§ï‡§æ ‡§ñ‡§§‡§∞‡§æ (Threat to Life) ‡§π‡•à, ‡§§‡•ã ‡§π‡•Ä ‡§Ö‡§Ç‡§§‡§ø‡§Æ ‡§µ‡§ø‡§ï‡§≤‡•ç‡§™ (Last Resort) ‡§ï‡•á ‡§∞‡•Ç‡§™ ‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç 'Firing below the waist' (‡§™‡•à‡§∞‡•ã‡§Ç ‡§™‡§∞) ‡§ï‡§æ ‡§Ü‡§¶‡•á‡§∂ ‡§¶‡•Ç‡§Ç‡§ó‡§æ‡•§
> ‡§∏‡§æ‡§• ‡§π‡•Ä Section 144 ‡§≤‡§ó‡§æ‡§ä‡§Ç‡§ó‡§æ‡•§
> **Communication:** Control Room ‡§ï‡•ã ‡§∏‡•Ç‡§ö‡§ø‡§§ ‡§ï‡§∞‡•Ç‡§Å‡§ó‡§æ ‡§§‡§æ‡§ï‡§ø extra force ‡§Ü ‡§∏‡§ï‡•á ‡§î‡§∞ ‡§Ö‡§´‡§µ‡§æ‡§π ‡§∞‡•ã‡§ï‡§®‡•á ‡§ï‡•á ‡§≤‡§ø‡§è Internet shutdown ‡§™‡§∞ ‡§µ‡§ø‡§ö‡§æ‡§∞ ‡§ï‡§∞‡•Ç‡§Å‡§ó‡§æ‡•§
> **Resolution:** ‡§∂‡§æ‡§Ç‡§§‡§ø ‡§∏‡§Æ‡§ø‡§§‡§ø (Peace Committee) ‡§ï‡•Ä ‡§¨‡•à‡§†‡§ï ‡§¨‡•Å‡§≤‡§æ‡§ï‡§∞ ‡§¶‡•ã‡§®‡•ã‡§Ç ‡§™‡§ï‡•ç‡§∑‡•ã‡§Ç ‡§∏‡•á ‡§¨‡§æ‡§§ ‡§ï‡§∞‡•Ç‡§Å‡§ó‡§æ‡•§"
> 
> 



#### **Scenario 2: The Flood Rescue (VIP Pressure)**

**Question:** *"Your district is flooded. You have only 1 boat. A Minister calls you to save his family in Village A, but Village B has poor people drowning. What will you do?"*

* ‚ùå **Wrong Answer:** "‡§Æ‡•à‡§Ç ‡§Æ‡§Ç‡§§‡•ç‡§∞‡•Ä ‡§ú‡•Ä ‡§ï‡•Ä ‡§¨‡§æ‡§§ ‡§Æ‡§æ‡§® ‡§≤‡•Ç‡§Ç‡§ó‡§æ ‡§µ‡§∞‡§®‡§æ ‡§ü‡•ç‡§∞‡§æ‡§Ç‡§∏‡§´‡§∞ ‡§π‡•ã ‡§ú‡§æ‡§è‡§ó‡§æ‡•§" (Corrupt).
* ‚úÖ **The SOP Answer (Triage):**
> "Sir, ‡§Ü‡§™‡§¶‡§æ ‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç **'Protocol of Triage'** (‡§ú‡•ã ‡§∏‡§¨‡§∏‡•á ‡§ú‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ‡§¶‡§æ ‡§ñ‡§§‡§∞‡•á ‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç ‡§π‡•à, ‡§µ‡•ã ‡§™‡§π‡§≤‡•á) ‡§ö‡§≤‡§§‡§æ ‡§π‡•à‡•§
> 1. **Assess:** ‡§Æ‡•à‡§Ç ‡§¶‡•á‡§ñ‡•Ç‡§Ç‡§ó‡§æ ‡§ï‡§ø 'Immediate Danger' (‡§°‡•Ç‡§¨‡§®‡•á ‡§ï‡§æ ‡§ñ‡§§‡§∞‡§æ) ‡§ï‡§π‡§æ‡§Å ‡§ú‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ‡§¶‡§æ ‡§π‡•à‡•§ ‡§Ö‡§ó‡§∞ Village B ‡§ï‡•á ‡§≤‡•ã‡§ó ‡§°‡•Ç‡§¨ ‡§∞‡§π‡•á ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç ‡§î‡§∞ Minister ‡§ï‡•Ä ‡§´‡•à‡§Æ‡§ø‡§≤‡•Ä ‡§∏‡§ø‡§∞‡•ç‡§´ ‡§´‡§Ç‡§∏‡•Ä ‡§π‡•Å‡§à (Stranded but safe) ‡§π‡•à, ‡§§‡•ã Boat Village B ‡§ú‡§æ‡§è‡§ó‡•Ä‡•§
> 2. **Communicate:** ‡§Æ‡•à‡§Ç ‡§Æ‡§Ç‡§§‡•ç‡§∞‡•Ä ‡§ú‡•Ä ‡§ï‡•ã ‡§µ‡§ø‡§®‡§Æ‡•ç‡§∞‡§§‡§æ ‡§∏‡•á ‡§¨‡§§‡§æ ‡§¶‡•Ç‡§Ç‡§ó‡§æ ‡§ï‡§ø 'Resoruces are diverted to critical casualties' ‡§î‡§∞ ‡§ú‡•à‡§∏‡•á ‡§π‡•Ä ‡§®‡§æ‡§µ ‡§ñ‡§æ‡§≤‡•Ä ‡§π‡•ã‡§ó‡•Ä, ‡§â‡§®‡§ï‡•á ‡§™‡§∞‡§ø‡§µ‡§æ‡§∞ ‡§ï‡•ã ‡§®‡§ø‡§ï‡§æ‡§≤ ‡§≤‡§ø‡§Ø‡§æ ‡§ú‡§æ‡§è‡§ó‡§æ‡•§
> 3. **Action:** ‡§è‡§ï ‡§™‡•ç‡§∞‡§∂‡§æ‡§∏‡§ï ‡§ï‡•á ‡§§‡•å‡§∞ ‡§™‡§∞ ‡§Æ‡•á‡§∞‡§æ ‡§ß‡§∞‡•ç‡§Æ 'Public Safety' ‡§π‡•à, 'VIP Service' ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç‡•§"
> 
> 



#### **Scenario 3: The Mob Lynching / Accident**

**Question:** *"Your official vehicle hits a pedestrian by mistake. A mob gathers and starts banging on your car. You have a gun. What will you do?"*

* ‚ùå **Wrong Answer:** "‡§Æ‡•à‡§Ç ‡§¨‡§æ‡§π‡§∞ ‡§®‡§ø‡§ï‡§≤‡§ï‡§∞ ‡§â‡§®‡§∏‡•á ‡§¨‡§æ‡§§ ‡§ï‡§∞‡•Ç‡§Å‡§ó‡§æ" (Suicidal) ‡§Ø‡§æ "‡§Æ‡•à‡§Ç ‡§ó‡•ã‡§≤‡•Ä ‡§ö‡§≤‡§æ ‡§¶‡•Ç‡§Ç‡§ó‡§æ" (Criminal).
* ‚úÖ **The SOP Answer (Self-Defense & Law):**
> "Sir, ‡§á‡§∏ ‡§∏‡•ç‡§•‡§ø‡§§‡§ø ‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç 'Crowd Psychology' ‡§ï‡§æ‡§Æ ‡§ï‡§∞‡§§‡•Ä ‡§π‡•à, ‡§§‡§∞‡•ç‡§ï (Logic) ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç‡•§
> 1. **Containment:** ‡§Æ‡•à‡§Ç ‡§ó‡§æ‡§°‡§º‡•Ä ‡§∏‡•á ‡§¨‡§æ‡§π‡§∞ ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç ‡§®‡§ø‡§ï‡§≤‡•Ç‡§Ç‡§ó‡§æ ‡§î‡§∞ ‡§∂‡•Ä‡§∂‡•á ‡§¨‡§Ç‡§¶ ‡§∞‡§ñ‡•Ç‡§Ç‡§ó‡§æ‡•§ ‡§Æ‡•à‡§Ç ‡§°‡•ç‡§∞‡§æ‡§á‡§µ‡§∞ ‡§ï‡•ã ‡§ó‡§æ‡§°‡§º‡•Ä ‡§ß‡•Ä‡§∞‡•á-‡§ß‡•Ä‡§∞‡•á ‡§∏‡•Å‡§∞‡§ï‡•ç‡§∑‡§ø‡§§ ‡§∏‡•ç‡§•‡§æ‡§® (Nearest Police Station) ‡§ï‡•Ä ‡§ì‡§∞ ‡§≤‡•á ‡§ú‡§æ‡§®‡•á ‡§ï‡•ã ‡§ï‡§π‡•Ç‡§Ç‡§ó‡§æ‡•§
> 2. **Communication:** ‡§Æ‡•à‡§Ç ‡§§‡•Å‡§∞‡§Ç‡§§ SP ‡§∏‡§æ‡§π‡§¨ ‡§ï‡•ã location ‡§≠‡•á‡§ú‡•Ç‡§Ç‡§ó‡§æ‡•§
> 3. **Resolution:** ‡§∏‡•Å‡§∞‡§ï‡•ç‡§∑‡§ø‡§§ ‡§π‡•ã‡§®‡•á ‡§ï‡•á ‡§¨‡§æ‡§¶, ‡§Æ‡•à‡§Ç ‡§ñ‡•Å‡§¶ ‡§ï‡§æ‡§®‡•Ç‡§® ‡§ï‡§æ ‡§™‡§æ‡§≤‡§® ‡§ï‡§∞‡•Ç‡§Å‡§ó‡§æ‡•§ ‡§ò‡§æ‡§Ø‡§≤ ‡§µ‡•ç‡§Ø‡§ï‡•ç‡§§‡§ø ‡§ï‡•ã ‡§Ö‡§∏‡•ç‡§™‡§§‡§æ‡§≤ ‡§™‡§π‡•Å‡§Ç‡§ö‡§æ‡§®‡§æ ‡§î‡§∞ ‡§™‡•Å‡§≤‡§ø‡§∏ ‡§ï‡•ã statement ‡§¶‡•á‡§®‡§æ ‡§Æ‡•á‡§∞‡•Ä ‡§ú‡§ø‡§Æ‡•ç‡§Æ‡•á‡§¶‡§æ‡§∞‡•Ä ‡§π‡•à‡•§ ‡§Æ‡•à‡§Ç ‡§™‡§¶ ‡§ï‡§æ ‡§¶‡•Å‡§∞‡•Å‡§™‡§Ø‡•ã‡§ó ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç ‡§ï‡§∞‡•Ç‡§Å‡§ó‡§æ‡•§"
> 
> 



#### **Scenario 4: The "Hospital Negligence" (Doctor vs Public)**

**Question:** *"A patient died in the Sadar Hospital. Relatives are beating the Doctor. You reach the spot. They demand immediate arrest of the Doctor."*

* ‚ùå **Wrong Answer:** "‡§≠‡•Ä‡§°‡§º ‡§ï‡•ã ‡§∂‡§æ‡§Ç‡§§ ‡§ï‡§∞‡§®‡•á ‡§ï‡•á ‡§≤‡§ø‡§è ‡§°‡•â‡§ï‡•ç‡§ü‡§∞ ‡§ï‡•ã ‡§Ö‡§∞‡•á‡§∏‡•ç‡§ü ‡§ï‡§∞ ‡§≤‡•Ç‡§Ç‡§ó‡§æ‡•§" (Injustice to Doctor).
* ‚úÖ **The SOP Answer (De-escalation):**
> "Sir, ‡§Ø‡§π 'Emotional Outburst' ‡§π‡•à‡•§
> 1. **Containment:** ‡§∏‡§¨‡§∏‡•á ‡§™‡§π‡§≤‡•á ‡§Æ‡•à‡§Ç ‡§™‡•Å‡§≤‡§ø‡§∏ ‡§¨‡§≤ ‡§ï‡•á ‡§∏‡§æ‡§• ‡§°‡•â‡§ï‡•ç‡§ü‡§∞ ‡§ï‡•ã ‡§∏‡•Å‡§∞‡§ï‡•ç‡§∑‡§ø‡§§ (Rescue) ‡§ï‡§∞‡•Ç‡§Å‡§ó‡§æ ‡§ï‡•ç‡§Ø‡•ã‡§Ç‡§ï‡§ø 'Medical Protection Act' ‡§ï‡•á ‡§§‡§π‡§§ ‡§â‡§®‡•ç‡§π‡•á‡§Ç ‡§∏‡•Å‡§∞‡§ï‡•ç‡§∑‡§æ ‡§™‡•ç‡§∞‡§æ‡§™‡•ç‡§§ ‡§π‡•à‡•§
> 2. **Communication:** ‡§Æ‡•à‡§Ç ‡§≠‡•Ä‡§°‡§º ‡§ï‡•á ‡§®‡•á‡§§‡§æ‡§ì‡§Ç (Leaders) ‡§∏‡•á ‡§¨‡§æ‡§§ ‡§ï‡§∞‡•Ç‡§Å‡§ó‡§æ ‡§î‡§∞ ‡§â‡§®‡•ç‡§π‡•á‡§Ç **'Magisterial Inquiry'** (‡§®‡§ø‡§∑‡•ç‡§™‡§ï‡•ç‡§∑ ‡§ú‡§æ‡§Ç‡§ö) ‡§ï‡§æ ‡§≤‡§ø‡§ñ‡§ø‡§§ ‡§Ü‡§∂‡•ç‡§µ‡§æ‡§∏‡§® (Assurance) ‡§¶‡•Ç‡§Ç‡§ó‡§æ‡•§
> 3. **Resolution:** ‡§Ö‡§ó‡§∞ ‡§°‡•â‡§ï‡•ç‡§ü‡§∞ ‡§¶‡•ã‡§∑‡•Ä ‡§™‡§æ‡§è ‡§ó‡§è, ‡§§‡•ã ‡§ï‡§æ‡§∞‡•ç‡§∞‡§µ‡§æ‡§à ‡§π‡•ã‡§ó‡•Ä, ‡§≤‡•á‡§ï‡§ø‡§® ‡§≠‡•Ä‡§°‡§º ‡§ï‡•á ‡§¶‡§¨‡§æ‡§µ ‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç ‡§ó‡§ø‡§∞‡§´‡•ç‡§§‡§æ‡§∞‡•Ä ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç ‡§π‡•ã‡§ó‡•Ä‡•§"
> 
> 



#### **Scenario 5: The "Exam Center" Crisis**

**Question:** *"You are DM. 15 minutes before the BPSC exam, a rumor spreads that the paper is leaked. Students start protesting and refuse to enter. What will you do?"*

* ‚ùå **Wrong Answer:** "‡§Æ‡•à‡§Ç ‡§è‡§ó‡•ç‡§ú‡§æ‡§Æ ‡§ï‡•à‡§Ç‡§∏‡§ø‡§≤ ‡§ï‡§∞ ‡§¶‡•Ç‡§Ç‡§ó‡§æ‡•§" (Hasty Decision).
* ‚úÖ **The SOP Answer (Fact-Check):**
> "Sir, ‡§Ö‡§´‡§µ‡§æ‡§π (Rumor) ‡§î‡§∞ ‡§§‡§•‡•ç‡§Ø (Fact) ‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç ‡§Ö‡§Ç‡§§‡§∞ ‡§π‡•à‡•§
> 1. **Containment:** ‡§Æ‡•à‡§Ç ‡§§‡•Å‡§∞‡§Ç‡§§ ‡§Æ‡§æ‡§á‡§ï ‡§™‡§∞ announcement ‡§ï‡§∞‡•Ç‡§Å‡§ó‡§æ ‡§ï‡§ø 'Paper Secure' ‡§π‡•à ‡§î‡§∞ ‡§Ö‡§´‡§µ‡§æ‡§π‡•ã‡§Ç ‡§™‡§∞ ‡§ß‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ‡§® ‡§® ‡§¶‡•á‡§Ç‡•§
> 2. **Action:** ‡§Æ‡•à‡§Ç ‡§™‡•ç‡§∞‡§∂‡•ç‡§®-‡§™‡§§‡•ç‡§∞ (Question Paper) ‡§ï‡•á ‡§∏‡•Ä‡§≤ (Seal) ‡§ï‡•ã ‡§õ‡§æ‡§§‡•ç‡§∞‡•ã‡§Ç ‡§ï‡•á ‡§™‡•ç‡§∞‡§§‡§ø‡§®‡§ø‡§ß‡§ø‡§Ø‡•ã‡§Ç (Student Reps) ‡§î‡§∞ ‡§µ‡•Ä‡§°‡§ø‡§Ø‡•ã‡§ó‡•ç‡§∞‡§æ‡§´‡•Ä ‡§ï‡•á ‡§∏‡§æ‡§Æ‡§®‡•á ‡§ñ‡•ã‡§≤‡•Ç‡§Ç‡§ó‡§æ ‡§§‡§æ‡§ï‡§ø ‡§™‡§æ‡§∞‡§¶‡§∞‡•ç‡§∂‡§ø‡§§‡§æ (Transparency) ‡§¶‡§ø‡§ñ‡•á‡•§
> 3. **Communication:** ‡§Ö‡§ó‡§∞ ‡§≤‡•Ä‡§ï ‡§ï‡•Ä ‡§™‡•Å‡§∑‡•ç‡§ü‡§ø ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç ‡§π‡•ã‡§§‡•Ä ‡§π‡•à, ‡§§‡•ã ‡§è‡§ó‡•ç‡§ú‡§æ‡§Æ ‡§∏‡§Æ‡§Ø ‡§™‡§∞ ‡§π‡•ã‡§ó‡§æ‡•§ ‡§Ö‡§ó‡§∞ ‡§™‡•Å‡§∑‡•ç‡§ü‡§ø ‡§π‡•ã‡§§‡•Ä ‡§π‡•à, ‡§§‡•ã Commission ‡§∏‡•á ‡§¨‡§æ‡§§ ‡§ï‡§∞‡§ï‡•á ‡§π‡•Ä ‡§ï‡•à‡§Ç‡§∏‡§ø‡§≤ ‡§ï‡§∞‡§®‡•á ‡§ï‡§æ ‡§®‡§ø‡§∞‡•ç‡§£‡§Ø ‡§≤‡•Ç‡§Ç‡§ó‡§æ‡•§"
> 
> 



---

### **3. Potential Board Questions (Prepare for Fire)**

Board ‡§Ü‡§™‡§ï‡•ã ‡§á‡§® ‡§∏‡§µ‡§æ‡§≤‡•ã‡§Ç ‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç 10-20 ‡§∏‡•á‡§ï‡§Ç‡§° ‡§∏‡•á ‡§ú‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ‡§¶‡§æ ‡§∏‡•ã‡§ö‡§®‡•á ‡§ï‡§æ ‡§µ‡§ï‡•ç‡§§ ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç ‡§¶‡•á‡§ó‡§æ‡•§

**Type A: Law & Order**

1. *"‡§Ü‡§™ ‡§è‡§ï ‡§Æ‡§π‡§ø‡§≤‡§æ SDM ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç‡•§ ‡§¶‡§Ç‡§ó‡§æ‡§à ‡§Ü‡§™‡§ï‡•ã ‡§ò‡•á‡§∞ ‡§≤‡•á‡§§‡•á ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç ‡§î‡§∞ ‡§Ö‡§≠‡§¶‡•ç‡§∞ (Abusive) ‡§≠‡§æ‡§∑‡§æ ‡§ï‡§æ ‡§™‡•ç‡§∞‡§Ø‡•ã‡§ó ‡§ï‡§∞‡§§‡•á ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç‡•§ ‡§Ü‡§™ ‡§ï‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ ‡§ï‡§∞‡•á‡§Ç‡§ó‡•Ä?"*
* *(Hint: Ignore insults, focus on tactical command. Don't cry, don't get angry. Use force if threat escalates.)*


2. *"‡§Ü‡§™‡§ï‡•á ‡§ú‡§ø‡§≤‡•á ‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç ‡§ú‡§π‡§∞‡•Ä‡§≤‡•Ä ‡§∂‡§∞‡§æ‡§¨ (Hooch Tragedy) ‡§∏‡•á 10 ‡§≤‡•ã‡§ó ‡§Æ‡§∞ ‡§ó‡§è‡•§ ‡§Æ‡•Ä‡§°‡§ø‡§Ø‡§æ ‡§Ü‡§™ ‡§™‡§∞ ‡§∏‡§µ‡§æ‡§≤ ‡§â‡§†‡§æ ‡§∞‡§π‡•Ä ‡§π‡•à‡•§ ‡§Ü‡§™ ‡§™‡•ç‡§∞‡•á‡§∏ ‡§ï‡•â‡§®‡•ç‡§´‡•ç‡§∞‡•á‡§Ç‡§∏ ‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç ‡§ï‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ ‡§¨‡•ã‡§≤‡•á‡§Ç‡§ó‡•á?"*
* *(Hint: Accept responsibility, announce medical help for survivors, crackdown on mafia. No blame game.)*



**Type B: Administrative Ethics**
3.  *"Election ‡§ï‡•á ‡§¶‡§ø‡§® ‡§Ü‡§™‡§ï‡•ã ‡§™‡§§‡§æ ‡§ö‡§≤‡§§‡§æ ‡§π‡•à ‡§ï‡§ø EVM ‡§Æ‡§∂‡•Ä‡§® ‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç ‡§ñ‡§∞‡§æ‡§¨‡•Ä ‡§π‡•à ‡§î‡§∞ ‡§≠‡•Ä‡§°‡§º ‡§¨‡•Ç‡§• ‡§≤‡•Ç‡§ü‡§®‡•á ‡§Ü ‡§∞‡§π‡•Ä ‡§π‡•à‡•§ ‡§™‡•ã‡§≤‡§ø‡§Ç‡§ó ‡§è‡§ú‡•á‡§Ç‡§ü ‡§≠‡§æ‡§ó ‡§ó‡§è ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç‡•§ ‡§Ü‡§™ ‡§Ö‡§ï‡•á‡§≤‡•á ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç‡•§ ‡§ï‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ ‡§ï‡§∞‡•á‡§Ç‡§ó‡•á?"*
* *(Hint: Secure the EVM first (it has votes). Lock the room. Call paramilitary. Life > Machine, but Duty > Fear.)*

**Type C: Resource Crisis**
4.  *"Oxygen Cylinder ‡§ñ‡§§‡•ç‡§Æ ‡§π‡•ã ‡§ó‡§è ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç (Covid scenario), ‡§î‡§∞ 2 ‡§Æ‡§∞‡•Ä‡§ú critical ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç‚Äî‡§è‡§ï 80 ‡§∏‡§æ‡§≤ ‡§ï‡§æ ‡§¨‡•Å‡§ú‡•Å‡§∞‡•ç‡§ó ‡§î‡§∞ ‡§è‡§ï 10 ‡§∏‡§æ‡§≤ ‡§ï‡§æ ‡§¨‡§ö‡•ç‡§ö‡§æ‡•§ ‡§Ü‡§™ ‡§ï‡§ø‡§∏‡•á ‡§¨‡§ö‡§æ‡§è‡§Ç‡§ó‡•á?"*
* *(Hint: Medical Ethics says 'Save who has better chance of survival'. Let the Doctor decide clinically, not you emotionally.)*

---

### **4. How to Prepare (The Perfect Way: SOP Charts)**

‡§¶‡§ø‡§Æ‡§æ‡§ó ‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç ‡§™‡§π‡§≤‡•á ‡§∏‡•á "Flowchart" ‡§¨‡§®‡§æ ‡§π‡•ã‡§®‡§æ ‡§ö‡§æ‡§π‡§ø‡§è‡•§

#### **Drill 1: The "If-Then" Table**

* **Task:** ‡§è‡§ï ‡§ö‡§æ‡§∞‡•ç‡§ü ‡§™‡•á‡§™‡§∞ ‡§≤‡•á‡§Ç‡•§ ‡§â‡§∏ ‡§™‡§∞ ‡§≤‡§ø‡§ñ‡•á‡§Ç:
* **Crisis:** Fire / Flood / Riot / Earthquake.
* **Action 1 (Immediate):** (e.g., Fire Brigade / Evacuation).
* **Action 2 (Authority):** (e.g., Call NDRF / Call SP).
* **Action 3 (Post-Crisis):** (e.g., Compensation / Inquiry).


* **Benefit:** ‡§ú‡§¨ Board ‡§∏‡§µ‡§æ‡§≤ ‡§™‡•Ç‡§õ‡•á‡§ó‡§æ, ‡§Ü‡§™‡§ï‡§æ ‡§¶‡§ø‡§Æ‡§æ‡§ó "Search" ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç ‡§ï‡§∞‡•á‡§ó‡§æ, ‡§∏‡•Ä‡§ß‡§æ "Execute" ‡§ï‡§∞‡•á‡§ó‡§æ‡•§

#### **Drill 2: The "Visualization" (‡§Ü‡§Ç‡§ñ‡•á‡§Ç ‡§¨‡§Ç‡§¶ ‡§ï‡§∞‡§ï‡•á)**

* **Task:** ‡§∏‡•ã‡§®‡•á ‡§∏‡•á ‡§™‡§π‡§≤‡•á 5 ‡§Æ‡§ø‡§®‡§ü imagine ‡§ï‡§∞‡•á‡§Ç ‡§ï‡§ø ‡§Ü‡§™ ‡§ï‡•Å‡§∞‡•ç‡§∏‡•Ä ‡§™‡§∞ ‡§¨‡•à‡§†‡•á ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç ‡§î‡§∞ ‡§´‡•ã‡§® ‡§¨‡§ú‡§§‡§æ ‡§π‡•à‚Äî *"‡§∏‡§∞, ‡§¶‡§Ç‡§ó‡§æ ‡§π‡•ã ‡§ó‡§Ø‡§æ‡•§"*
* **Action:** ‡§Æ‡§® ‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç ‡§™‡•Ç‡§∞‡§æ ‡§™‡•ç‡§∞‡•ã‡§∏‡•á‡§∏ ‡§ö‡§≤‡§æ‡§è‡§Ç‡•§ ‡§ó‡§æ‡§°‡§º‡•Ä ‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç ‡§¨‡•à‡§†‡§®‡§æ -> ‡§Æ‡•å‡§ï‡•á ‡§™‡§∞ ‡§™‡§π‡•Å‡§Ç‡§ö‡§®‡§æ -> ‡§Æ‡§æ‡§á‡§ï ‡§•‡§æ‡§Æ‡§®‡§æ -> ‡§Ü‡§∞‡•ç‡§°‡§∞ ‡§¶‡•á‡§®‡§æ‡•§
* **Goal:** ‡§°‡§∞ (Anxiety) ‡§ï‡•ã ‡§ñ‡§§‡•ç‡§Æ ‡§ï‡§∞‡§®‡§æ‡•§

---

### **5. Neuro-Interrogation (Think Deeply)**

1. **Hero Syndrome:** *"‡§ï‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ ‡§Æ‡•Å‡§ù‡•á ‡§≤‡§ó‡§§‡§æ ‡§π‡•à ‡§ï‡§ø ‡§Æ‡•à‡§Ç ‡§Ö‡§ï‡•á‡§≤‡§æ ‡§∏‡§¨ ‡§†‡•Ä‡§ï ‡§ï‡§∞ ‡§¶‡•Ç‡§Ç‡§ó‡§æ?"*
* (‡§ó‡§≤‡§§‡•§ DM "Team Leader" ‡§π‡•ã‡§§‡§æ ‡§π‡•à‡•§ "‡§Æ‡•à‡§Ç ‡§ï‡§∞‡•Ç‡§Å‡§ó‡§æ" ‡§ï‡•Ä ‡§ú‡§ó‡§π "‡§Æ‡•à‡§Ç ‡§ü‡•Ä‡§Æ ‡§ï‡•ã ‡§®‡§ø‡§∞‡•ç‡§¶‡•á‡§∂ ‡§¶‡•Ç‡§Ç‡§ó‡§æ" (I will direct the team) ‡§¨‡•ã‡§≤‡•á‡§Ç‡•§)


2. **Panic Trigger:** *"‡§Ö‡§ó‡§∞ Board ‡§Æ‡•Å‡§ù ‡§™‡§∞ ‡§ö‡§ø‡§≤‡•ç‡§≤‡§æ‡§è ‡§ï‡§ø '‡§§‡•Å‡§Æ‡§®‡•á 10 ‡§≤‡•ã‡§ó ‡§Æ‡§æ‡§∞ ‡§¶‡§ø‡§è', ‡§§‡•ã ‡§ï‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ ‡§Æ‡•à‡§Ç ‡§°‡§ø‡§´‡•á‡§Ç‡§∏‡§ø‡§µ ‡§π‡•ã ‡§ú‡§æ‡§ä‡§Ç‡§ó‡§æ?"*
* (Board Pressure ‡§¨‡§®‡§æ‡§è‡§ó‡§æ‡•§ ‡§Ü‡§™‡§ï‡•ã ‡§∂‡§æ‡§Ç‡§§ ‡§∞‡§π‡§ï‡§∞ ‡§ï‡§π‡§®‡§æ ‡§π‡•à: *"Sir, decision was taken based on situational necessity to save more lives."*)



---

### **6. Overall Effect on Interview**

‡§ú‡§¨ ‡§Ü‡§™ SOP-based answers ‡§¶‡•á‡§§‡•á ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç:

1. **Leadership:** Board ‡§ï‡•ã ‡§¶‡§ø‡§ñ‡§§‡§æ ‡§π‡•à‚Äî *"‡§Ø‡§π ‡§¨‡§ö‡•ç‡§ö‡§æ ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç, ‡§Ø‡§π ‡§ï‡§Æ‡§æ‡§Ç‡§°‡§∞ ‡§π‡•à‡•§"*
2. **Safety:** ‡§â‡§®‡•ç‡§π‡•á‡§Ç ‡§≠‡§∞‡•ã‡§∏‡§æ ‡§π‡•ã‡§§‡§æ ‡§π‡•à ‡§ï‡§ø ‡§Ü‡§™ ‡§ú‡§ø‡§≤‡•á ‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç ‡§Ü‡§ó ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç ‡§≤‡§ó‡§æ‡§è‡§Ç‡§ó‡•á, ‡§¨‡§≤‡•ç‡§ï‡§ø ‡§Ü‡§ó ‡§¨‡•Å‡§ù‡§æ‡§è‡§Ç‡§ó‡•á‡•§
3. **Process Orientation:** ‡§Ü‡§™ ‡§¶‡§ø‡§ñ‡§æ‡§§‡•á ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç ‡§ï‡§ø ‡§Ü‡§™ ‡§∏‡§ø‡§∏‡•ç‡§ü‡§Æ (System) ‡§î‡§∞ ‡§ï‡§æ‡§®‡•Ç‡§® (Law) ‡§™‡§∞ ‡§ö‡§≤‡§§‡•á ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç, ‡§á‡§Æ‡•ã‡§∂‡§Ç‡§∏ ‡§™‡§∞ ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç‡•§

---

### **Today's Action Plan (‡§Ü‡§ú ‡§ï‡§æ ‡§π‡•ã‡§Æ‡§µ‡§∞‡•ç‡§ï)**

1. **Draft:** **Scenario 1 (Communal Riot)** ‡§ï‡§æ ‡§ú‡§µ‡§æ‡§¨ ‡§≤‡§ø‡§ñ‡•á‡§Ç‡•§ ‡§â‡§∏‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç **Section 144** ‡§î‡§∞ **Peace Committee** ‡§ú‡•à‡§∏‡•á ‡§∂‡§¨‡•ç‡§¶ ‡§ú‡§∞‡•Ç‡§∞ ‡§á‡§∏‡•ç‡§§‡•á‡§Æ‡§æ‡§≤ ‡§ï‡§∞‡•á‡§Ç‡•§
2. **Record:** ‡§Ö‡§™‡§®‡•á ‡§¶‡•ã‡§∏‡•ç‡§§ ‡§∏‡•á ‡§ï‡§π‡•á‡§Ç ‡§ï‡§ø ‡§µ‡•ã "Hospital Negligence" ‡§µ‡§æ‡§≤‡§æ ‡§∏‡§µ‡§æ‡§≤ ‡§™‡•Ç‡§õ‡•á ‡§î‡§∞ ‡§Ü‡§™ ‡§™‡§∞ ‡§ö‡§ø‡§≤‡•ç‡§≤‡§æ‡§è‡•§ ‡§Ü‡§™ ‡§∂‡§æ‡§Ç‡§§ ‡§∞‡§π‡§ï‡§∞ ‡§ú‡§µ‡§æ‡§¨ ‡§¶‡•á‡§Ç‡•§
3. **Read:** **CrPC Section 129, 130, 144** ‡§î‡§∞ **NDMA Guidelines** ‡§ï‡•á ‡§¨‡•á‡§∏‡§ø‡§ï‡•ç‡§∏ ‡§™‡§¢‡§º ‡§≤‡•á‡§Ç‡•§ (‡§∏‡§ø‡§∞‡•ç‡§´ ‡§π‡•á‡§°‡§≤‡§æ‡§á‡§®)‡•§

**Chapter Mantra:**

> *"‡§∏‡§Ç‡§ï‡§ü (Crisis) ‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç ‡§ö‡§∞‡§ø‡§§‡•ç‡§∞ (Character) ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç, '‡§™‡•ç‡§∞‡§∂‡§ø‡§ï‡•ç‡§∑‡§£' (Training) ‡§ï‡§æ‡§Æ ‡§Ü‡§§‡§æ ‡§π‡•à‡•§ ‡§Ö‡§™‡§®‡•á ‡§¶‡§ø‡§Æ‡§æ‡§ó ‡§ï‡•ã 'War Room' ‡§¨‡§®‡§æ ‡§≤‡•ã‡•§"*

---

**Next:** **Chapter 15 (Mock Strategy)** ‚Äî Interview ‡§∏‡•á ‡§™‡§π‡§≤‡•á Mock Test ‡§ï‡•à‡§∏‡•á ‡§¶‡•á‡§®‡•á ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç? (‡§§‡§æ‡§ï‡§ø Mock ‡§Ü‡§™‡§ï‡•á Confidence ‡§ï‡•ã ‡§§‡•ã‡§°‡§º‡•á ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç, ‡§¨‡§≤‡•ç‡§ï‡§ø ‡§¨‡§®‡§æ‡§è)‡•§






---


## Chapter 15: Mock Strategy (‡§∏‡§∞‡•ç‡§ú‡§∞‡•Ä, ‡§™‡§∞‡§´‡•â‡§∞‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç‡§∏ ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç)
This chapter deals with the most misunderstood part of preparation: **Mock Interviews.**
**Core Concept:** Extracting Signal from Noise (‡§∂‡•ã‡§∞ ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç, ‡§∏‡•Å‡§ß‡§æ‡§∞ ‡§ö‡§æ‡§π‡§ø‡§è).
**The Strategy:** **Mock \rightarrow Deep Analysis \rightarrow Fix Pattern.** (‡§Ö‡§Ç‡§ß‡§æ‡§ß‡•Å‡§Ç‡§ß Mocks ‡§¶‡•á‡§®‡§æ ‡§Æ‡§®‡§æ ‡§π‡•à).

---

### **Namaskar Future Officer.**

Interview ‡§∏‡•á ‡§™‡§π‡§≤‡•á Mocks ‡§¶‡•á‡§®‡§æ ‡§ú‡§∞‡•Ç‡§∞‡•Ä ‡§π‡•à, ‡§≤‡•á‡§ï‡§ø‡§® **"Mocks ‡§ï‡§æ ‡§®‡§∂‡§æ"** ‡§ï‡§∞‡§®‡§æ ‡§ñ‡§§‡§∞‡§®‡§æ‡§ï ‡§π‡•à‡•§
‡§ï‡§à students 10-15 Mocks ‡§¶‡•á ‡§¶‡•á‡§§‡•á ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç‡•§ ‡§π‡§∞ Mock ‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç ‡§â‡§®‡•ç‡§π‡•á‡§Ç ‡§Ö‡§≤‡§ó feedback ‡§Æ‡§ø‡§≤‡§§‡§æ ‡§π‡•à:

* *Mock 1:* "‡§Ü‡§™ ‡§¨‡§π‡•Å‡§§ ‡§ß‡•Ä‡§∞‡•á ‡§¨‡•ã‡§≤‡§§‡•á ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç‡•§"
* *Mock 2:* "‡§Ü‡§™ ‡§¨‡§π‡•Å‡§§ ‡§§‡•á‡§ú ‡§¨‡•ã‡§≤‡§§‡•á ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç‡•§"
* *Mock 3:* "‡§Ü‡§™‡§ï‡§æ content ‡§Ö‡§ö‡•ç‡§õ‡§æ ‡§π‡•à, ‡§≤‡•á‡§ï‡§ø‡§® smile ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç ‡§π‡•à‡•§"

‡§™‡§∞‡§ø‡§£‡§æ‡§Æ? **Confusion.**
Exam ‡§µ‡§æ‡§≤‡•á ‡§¶‡§ø‡§® ‡§µ‡•ã student ‡§è‡§ï "Robot" ‡§¨‡§® ‡§ú‡§æ‡§§‡§æ ‡§π‡•à ‡§ú‡•ã ‡§∏‡§¨‡§ï‡•á suggestions ‡§Ø‡§æ‡§¶ ‡§ï‡§∞‡§®‡•á ‡§ï‡•Ä ‡§ï‡•ã‡§∂‡§ø‡§∂ ‡§ï‡§∞ ‡§∞‡§π‡§æ ‡§π‡•à‡•§

**Golden Rule:**

> *"Mock Interview ‡§ï‡•ã‡§à 'Theater Performance' ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç ‡§π‡•à, ‡§Ø‡§π ‡§è‡§ï 'Surgery' ‡§π‡•à‡•§ ‡§Ö‡§ó‡§∞ ‡§¨‡•Ä‡§Æ‡§æ‡§∞‡•Ä (Weakness) ‡§™‡§ï‡§°‡§º ‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç ‡§Ü ‡§ó‡§à ‡§π‡•à, ‡§§‡•ã ‡§™‡§π‡§≤‡•á ‡§â‡§∏‡§ï‡§æ ‡§á‡§≤‡§æ‡§ú ‡§ï‡§∞‡•ã, ‡§´‡§ø‡§∞ ‡§¶‡•ã‡§¨‡§æ‡§∞‡§æ ‡§ú‡§æ‡§Ç‡§ö ‡§ï‡§∞‡§æ‡§ì‡•§"*

‡§è‡§ï Officer "Quantity" ‡§™‡§∞ ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç, **"Calibration"** (‡§∏‡•Å‡§ß‡§æ‡§∞) ‡§™‡§∞ ‡§µ‡§ø‡§∂‡•ç‡§µ‡§æ‡§∏ ‡§ï‡§∞‡§§‡§æ ‡§π‡•à‡•§

---

### **1. The Core Mechanics: The "One Mock - One Fix" Rule**

‡§Ü‡§™‡§ï‡•ã **3 ‡§∏‡•á 5 Mocks** ‡§∏‡•á ‡§ú‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ‡§¶‡§æ ‡§ï‡•Ä ‡§ú‡§∞‡•Ç‡§∞‡§§ ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç ‡§π‡•à, ‡§¨‡§∂‡§∞‡•ç‡§§‡•á ‡§Ü‡§™ ‡§∏‡§π‡•Ä ‡§§‡§∞‡•Ä‡§ï‡§æ ‡§Ö‡§™‡§®‡§æ‡§è‡§Ç:

1. **Give Mock 1 (Diagnostic):** ‡§¨‡§ø‡§®‡§æ ‡§ú‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ‡§¶‡§æ ‡§§‡•à‡§Ø‡§æ‡§∞‡•Ä ‡§ï‡•á ‡§¶‡•á‡§Ç‡•§ ‡§Ö‡§™‡§®‡•Ä "Natural State" ‡§ö‡•á‡§ï ‡§ï‡§∞‡•á‡§Ç‡•§
2. **The Deep Analysis (Surgery):** ‡§Ö‡§™‡§®‡•á Mock ‡§ï‡§æ ‡§µ‡•Ä‡§°‡§ø‡§Ø‡•ã ‡§ñ‡•Å‡§¶ ‡§¶‡•á‡§ñ‡•á‡§Ç‡•§ (Marks ‡§Æ‡§§ ‡§¶‡•á‡§ñ‡•á‡§Ç, Video ‡§¶‡•á‡§ñ‡•á‡§Ç)‡•§
3. **Identify Pattern:** ‡§Ö‡§™‡§®‡•Ä **"Top 3 Killers"** (‡§∏‡§¨‡§∏‡•á ‡§¨‡§°‡§º‡•Ä ‡§ï‡§Æ‡§ø‡§Ø‡§æ‡§Ç) ‡§®‡•ã‡§ü ‡§ï‡§∞‡•á‡§Ç‡•§
4. **The Fix:** ‡§Ö‡§ó‡§≤‡•á 3 ‡§¶‡§ø‡§® ‡§∏‡§ø‡§∞‡•ç‡§´ ‡§â‡§® ‡§ï‡§Æ‡§ø‡§Ø‡•ã‡§Ç ‡§ï‡•ã ‡§¶‡•Ç‡§∞ ‡§ï‡§∞‡§®‡•á ‡§ï‡•Ä practice ‡§ï‡§∞‡•á‡§Ç (Mirror work)‡•§
5. **Give Mock 2 (Test):** ‡§Ø‡§π ‡§ö‡•á‡§ï ‡§ï‡§∞‡§®‡•á ‡§ï‡•á ‡§≤‡§ø‡§è ‡§ï‡§ø ‡§ï‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ ‡§µ‡•ã 3 ‡§ï‡§Æ‡§ø‡§Ø‡§æ‡§Ç ‡§†‡•Ä‡§ï ‡§π‡•Å‡§à‡§Ç?

---

### **2. The 5 Examples: Common "Red Flags" in Mocks**

Mocks ‡§ï‡§æ ‡§Ö‡§∏‡§≤‡•Ä ‡§Æ‡§ï‡§∏‡§¶ ‡§á‡§® "Red Flags" (‡§ñ‡§§‡§∞‡•á ‡§ï‡•Ä ‡§ò‡§Ç‡§ü‡§ø‡§Ø‡§æ‡§Ç) ‡§ï‡•ã ‡§™‡§ï‡§°‡§º‡§®‡§æ ‡§π‡•à‡•§ ‡§¶‡•á‡§ñ‡§ø‡§è ‡§ï‡§ø video analysis ‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç ‡§ï‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ ‡§¢‡•Ç‡§Å‡§¢‡§®‡§æ ‡§π‡•à:

#### **Red Flag 1: The "Nodding Head" (‡§ú‡•Ä ‡§π‡§ú‡•Ç‡§∞‡•Ä)**

* **Problem:** Board Member ‡§∏‡§µ‡§æ‡§≤ ‡§™‡•Ç‡§õ ‡§∞‡§π‡•á ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç ‡§î‡§∞ ‡§Ü‡§™ ‡§≤‡§ó‡§æ‡§§‡§æ‡§∞ ‡§∏‡§ø‡§∞ ‡§π‡§ø‡§≤‡§æ ‡§∞‡§π‡•á ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç (Bobblehead doll ‡§ï‡•Ä ‡§§‡§∞‡§π)‡•§
* **Diagnosis:** ‡§Ø‡§π "Submissiveness" (‡§¶‡§¨‡•ç‡§¨‡•Ç‡§™‡§®) ‡§î‡§∞ "Confidence ‡§ï‡•Ä ‡§ï‡§Æ‡•Ä" ‡§¶‡§ø‡§ñ‡§æ‡§§‡§æ ‡§π‡•à‡•§
* **The Fix:** ‡§∂‡•Ä‡§∂‡•á ‡§ï‡•á ‡§∏‡§æ‡§Æ‡§®‡•á practice ‡§ï‡§∞‡•á‡§Ç‚Äî‡§∏‡§ø‡§∞ ‡§ï‡•ã ‡§∏‡•ç‡§•‡§ø‡§∞ (Steady) ‡§∞‡§ñ‡•á‡§Ç‡•§ ‡§∏‡§ø‡§∞‡•ç‡§´ ‡§ú‡§∞‡•Ç‡§∞‡•Ä ‡§¨‡§æ‡§§ ‡§™‡§∞ ‡§è‡§ï ‡§¨‡§æ‡§∞ ‡§∏‡§ø‡§∞ ‡§π‡§ø‡§≤‡§æ‡§è‡§Ç‡•§

#### **Red Flag 2: The "Hand Chopper" (‡§π‡§æ‡§•‡•ã‡§Ç ‡§ï‡§æ ‡§ú‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ‡§¶‡§æ ‡§™‡•ç‡§∞‡§Ø‡•ã‡§ó)**

* **Problem:** ‡§¨‡§æ‡§§ ‡§ï‡§∞‡§§‡•á ‡§µ‡§ï‡•ç‡§§ ‡§π‡§æ‡§• ‡§π‡§µ‡§æ ‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç ‡§â‡§°‡§º ‡§∞‡§π‡•á ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç, ‡§ú‡•à‡§∏‡•á ‡§Ü‡§™ ‡§ü‡•ç‡§∞‡•à‡§´‡§ø‡§ï ‡§ï‡§Ç‡§ü‡•ç‡§∞‡•ã‡§≤ ‡§ï‡§∞ ‡§∞‡§π‡•á ‡§π‡•ã‡§Ç‡•§
* **Diagnosis:** ‡§Ø‡§π "Nervousness" ‡§î‡§∞ "Aggression" ‡§¶‡§ø‡§ñ‡§æ‡§§‡§æ ‡§π‡•à‡•§
* **The Fix:** **"Steeple Hand"** ‡§Ø‡§æ ‡§ó‡•ã‡§¶ ‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç ‡§π‡§æ‡§• ‡§≤‡•â‡§ï ‡§ï‡§∞‡§®‡•á ‡§ï‡•Ä practice ‡§ï‡§∞‡•á‡§Ç‡•§

#### **Red Flag 3: The "Ummm... Aaa..." (Fillers)**

* **Problem:** ‡§π‡§∞ ‡§¶‡•Ç‡§∏‡§∞‡•á ‡§∂‡§¨‡•ç‡§¶ ‡§ï‡•á ‡§¨‡§æ‡§¶ "‡§Ö... ‡§Æ‡§§‡§≤‡§¨... ‡§µ‡•ã..." ‡§¨‡•ã‡§≤‡§®‡§æ‡•§
* **Diagnosis:** ‡§á‡§∏‡§ï‡§æ ‡§Æ‡§§‡§≤‡§¨ ‡§π‡•à ‡§ï‡§ø ‡§Ü‡§™ ‡§∏‡•ã‡§ö (Think) ‡§î‡§∞ ‡§¨‡•ã‡§≤ (Speak) ‡§∏‡§æ‡§•-‡§∏‡§æ‡§• ‡§∞‡§π‡•á ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç‡•§ Processing slow ‡§π‡•à‡•§
* **The Fix:** **"The Pause Technique."** ‡§¨‡•ã‡§≤‡§®‡•á ‡§∏‡•á ‡§™‡§π‡§≤‡•á 2 ‡§∏‡•á‡§ï‡§Ç‡§° ‡§∞‡•Å‡§ï‡•á‡§Ç‡•§ ‡§∂‡§æ‡§Ç‡§§ ‡§∞‡§π‡§®‡§æ "‡§Ö..." ‡§¨‡•ã‡§≤‡§®‡•á ‡§∏‡•á ‡§¨‡•á‡§π‡§§‡§∞ ‡§π‡•à‡•§

#### **Red Flag 4: The "Defense Lawyer" (‡§¨‡§π‡§∏ ‡§ï‡§∞‡§®‡§æ)**

* **Problem:** ‡§ú‡§¨ Panelist ‡§®‡•á ‡§ï‡§π‡§æ "You are wrong", ‡§§‡•ã ‡§Ü‡§™‡§®‡•á ‡§§‡•Å‡§∞‡§Ç‡§§ ‡§ï‡§π‡§æ "No Sir, actually..."‡•§
* **Diagnosis:** ‡§Ü‡§™ Feedback ‡§Ø‡§æ Criticism ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç ‡§≤‡•á ‡§∏‡§ï‡§§‡•á‡•§ (Ego issue).
* **The Fix:** **"Poker Face."** ‡§Ü‡§≤‡•ã‡§ö‡§®‡§æ ‡§™‡§∞ ‡§Æ‡•Å‡§∏‡•ç‡§ï‡•Å‡§∞‡§æ‡§®‡§æ ‡§∏‡•Ä‡§ñ‡•á‡§Ç‡•§ "Thank you Sir, I will recheck this."

#### **Red Flag 5: The "Plastic Smile" (‡§´‡§∞‡•ç‡§ú‡•Ä ‡§π‡§Ç‡§∏‡•Ä)**

* **Problem:** ‡§™‡•Ç‡§∞‡•á 20 ‡§Æ‡§ø‡§®‡§ü ‡§ö‡•á‡§π‡§∞‡•á ‡§™‡§∞ ‡§è‡§ï ‡§ö‡§ø‡§™‡§ï‡•Ä ‡§π‡•Å‡§à ‡§Æ‡•Å‡§∏‡•ç‡§ï‡§æ‡§® ‡§∞‡§ñ‡§®‡§æ, ‡§ö‡§æ‡§π‡•á ‡§∏‡§µ‡§æ‡§≤ ‡§∏‡•Ä‡§∞‡§ø‡§Ø‡§∏ ‡§π‡•Ä ‡§ï‡•ç‡§Ø‡•ã‡§Ç ‡§® ‡§π‡•ã‡•§
* **Diagnosis:** ‡§Ø‡§π ‡§Ü‡§™‡§ï‡•ã "Fake" ‡§î‡§∞ "Insensitive" ‡§¶‡§ø‡§ñ‡§æ‡§§‡§æ ‡§π‡•à‡•§ (e.g., ‡§ó‡§∞‡•Ä‡§¨‡•Ä ‡§™‡§∞ ‡§¨‡§æ‡§§ ‡§ï‡§∞‡§§‡•á ‡§µ‡§ï‡•ç‡§§ ‡§≠‡•Ä ‡§∏‡•ç‡§Æ‡§æ‡§á‡§≤)‡•§
* **The Fix:** **"Expression Matching."** ‡§ü‡•â‡§™‡§ø‡§ï ‡§ï‡•á ‡§π‡§ø‡§∏‡§æ‡§¨ ‡§∏‡•á ‡§ö‡•á‡§π‡§∞‡§æ ‡§¨‡§¶‡§≤‡•á‡§Ç‡•§ ‡§∏‡•Ä‡§∞‡§ø‡§Ø‡§∏ ‡§¨‡§æ‡§§ ‡§™‡§∞ ‡§∏‡•Ä‡§∞‡§ø‡§Ø‡§∏, ‡§π‡§≤‡•ç‡§ï‡•Ä ‡§¨‡§æ‡§§ ‡§™‡§∞ ‡§∏‡•ç‡§Æ‡§æ‡§á‡§≤‡•§

---

### **3. Strategic Questions to Ask Yourself (After Mock)**

Mock ‡§¶‡•á‡§®‡•á ‡§ï‡•á ‡§¨‡§æ‡§¶ Panelist ‡§∏‡•á ‡§™‡•Ç‡§õ‡§®‡•á ‡§∏‡•á ‡§™‡§π‡§≤‡•á, **‡§ñ‡•Å‡§¶ ‡§∏‡•á** ‡§Ø‡•á ‡§∏‡§µ‡§æ‡§≤ ‡§™‡•Ç‡§õ‡•á‡§Ç:

**Type A: The Energy Audit**

1. *"‡§ï‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ 25‡§µ‡•á‡§Ç ‡§Æ‡§ø‡§®‡§ü ‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç ‡§≠‡•Ä ‡§Æ‡•á‡§∞‡•Ä ‡§Ü‡§µ‡§æ‡§ú‡§º ‡§â‡§§‡§®‡•Ä ‡§π‡•Ä ‡§¨‡•Å‡§≤‡§Ç‡§¶ ‡§•‡•Ä ‡§ú‡§ø‡§§‡§®‡•Ä ‡§™‡§π‡§≤‡•á ‡§Æ‡§ø‡§®‡§ü ‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç?"*
* (‡§Ö‡§ó‡§∞ ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç, ‡§§‡•ã Stamina ‡§¨‡§¢‡§º‡§æ‡§è‡§Ç‡•§ ‡§•‡§ï‡§æ ‡§π‡•Å‡§Ü Officer ‡§ó‡§≤‡§§ ‡§´‡•à‡§∏‡§≤‡•á ‡§≤‡•á‡§§‡§æ ‡§π‡•à‡•§)



**Type B: The Listening Audit**
2.  *"‡§ï‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ ‡§Æ‡•à‡§Ç‡§®‡•á ‡§ï‡•ã‡§à ‡§∏‡§µ‡§æ‡§≤ ‡§¨‡•Ä‡§ö ‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç ‡§ï‡§æ‡§ü‡§æ (Interrupt ‡§ï‡§ø‡§Ø‡§æ)?"*
* (‡§Ø‡§π ‡§∏‡§¨‡§∏‡•á ‡§¨‡§°‡§º‡§æ ‡§™‡§æ‡§™ ‡§π‡•à‡•§ ‡§µ‡•Ä‡§°‡§ø‡§Ø‡•ã ‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç ‡§ö‡•á‡§ï ‡§ï‡§∞‡•á‡§Ç‡•§)

**Type C: The Content Audit**
3.  *"‡§Æ‡•à‡§Ç‡§®‡•á ‡§ï‡§ø‡§§‡§®‡•Ä ‡§¨‡§æ‡§∞ 'Bihar' ‡§Ø‡§æ ‡§Ö‡§™‡§®‡•á 'District' ‡§ï‡§æ ‡§®‡§æ‡§Æ ‡§≤‡§ø‡§Ø‡§æ?"*
* (‡§Ö‡§ó‡§∞ ‡§™‡•Ç‡§∞‡•á ‡§á‡§Ç‡§ü‡§∞‡§µ‡•ç‡§Ø‡•Ç ‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç ‡§è‡§ï ‡§¨‡§æ‡§∞ ‡§≠‡•Ä local example ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç ‡§¶‡§ø‡§Ø‡§æ, ‡§§‡•ã ‡§Ü‡§™ ‡§´‡•á‡§≤ ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç‡•§ Chapter 6 ‡§¶‡•á‡§ñ‡•á‡§Ç‡•§)

---

### **4. How to Prepare (The Perfect Way: The Surgery)**

Mock Institute ‡§ú‡§æ‡§ï‡§∞ ‡§¨‡§∏ "‡§¨‡•à‡§†‡§ï‡§∞" ‡§® ‡§Ü‡§è‡§Ç‡•§ ‡§â‡§∏‡•á ‡§ï‡§Ç‡§ü‡•ç‡§∞‡•ã‡§≤ ‡§ï‡§∞‡•á‡§Ç‡•§

#### **Drill 1: The "Specific Demand" (Panel ‡§ï‡•ã ‡§¨‡§§‡§æ‡§è‡§Ç)**

* **Task:** Mock ‡§∂‡•Å‡§∞‡•Ç ‡§π‡•ã‡§®‡•á ‡§∏‡•á ‡§™‡§π‡§≤‡•á ‡§π‡•Ä (‡§Ø‡§æ ‡§´‡•â‡§∞‡•ç‡§Æ ‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç) ‡§≤‡§ø‡§ñ‡•á‡§Ç:
* *"Sir, I am working on my Eye Contact and Stress Management. Please test me specifically on these."*


* **Benefit:** Panel ‡§´‡§æ‡§≤‡§§‡•Ç ‡§∏‡§µ‡§æ‡§≤ ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç ‡§™‡•Ç‡§õ‡•á‡§ó‡§æ, ‡§µ‡•ã ‡§Ü‡§™‡§ï‡•Ä ‡§ï‡§Æ‡§ú‡•ã‡§∞‡•Ä (Weakness) ‡§™‡§∞ ‡§µ‡§æ‡§∞ ‡§ï‡§∞‡•á‡§ó‡§æ‡•§ ‡§Ø‡§π‡•Ä ‡§Ö‡§∏‡§≤‡•Ä ‡§™‡•ç‡§∞‡•à‡§ï‡•ç‡§ü‡§ø‡§∏ ‡§π‡•à‡•§

#### **Drill 2: The "Video Post-Mortem"**

* **Task:** Mock ‡§ï‡§æ ‡§µ‡•Ä‡§°‡§ø‡§Ø‡•ã ‡§ò‡§∞ ‡§≤‡§æ‡§è‡§Ç‡•§
* **Action:**
1. **Mute ‡§ï‡§∞‡§ï‡•á ‡§¶‡•á‡§ñ‡•á‡§Ç:** ‡§∏‡§ø‡§∞‡•ç‡§´ Body Language ‡§ö‡•á‡§ï ‡§ï‡§∞‡•á‡§Ç (‡§π‡§æ‡§•, ‡§™‡•à‡§∞, ‡§Ü‡§Ç‡§ñ‡•á‡§Ç)‡•§
2. **Audio Only:** ‡§Ü‡§Ç‡§ñ‡•á‡§Ç ‡§¨‡§Ç‡§¶ ‡§ï‡§∞‡§ï‡•á ‡§∏‡•Å‡§®‡•á‡§Ç‡•§ ‡§ï‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ ‡§Ü‡§µ‡§æ‡§ú‡§º ‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç ‡§°‡§∞ (Shakiness) ‡§π‡•à?
3. **Content:** ‡§ï‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ ‡§Ü‡§™‡§ï‡•á ‡§ú‡§µ‡§æ‡§¨ "Level 1, 2, 3" framework (Chapter 4) ‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç ‡§•‡•á?



#### **Drill 3: The "Red Flag Checklist"**

* **Task:** ‡§è‡§ï ‡§°‡§æ‡§Ø‡§∞‡•Ä ‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç 3 ‡§ï‡•â‡§≤‡§Æ ‡§¨‡§®‡§æ‡§è‡§Ç:
* **Mistake:** (e.g., Looking down while thinking).
* **Trigger:** (e.g., When I don't know the answer).
* **Correction:** (e.g., Look straight and say "Sorry").


* **Goal:** ‡§Ö‡§ó‡§≤‡•á Mock ‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç ‡§ú‡§æ‡§®‡•á ‡§∏‡•á ‡§™‡§π‡§≤‡•á ‡§á‡§∏ ‡§≤‡§ø‡§∏‡•ç‡§ü ‡§ï‡•ã ‡§™‡§¢‡§º‡•á‡§Ç‡•§ ‡§ó‡§≤‡§§‡•Ä ‡§¶‡•ã‡§π‡§∞‡§æ‡§®‡§æ ‡§Æ‡§®‡§æ ‡§π‡•à‡•§

---

### **5. Neuro-Interrogation (Self-Reflection)**

1. **Feedback Filter:** *"‡§Ö‡§ó‡§∞ ‡§è‡§ï ‡§™‡•à‡§®‡§≤‡§ø‡§∏‡•ç‡§ü ‡§®‡•á ‡§ï‡§π‡§æ 'Aggressive ‡§π‡•ã' ‡§î‡§∞ ‡§¶‡•Ç‡§∏‡§∞‡•á ‡§®‡•á ‡§ï‡§π‡§æ 'Confident ‡§π‡•ã', ‡§§‡•ã ‡§Æ‡•à‡§Ç ‡§ï‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ ‡§Æ‡§æ‡§®‡•Ç‡§Å?"*
* (‡§ñ‡•Å‡§¶ ‡§µ‡•Ä‡§°‡§ø‡§Ø‡•ã ‡§¶‡•á‡§ñ‡•á‡§Ç‡•§ Panelist ‡§ï‡§æ ‡§Æ‡•Ç‡§° ‡§Ö‡§≤‡§ó ‡§π‡•ã ‡§∏‡§ï‡§§‡§æ ‡§π‡•à, ‡§ï‡•à‡§Æ‡§∞‡§æ ‡§ù‡•Ç‡§† ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç ‡§¨‡•ã‡§≤‡§§‡§æ‡•§)


2. **Score Trap:** *"‡§Æ‡•Å‡§ù‡•á Mock ‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç 60/100 ‡§Æ‡§ø‡§≤‡•á‡•§ ‡§ï‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ ‡§Æ‡•à‡§Ç ‡§¨‡§∞‡•ç‡§¨‡§æ‡§¶ ‡§π‡•Ç‡§Å?"*
* (Mock ‡§ï‡•á ‡§Æ‡§æ‡§∞‡•ç‡§ï‡•ç‡§∏ ‡§ï‡§ö‡§∞‡§æ ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç‡•§ ‡§â‡§®‡•ç‡§π‡•á‡§Ç ‡§á‡§ó‡•ç‡§®‡•ã‡§∞ ‡§ï‡§∞‡•á‡§Ç‡•§ ‡§Ö‡§∏‡§≤‡•Ä ‡§ï‡§Æ‡§æ‡§à ‡§µ‡•ã "‡§∏‡•Å‡§ß‡§æ‡§∞" (Improvement) ‡§π‡•à ‡§ú‡•ã ‡§Ü‡§™‡§®‡•á ‡§ï‡§ø‡§Ø‡§æ‡•§)



---

### **6. Overall Effect on Interview**

‡§ú‡§¨ ‡§Ü‡§™ Mocks ‡§ï‡•ã "Surgery" ‡§ï‡•Ä ‡§§‡§∞‡§π ‡§á‡§∏‡•ç‡§§‡•á‡§Æ‡§æ‡§≤ ‡§ï‡§∞‡§§‡•á ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç:

1. **Precision:** ‡§Ü‡§™ Exam ‡§µ‡§æ‡§≤‡•á ‡§¶‡§ø‡§® "Experiment" ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç ‡§ï‡§∞‡§§‡•á, ‡§Ü‡§™ "Execute" ‡§ï‡§∞‡§§‡•á ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç‡•§
2. **Self-Awareness:** ‡§Ü‡§™‡§ï‡•ã ‡§Ö‡§™‡§®‡•Ä ‡§ï‡§Æ‡§ø‡§Ø‡§æ‡§Ç ‡§™‡§§‡§æ ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç, ‡§§‡•ã ‡§Ü‡§™ ‡§â‡§®‡•ç‡§π‡•á‡§Ç ‡§õ‡§ø‡§™‡§æ‡§®‡§æ (Manage) ‡§∏‡•Ä‡§ñ ‡§ú‡§æ‡§§‡•á ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç‡•§
3. **Peak Performance:** ‡§Ü‡§™‡§®‡•á ‡§Ö‡§™‡§®‡•Ä ‡§ó‡§≤‡§§‡§ø‡§Ø‡§æ‡§Ç Mocks ‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç ‡§π‡•Ä ‡§ñ‡§§‡•ç‡§Æ ‡§ï‡§∞ ‡§¶‡•Ä ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç‡•§ ‡§Ö‡§¨ "Final Match" ‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç ‡§∏‡§ø‡§∞‡•ç‡§´ ‡§ö‡•å‡§ï‡•á-‡§õ‡§ï‡•ç‡§ï‡•á ‡§≤‡§ó‡•á‡§Ç‡§ó‡•á‡•§

---

### **Today's Action Plan (‡§Ü‡§ú ‡§ï‡§æ ‡§π‡•ã‡§Æ‡§µ‡§∞‡•ç‡§ï)**

1. **Book:** ‡§Ö‡§™‡§®‡§æ ‡§™‡§π‡§≤‡§æ Mock Interview ‡§¨‡•Å‡§ï ‡§ï‡§∞‡•á‡§Ç (Online/Offline)‡•§
2. **Prepare:** ‡§ú‡§æ‡§®‡•á ‡§∏‡•á ‡§™‡§π‡§≤‡•á Chapter 1 ‡§∏‡•á 14 ‡§§‡§ï ‡§ï‡•á ‡§Ö‡§™‡§®‡•á ‡§®‡•ã‡§ü‡•ç‡§∏ ‡§ï‡•ã Revise ‡§ï‡§∞‡•á‡§Ç‡•§
3. **Mindset:** ‡§ñ‡•Å‡§¶ ‡§∏‡•á ‡§ï‡§π‡•á‡§Ç: *"‡§Æ‡•à‡§Ç ‡§µ‡§π‡§æ‡§Ç ‡§ú‡§ú ‡§π‡•ã‡§®‡•á ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç ‡§ú‡§æ ‡§∞‡§π‡§æ, ‡§Æ‡•à‡§Ç ‡§Ö‡§™‡§®‡•Ä ‡§ï‡§Æ‡§ø‡§Ø‡§æ‡§Ç ‡§¢‡•Ç‡§Ç‡§¢‡§®‡•á ‡§ú‡§æ ‡§∞‡§π‡§æ ‡§π‡•Ç‡§Å‡•§"*

**Chapter Mantra:**

> *"Mock Interview ‡§è‡§ï 'Net Practice' ‡§π‡•à‡•§ ‡§Ø‡§π‡§æ‡§Å 'Out' ‡§π‡•ã‡§®‡•á ‡§∏‡•á ‡§Æ‡§§ ‡§°‡§∞‡•ã, ‡§¨‡§∏ ‡§Ø‡§π ‡§¶‡•á‡§ñ‡•ã ‡§ï‡§ø 'Shot' ‡§ó‡§≤‡§§ ‡§ï‡•ç‡§Ø‡•ã‡§Ç ‡§≤‡§ó‡§æ‡•§"*

---

**Next:** **Chapter 16 (The Final 7-Day Conditioning)** ‚Äî ‡§Ö‡§¨ ‡§Ü‡§ñ‡§ø‡§∞‡•Ä ‡§π‡§´‡•ç‡§§‡§æ‡•§ ‡§™‡§¢‡§º‡§æ‡§à ‡§¨‡§Ç‡§¶, ‡§Æ‡§æ‡§á‡§Ç‡§°‡§∏‡•á‡§ü ‡§ö‡§æ‡§≤‡•Ç‡•§ (Sleep, Diet, Dress, and the Winner's Vibe).








## Chapter 16: The Final 7-Day Conditioning (Officer Mindset)
This chapter is the **Final Ritual**. This is not about studying; it is about "Becoming."
**Core Focus:** Visualizing the Win (‡§ú‡•Ä‡§§ ‡§ï‡•Ä ‡§§‡•à‡§Ø‡§æ‡§∞‡•Ä).
**The Rituals:** Sleep, Diet, Dress, and the "Entry Protocol."
**The Mantra:** *"I am not here to pass. I am here to lead."* (‡§Æ‡•à‡§Ç ‡§Ø‡§π‡§æ‡§Ç ‡§™‡§æ‡§∏ ‡§π‡•ã‡§®‡•á ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç, ‡§≤‡•Ä‡§° ‡§ï‡§∞‡§®‡•á ‡§Ü‡§Ø‡§æ ‡§π‡•Ç‡§Å‡•§)

---

### **Namaskar Future Officer.**

‡§Ø‡•á ‡§Ü‡§ñ‡§ø‡§∞‡•Ä ‡§™‡§°‡§º‡§æ‡§µ ‡§π‡•à‡•§
Interview ‡§∏‡•á 7 ‡§¶‡§ø‡§® ‡§™‡§π‡§≤‡•á, ‡§ú‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ‡§¶‡§æ‡§§‡§∞ students ‡§è‡§ï ‡§ó‡§≤‡§§‡•Ä ‡§ï‡§∞‡§§‡•á ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç‚Äî **Panic Reading.**
‡§µ‡•ã ‡§®‡§è ‡§®‡•ã‡§ü‡•ç‡§∏ ‡§™‡§¢‡§º‡§§‡•á ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç, ‡§∞‡§æ‡§§ ‡§≠‡§∞ ‡§ú‡§æ‡§ó‡§§‡•á ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç, ‡§î‡§∞ ‡§Ö‡§ñ‡§¨‡§æ‡§∞ ‡§∞‡§ü‡§§‡•á ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç‡•§
‡§™‡§∞‡§ø‡§£‡§æ‡§Æ? Interview ‡§µ‡§æ‡§≤‡•á ‡§¶‡§ø‡§® ‡§â‡§®‡§ï‡•Ä ‡§Ü‡§Ç‡§ñ‡•ã‡§Ç ‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç ‡§•‡§ï‡§æ‡§® (Fatigue) ‡§î‡§∞ ‡§¶‡§ø‡§Æ‡§æ‡§ó ‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç ‡§ß‡•Å‡§Ç‡§ß (Fog) ‡§π‡•ã‡§§‡•Ä ‡§π‡•à‡•§

Board ‡§ï‡•ã **"Thaka hua Gyani"** ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç ‡§ö‡§æ‡§π‡§ø‡§è‡•§ ‡§â‡§®‡•ç‡§π‡•á‡§Ç **"Energetic Leader"** ‡§ö‡§æ‡§π‡§ø‡§è‡•§
‡§è‡§ï IAS/SDM ‡§ï‡•ã ‡§¶‡§ø‡§® ‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç 15 ‡§ò‡§Ç‡§ü‡•á ‡§ï‡§æ‡§Æ ‡§ï‡§∞‡§®‡§æ ‡§™‡§°‡§º‡§§‡§æ ‡§π‡•à, ‡§î‡§∞ ‡§Ö‡§ó‡§∞ ‡§Ü‡§™ 30 ‡§Æ‡§ø‡§®‡§ü ‡§ï‡•á Interview ‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç ‡§•‡§ï‡•á ‡§π‡•Å‡§è ‡§≤‡§ó‡•á, ‡§§‡•ã ‡§Ü‡§™ ‡§∞‡§ø‡§ú‡•á‡§ï‡•ç‡§ü ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç‡•§

‡§Ø‡§π ‡§π‡§´‡•ç‡§§‡§æ "‡§™‡§¢‡§º‡§®‡•á" ‡§ï‡§æ ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç, **"‡§¢‡§≤‡§®‡•á" (Conditioning)** ‡§ï‡§æ ‡§π‡•à‡•§
‡§ú‡•à‡§∏‡•á ‡§è‡§ï ‡§è‡§•‡§≤‡•Ä‡§ü ‡§´‡§æ‡§á‡§®‡§≤ ‡§Æ‡•à‡§ö ‡§∏‡•á ‡§™‡§π‡§≤‡•á "Tapering" (‡§Ü‡§∞‡§æ‡§Æ ‡§î‡§∞ ‡§´‡•ã‡§ï‡§∏) ‡§ï‡§∞‡§§‡§æ ‡§π‡•à, ‡§µ‡•à‡§∏‡•á ‡§π‡•Ä ‡§Ü‡§™‡§ï‡•ã ‡§Ö‡§¨ ‡§Ö‡§™‡§®‡•á ‡§¶‡§ø‡§Æ‡§æ‡§ó ‡§î‡§∞ ‡§∂‡§∞‡•Ä‡§∞ ‡§ï‡•ã **Peak Performance** ‡§ï‡•á ‡§≤‡§ø‡§è ‡§§‡•à‡§Ø‡§æ‡§∞ ‡§ï‡§∞‡§®‡§æ ‡§π‡•à‡•§

---

### **1. The Core Mechanics: The 7-Day Protocol**

‡§Ö‡§ó‡§≤‡•á 7 ‡§¶‡§ø‡§® ‡§Ü‡§™‡§ï‡•ã ‡§è‡§ï **Monk (‡§∏‡§æ‡§ß‡•Å)** ‡§î‡§∞ ‡§è‡§ï **Soldier (‡§∏‡•à‡§®‡§ø‡§ï)** ‡§ï‡•Ä ‡§§‡§∞‡§π ‡§ú‡•Ä‡§®‡•á ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç‡•§

#### **Protocol 1: Biological Clock Reset**

* **The Rule:** ‡§Ö‡§ó‡§∞ ‡§Ü‡§™‡§ï‡§æ Interview ‡§∏‡•Å‡§¨‡§π 10 ‡§¨‡§ú‡•á ‡§π‡•à, ‡§§‡•ã ‡§Ö‡§ó‡§≤‡•á 7 ‡§¶‡§ø‡§® ‡§†‡•Ä‡§ï 10 ‡§¨‡§ú‡•á ‡§Ü‡§™ **"Active Mode"** ‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç ‡§π‡•ã‡§®‡•á ‡§ö‡§æ‡§π‡§ø‡§è‡•§
* **Action:** ‡§∞‡•ã‡§ú ‡§∏‡•Å‡§¨‡§π 10 ‡§¨‡§ú‡•á ‡§®‡§π‡§æ-‡§ß‡•ã‡§ï‡§∞, ‡§´‡•â‡§∞‡•ç‡§Æ‡§≤ ‡§ï‡§™‡§°‡§º‡•á ‡§™‡§π‡§®‡§ï‡§∞ ‡§ï‡•Å‡§∞‡•ç‡§∏‡•Ä ‡§™‡§∞ ‡§¨‡•à‡§†‡•á‡§Ç ‡§î‡§∞ ‡§ú‡•ã‡§∞-‡§ú‡•ã‡§∞ ‡§∏‡•á (Loudly) ‡§Ö‡§ñ‡§¨‡§æ‡§∞ ‡§™‡§¢‡§º‡•á‡§Ç ‡§Ø‡§æ Mock ‡§¶‡•á‡§Ç‡•§
* **Why:** ‡§§‡§æ‡§ï‡§ø Interview ‡§µ‡§æ‡§≤‡•á ‡§¶‡§ø‡§® 10 ‡§¨‡§ú‡•á ‡§Ü‡§™‡§ï‡§æ ‡§¶‡§ø‡§Æ‡§æ‡§ó ‡§∏‡§¨‡§∏‡•á ‡§ú‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ‡§¶‡§æ Sharp ‡§π‡•ã‡•§ (Circadian Rhythm).

#### **Protocol 2: The Information Diet**

* **The Rule:** "Negative News" ‡§¨‡§Ç‡§¶‡•§
* **Action:** ‡§ï‡•ç‡§∞‡§æ‡§á‡§Æ, ‡§∞‡•á‡§™ ‡§Ø‡§æ ‡§∞‡§æ‡§ú‡§®‡•Ä‡§§‡§ø ‡§ï‡•Ä ‡§ñ‡§¨‡§∞‡•á‡§Ç ‡§™‡§¢‡§º‡§®‡§æ ‡§ï‡§Æ ‡§ï‡§∞‡•á‡§Ç‡•§ ‡§∏‡§ø‡§∞‡•ç‡§´ **Editorials** ‡§î‡§∞ **Positive Case Studies** ‡§™‡§¢‡§º‡•á‡§Ç‡•§
* **Why:** ‡§ú‡•à‡§∏‡§æ ‡§á‡§®‡§™‡•Å‡§ü ‡§π‡•ã‡§ó‡§æ, ‡§µ‡•à‡§∏‡§æ ‡§Ü‡§â‡§ü‡§™‡•Å‡§ü‡•§ ‡§Ö‡§ó‡§∞ ‡§Ü‡§™ ‡§ï‡§ö‡§∞‡§æ ‡§™‡§¢‡§º‡•á‡§Ç‡§ó‡•á, ‡§§‡•ã Interview ‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç ‡§Æ‡•Å‡§Ç‡§π ‡§∏‡•á ‡§®‡§ø‡§∞‡§æ‡§∂‡§æ (Pessimism) ‡§®‡§ø‡§ï‡§≤‡•á‡§ó‡•Ä‡•§

#### **Protocol 3: The "Uniform" Test**

* **The Rule:** ‡§®‡§è ‡§ï‡§™‡§°‡§º‡•á Interview ‡§µ‡§æ‡§≤‡•á ‡§¶‡§ø‡§® ‡§® ‡§™‡§π‡§®‡•á‡§Ç‡•§
* **Action:** ‡§Ö‡§™‡§®‡•á Interview ‡§µ‡§æ‡§≤‡•á ‡§ï‡§™‡§°‡§º‡•á (Shirt, Tie, Saree, Shoes) ‡§ï‡§Æ ‡§∏‡•á ‡§ï‡§Æ 2 ‡§¨‡§æ‡§∞ ‡§™‡§π‡§®‡§ï‡§∞ Mock ‡§¶‡•á‡§Ç ‡§Ø‡§æ ‡§ò‡§∞ ‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç ‡§ü‡§π‡§≤‡•á‡§Ç‡•§
* **Why:** ‡§Ö‡§ó‡§∞ ‡§ï‡•â‡§≤‡§∞ ‡§ü‡§æ‡§á‡§ü ‡§π‡•à ‡§Ø‡§æ ‡§ú‡•Ç‡§§‡•á ‡§ï‡§æ‡§ü ‡§∞‡§π‡•á ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç, ‡§§‡•ã ‡§Ü‡§™‡§ï‡§æ ‡§ß‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ‡§® Board ‡§™‡§∞ ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç, ‡§Ö‡§™‡§®‡•á ‡§¶‡§∞‡•ç‡§¶ ‡§™‡§∞ ‡§π‡•ã‡§ó‡§æ‡•§

---

### **2. The 5 Examples: Small Things, Big Impact**

Interview ‡§µ‡§æ‡§≤‡•á ‡§¶‡§ø‡§® ‡§Ø‡•á ‡§õ‡•ã‡§ü‡•Ä ‡§ó‡§≤‡§§‡§ø‡§Ø‡§æ‡§Ç ‡§≠‡§æ‡§∞‡•Ä ‡§™‡§°‡§º‡§§‡•Ä ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç‡•§ ‡§¶‡•á‡§ñ‡§ø‡§è ‡§è‡§ï Officer ‡§ï‡•à‡§∏‡•á ‡§§‡•à‡§Ø‡§æ‡§∞ ‡§π‡•ã‡§§‡§æ ‡§π‡•à‡•§

#### **Scenario 1: The "Waiting Room" Stress**

**Situation:** ‡§Ü‡§™ ‡§¨‡§æ‡§π‡§∞ ‡§¨‡•à‡§†‡•á ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç‡•§ ‡§Ö‡§Ç‡§¶‡§∞ ‡§∏‡•á ‡§ï‡•ã‡§à ‡§®‡§ø‡§ï‡§≤‡§æ ‡§î‡§∞ ‡§¨‡•ã‡§≤‡§æ *"‡§≠‡§æ‡§à, ‡§¨‡§π‡•Å‡§§ ‡§ñ‡§§‡§∞‡§®‡§æ‡§ï ‡§¨‡•ã‡§∞‡•ç‡§° ‡§π‡•à, ‡§´‡§æ‡§°‡§º ‡§¶‡§ø‡§Ø‡§æ ‡§Æ‡•Å‡§ù‡•á‡•§"*

* ‚ùå **Student:** (Panic) ‡§™‡§∏‡•Ä‡§®‡§æ ‡§™‡•ã‡§Ç‡§õ‡§®‡•á ‡§≤‡§ó‡§§‡§æ ‡§π‡•à, ‡§®‡•ã‡§ü‡•ç‡§∏ ‡§™‡§≤‡§ü‡§®‡•á ‡§≤‡§ó‡§§‡§æ ‡§π‡•à‡•§
* ‚úÖ **Officer:** (Smiles) ‡§ï‡§æ‡§® ‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç ‡§∞‡•Å‡§à (Imaginary earplugs) ‡§°‡§æ‡§≤ ‡§≤‡•á‡§§‡§æ ‡§π‡•à‡•§
* *Thinking:* "‡§â‡§∏‡§ï‡§æ ‡§™‡•á‡§™‡§∞ ‡§ñ‡§∞‡§æ‡§¨ ‡§π‡•Å‡§Ü, ‡§Æ‡•á‡§∞‡§æ ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç‡•§ ‡§Æ‡•á‡§∞‡§æ ‡§Æ‡•à‡§ö ‡§Ö‡§≠‡•Ä ‡§¨‡§æ‡§ï‡•Ä ‡§π‡•à‡•§" (Mental Insulation).



#### **Scenario 2: The "Sleep" Trap**

**Situation:** Interview ‡§∏‡•á ‡§™‡§π‡§≤‡•á ‡§µ‡§æ‡§≤‡•Ä ‡§∞‡§æ‡§§ ‡§®‡•Ä‡§Ç‡§¶ ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç ‡§Ü ‡§∞‡§π‡•Ä‡•§

* ‚ùå **Student:** ‡§∞‡§æ‡§§ ‡§≠‡§∞ ‡§ï‡§∞‡§µ‡§ü ‡§¨‡§¶‡§≤‡§§‡§æ ‡§π‡•à, ‡§∏‡•Å‡§¨‡§π ‡§≤‡§æ‡§≤ ‡§Ü‡§Ç‡§ñ‡•ã‡§Ç ‡§ï‡•á ‡§∏‡§æ‡§• ‡§â‡§†‡§§‡§æ ‡§π‡•à‡•§
* ‚úÖ **Officer:**
* 9 PM: Phone Switch Off.
* 10 PM: Warm Milk + Deep Breathing.
* *Mantra:* "‡§Æ‡•à‡§Ç‡§®‡•á ‡§Æ‡•á‡§π‡§®‡§§ ‡§ï‡•Ä ‡§π‡•à‡•§ ‡§Ö‡§¨ ‡§ú‡•ã ‡§π‡•ã‡§ó‡§æ ‡§¶‡•á‡§ñ‡§æ ‡§ú‡§æ‡§è‡§ó‡§æ‡•§" (Sleep is the best revision).



#### **Scenario 3: The "Entry" Ritual**

**Situation:** ‡§¶‡§∞‡§µ‡§æ‡§ú‡§æ ‡§ñ‡•ã‡§≤‡§®‡•á ‡§∏‡•á ‡§†‡•Ä‡§ï ‡§™‡§π‡§≤‡•á ‡§ï‡§æ 10 ‡§∏‡•á‡§ï‡§Ç‡§°‡•§

* ‚ùå **Student:** (Thinking) "‡§π‡•á ‡§≠‡§ó‡§µ‡§æ‡§®, ‡§™‡•ç‡§≤‡•Ä‡§ú ‡§Ü‡§∏‡§æ‡§® ‡§∏‡§µ‡§æ‡§≤ ‡§™‡•Ç‡§õ‡§®‡§æ‡•§" (Begging mindset).
* ‚úÖ **Officer:**
* ‡§ï‡§Ç‡§ß‡•ã‡§Ç ‡§ï‡•ã ‡§™‡•Ä‡§õ‡•á ‡§ñ‡•Ä‡§Ç‡§ö‡§§‡§æ ‡§π‡•à (Shoulders back)‡•§
* ‡§è‡§ï ‡§ó‡§π‡§∞‡•Ä ‡§∏‡§æ‡§Ç‡§∏ ‡§≤‡•á‡§§‡§æ ‡§π‡•à (Deep Breath)‡•§
* *Thinking:* "‡§Æ‡•Å‡§ù‡•á ‡§Ö‡§Ç‡§¶‡§∞ ‡§ú‡§æ‡§ï‡§∞ ‡§á‡§® 5 ‡§µ‡§∞‡§ø‡§∑‡•ç‡§† ‡§≤‡•ã‡§ó‡•ã‡§Ç ‡§∏‡•á **‡§¨‡§æ‡§§** ‡§ï‡§∞‡§®‡•Ä ‡§π‡•à‡•§ ‡§Æ‡•Å‡§ù‡•á ‡§â‡§®‡•ç‡§π‡•á‡§Ç ‡§ú‡§æ‡§®‡§®‡§æ ‡§π‡•à ‡§î‡§∞ ‡§â‡§®‡•ç‡§π‡•á‡§Ç ‡§Æ‡•Å‡§ù‡•á ‡§ú‡§æ‡§®‡§®‡§æ ‡§π‡•à‡•§" (Equality mindset).



#### **Scenario 4: The "Breakfast" Mistake**

* ‚ùå **Student:** ‡§≠‡•Ç‡§ñ ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç ‡§π‡•à ‡§§‡•ã ‡§ï‡•Å‡§õ ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç ‡§ñ‡§æ‡§Ø‡§æ, ‡§Ø‡§æ ‡§™‡•á‡§ü ‡§≠‡§∞‡§ï‡§∞ ‡§™‡§∞‡§æ‡§Ç‡§†‡•á ‡§ñ‡§æ ‡§≤‡§ø‡§è (‡§®‡•Ä‡§Ç‡§¶ ‡§Ü‡§è‡§ó‡•Ä)‡•§
* ‚úÖ **Officer:**
* Light Protein (Eggs/Poha/Fruits).
* Hydration (Water), but not too much right before entry.



#### **Scenario 5: The "Document" Panic**

* ‚ùå **Student:** ‡§∏‡•Å‡§¨‡§π 8 ‡§¨‡§ú‡•á ‡§´‡•ã‡§ü‡•ã‡§ï‡•â‡§™‡•Ä ‡§¢‡•Ç‡§Ç‡§¢ ‡§∞‡§π‡§æ ‡§π‡•à‡•§
* ‚úÖ **Officer:**
* 2 ‡§¶‡§ø‡§® ‡§™‡§π‡§≤‡•á ‡§π‡•Ä "Interview Kit" (Admit Card, Photos, Pen, Water) ‡§§‡•à‡§Ø‡§æ‡§∞ ‡§ï‡§∞‡§ï‡•á ‡§Æ‡•á‡§ú ‡§™‡§∞ ‡§∞‡§ñ‡•Ä ‡§π‡•à‡•§ No last-minute rush.



---

### **3. Potential Board Questions (Mental Prep)**

‡§Ø‡•á ‡§∏‡§µ‡§æ‡§≤ Board ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç, ‡§Ü‡§™‡§ï‡§æ **‡§¶‡§ø‡§Æ‡§æ‡§ó** ‡§Ü‡§™‡§∏‡•á ‡§™‡•Ç‡§õ‡•á‡§ó‡§æ‡•§ ‡§á‡§®‡§ï‡§æ ‡§ú‡§µ‡§æ‡§¨ ‡§Ö‡§≠‡•Ä ‡§§‡•à‡§Ø‡§æ‡§∞ ‡§ï‡§∞‡•á‡§Ç‡•§

**Type A: The Imposter Syndrome**

1. **Brain:** *"‡§§‡•Å‡§ù‡•á ‡§§‡•ã ‡§ï‡•Å‡§õ ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç ‡§Ü‡§§‡§æ‡•§ ‡§§‡•Ç‡§®‡•á ‡§¨‡§∏ ‡§∞‡§ü‡•ç‡§ü‡§æ ‡§Æ‡§æ‡§∞‡§æ ‡§π‡•à‡•§"*
* **You:** "‡§Æ‡•à‡§Ç‡§®‡•á Mains ‡§®‡§ø‡§ï‡§æ‡§≤‡§æ ‡§π‡•à‡•§ ‡§Æ‡•à‡§Ç ‡§°‡§ø‡§ú‡§∞‡•ç‡§µ ‡§ï‡§∞‡§§‡§æ ‡§π‡•Ç‡§Å‡•§ ‡§Æ‡•Å‡§ù‡•á ‡§∏‡§¨ ‡§ï‡•Å‡§õ ‡§ú‡§æ‡§®‡§®‡•á ‡§ï‡•Ä ‡§ú‡§∞‡•Ç‡§∞‡§§ ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç, ‡§¨‡§∏ '‡§∏‡•Ä‡§ñ‡§®‡•á ‡§ï‡•Ä ‡§≤‡§≤‡§ï' (Willingness to learn) ‡§ö‡§æ‡§π‡§ø‡§è‡•§"



**Type B: The Failure Fear**
2.  **Brain:** *"‡§Ö‡§ó‡§∞ ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç ‡§π‡•Å‡§Ü ‡§§‡•ã? ‡§™‡§æ‡§™‡§æ ‡§ï‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ ‡§ï‡§π‡•á‡§Ç‡§ó‡•á?"*
* **You:** "‡§Ø‡§π ‡§ú‡§ø‡§Ç‡§¶‡§ó‡•Ä ‡§ï‡§æ ‡§Ü‡§ñ‡§ø‡§∞‡•Ä ‡§è‡§ó‡•ç‡§ú‡§æ‡§Æ ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç ‡§π‡•à‡•§ ‡§Æ‡•à‡§Ç ‡§Ö‡§™‡§®‡§æ 100% ‡§¶‡•Ç‡§Ç‡§ó‡§æ, ‡§™‡§∞‡§ø‡§£‡§æ‡§Æ ‡§Æ‡•á‡§∞‡•á ‡§π‡§æ‡§• ‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç ‡§π‡•à‡•§" (Stoic Mindset).

**Type C: The Comparison Trap**
3.  **Brain:** *"‡§µ‡•ã ‡§¶‡•á‡§ñ‡•ã, ‡§µ‡•ã ‡§≤‡§°‡§º‡§ï‡§æ ‡§ï‡§ø‡§§‡§®‡§æ ‡§∏‡•ç‡§Æ‡§æ‡§∞‡•ç‡§ü ‡§≤‡§ó ‡§∞‡§π‡§æ ‡§π‡•à, ‡§á‡§Ç‡§ó‡•ç‡§≤‡§ø‡§∂ ‡§¨‡•ã‡§≤ ‡§∞‡§π‡§æ ‡§π‡•à‡•§"*
* **You:** "‡§â‡§∏‡§ï‡•Ä ‡§≤‡§°‡§º‡§æ‡§à ‡§Ö‡§≤‡§ó ‡§π‡•à, ‡§Æ‡•á‡§∞‡•Ä ‡§Ö‡§≤‡§ó‡•§ ‡§¨‡•ã‡§∞‡•ç‡§° ‡§ï‡•ã '‡§∏‡•ç‡§Æ‡§æ‡§∞‡•ç‡§ü‡§®‡•á‡§∏' ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç, '‡§à‡§Æ‡§æ‡§®‡§¶‡§æ‡§∞‡•Ä' (Integrity) ‡§ö‡§æ‡§π‡§ø‡§è, ‡§ú‡•ã ‡§Æ‡•á‡§∞‡•á ‡§™‡§æ‡§∏ ‡§π‡•à‡•§"

---

### **4. How to Prepare (The Perfect Way: Visualization)**

Olympic ‡§è‡§•‡§≤‡•Ä‡§ü‡•ç‡§∏ ‡§¶‡•å‡§°‡§º‡§®‡•á ‡§∏‡•á ‡§™‡§π‡§≤‡•á ‡§¶‡§ø‡§Æ‡§æ‡§ó ‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç ‡§¶‡•å‡§°‡§º ‡§™‡•Ç‡§∞‡•Ä ‡§ï‡§∞ ‡§≤‡•á‡§§‡•á ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç‡•§ ‡§á‡§∏‡•á **Visualization** ‡§ï‡§π‡§§‡•á ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç‡•§

#### **Drill 1: The "Movie Director" Technique**

* **Task:** ‡§∞‡•ã‡§ú ‡§∞‡§æ‡§§ ‡§ï‡•ã ‡§∏‡•ã‡§®‡•á ‡§∏‡•á ‡§™‡§π‡§≤‡•á 5 ‡§Æ‡§ø‡§®‡§ü ‡§ï‡•Ä ‡§è‡§ï "Mental Movie" ‡§ö‡§≤‡§æ‡§è‡§Ç:
* *Scene 1:* ‡§Ü‡§™ ‡§®‡§π‡§æ-‡§ß‡•ã‡§ï‡§∞ ‡§§‡•à‡§Ø‡§æ‡§∞ ‡§π‡•ã ‡§∞‡§π‡•á ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç (Feel confident).
* *Scene 2:* ‡§Ü‡§™ ‡§∞‡•Ç‡§Æ ‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç ‡§ò‡•Å‡§∏ ‡§∞‡§π‡•á ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç (Walk like a Tiger).
* *Scene 3:* ‡§Ü‡§™ ‡§π‡§Ç‡§∏‡§ï‡§∞ "Sorry Sir" ‡§¨‡•ã‡§≤ ‡§∞‡§π‡•á ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç (No Panic).
* *Scene 4:* ‡§Ü‡§™ ‡§π‡§æ‡§• ‡§Æ‡§ø‡§≤‡§æ‡§ï‡§∞ ‡§¨‡§æ‡§π‡§∞ ‡§Ü ‡§∞‡§π‡•á ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç ‡§î‡§∞ ‡§ñ‡•Å‡§∂ ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç‡•§


* **Benefit:** ‡§¶‡§ø‡§Æ‡§æ‡§ó ‡§ï‡•ã ‡§≤‡§ó‡•á‡§ó‡§æ ‡§Ø‡§π ‡§∏‡§¨ ‡§™‡§π‡§≤‡•á ‡§π‡•ã ‡§ö‡•Å‡§ï‡§æ ‡§π‡•à, ‡§§‡•ã ‡§µ‡§π‡§æ‡§Ç ‡§°‡§∞ ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç ‡§≤‡§ó‡•á‡§ó‡§æ‡•§ (D√©j√† vu effect).

#### **Drill 2: The "Power Pose" (Amy Cuddy Rule)**

* **Task:** ‡§á‡§Ç‡§ü‡§∞‡§µ‡•ç‡§Ø‡•Ç ‡§µ‡§æ‡§≤‡•á ‡§¶‡§ø‡§®, ‡§µ‡•á‡§ü‡§ø‡§Ç‡§ó ‡§∞‡•Ç‡§Æ ‡§ï‡•á ‡§ü‡•â‡§Ø‡§≤‡•á‡§ü ‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç ‡§ú‡§æ‡§è‡§Ç‡•§
* **Action:** 2 ‡§Æ‡§ø‡§®‡§ü ‡§ï‡•á ‡§≤‡§ø‡§è "Superman Pose" (‡§π‡§æ‡§• ‡§ï‡§Æ‡§∞ ‡§™‡§∞, ‡§™‡•à‡§∞ ‡§ö‡•å‡§°‡§º‡•á, ‡§∏‡•Ä‡§®‡§æ ‡§§‡§®‡§æ ‡§π‡•Å‡§Ü) ‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç ‡§ñ‡§°‡§º‡•á ‡§π‡•ã‡§Ç‡•§
* **Benefit:** ‡§Ø‡§π Scientifically ‡§Ü‡§™‡§ï‡•á Cortisol (Stress hormone) ‡§ï‡•ã ‡§ï‡§Æ ‡§ï‡§∞‡§§‡§æ ‡§π‡•à ‡§î‡§∞ Testosterone (Confidence hormone) ‡§ï‡•ã ‡§¨‡§¢‡§º‡§æ‡§§‡§æ ‡§π‡•à‡•§

---

### **5. Neuro-Interrogation (Final Check)**

1. **Smile Check:** *"‡§ï‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ ‡§Æ‡•à‡§Ç ‡§∂‡•Ä‡§∂‡•á ‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç ‡§ñ‡•Å‡§¶ ‡§ï‡•ã ‡§¶‡•á‡§ñ‡§ï‡§∞ ‡§∏‡•ç‡§Æ‡§æ‡§á‡§≤ ‡§ï‡§∞ ‡§∏‡§ï‡§§‡§æ ‡§π‡•Ç‡§Å?"*
* (‡§Ö‡§ó‡§∞ ‡§Ü‡§™ ‡§ñ‡•Å‡§¶ ‡§ï‡•ã ‡§™‡§∏‡§Ç‡§¶ ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç ‡§ï‡§∞‡§§‡•á, ‡§§‡•ã ‡§¨‡•ã‡§∞‡•ç‡§° ‡§ï‡•à‡§∏‡•á ‡§ï‡§∞‡•á‡§ó‡§æ?)


2. **Gratitude Check:** *"‡§ï‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ ‡§Æ‡•à‡§Ç‡§®‡•á ‡§â‡§® ‡§≤‡•ã‡§ó‡•ã‡§Ç ‡§ï‡•ã ‡§∂‡•Å‡§ï‡•ç‡§∞‡§ø‡§Ø‡§æ ‡§ï‡§π‡§æ ‡§ú‡§ø‡§®‡•ç‡§π‡•ã‡§Ç‡§®‡•á ‡§Æ‡§¶‡§¶ ‡§ï‡•Ä?"*
* (Gratitude keeps you humble and positive.)



---

### **6. Overall Effect on Interview**

‡§ú‡§¨ ‡§Ü‡§™ ‡§Ø‡•á 7 ‡§¶‡§ø‡§® ‡§ï‡•Ä ‡§ï‡§Ç‡§°‡•Ä‡§∂‡§®‡§ø‡§Ç‡§ó ‡§ï‡§∞ ‡§≤‡•á‡§§‡•á ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç:

1. **Aura:** ‡§Ü‡§™ ‡§ï‡§Æ‡§∞‡•á ‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç "Positive Vibes" ‡§≤‡•á‡§ï‡§∞ ‡§ò‡•Å‡§∏‡§§‡•á ‡§π‡•à‡§Ç‡•§ Board ‡§ï‡•ã ‡§Ö‡§ö‡•ç‡§õ‡§æ ‡§≤‡§ó‡§§‡§æ ‡§π‡•à‡•§
2. **Sharpness:** ‡§Ö‡§ö‡•ç‡§õ‡•Ä ‡§®‡•Ä‡§Ç‡§¶ ‡§ï‡•á ‡§ï‡§æ‡§∞‡§£ ‡§Ü‡§™‡§ï‡§æ ‡§¶‡§ø‡§Æ‡§æ‡§ó "Verbal Bullets" (Chapter 4) ‡§´‡§æ‡§Ø‡§∞ ‡§ï‡§∞‡§®‡•á ‡§ï‡•á ‡§≤‡§ø‡§è ‡§§‡•à‡§Ø‡§æ‡§∞ ‡§π‡•ã‡§§‡§æ ‡§π‡•à‡•§
3. **Resilience:** ‡§Ö‡§ó‡§∞ ‡§™‡§π‡§≤‡§æ ‡§∏‡§µ‡§æ‡§≤ ‡§¨‡§æ‡§â‡§Ç‡§∏‡§∞ ‡§≠‡•Ä ‡§π‡•ã, ‡§§‡•ã ‡§Ü‡§™ ‡§ò‡§¨‡§∞‡§æ‡§§‡•á ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç, ‡§ï‡•ç‡§Ø‡•ã‡§Ç‡§ï‡§ø ‡§Ü‡§™‡§®‡•á "Mental Movie" ‡§Æ‡•á‡§Ç ‡§á‡§∏‡§ï‡•Ä ‡§™‡•ç‡§∞‡•à‡§ï‡•ç‡§ü‡§ø‡§∏ ‡§ï‡•Ä ‡§•‡•Ä‡•§

---

### **Today's Action Plan (‡§Ü‡§ú ‡§ï‡§æ ‡§π‡•ã‡§Æ‡§µ‡§∞‡•ç‡§ï)**

1. **Lock:** ‡§Ö‡§™‡§®‡•á ‡§∏‡•ã‡§®‡•á ‡§î‡§∞ ‡§ú‡§æ‡§ó‡§®‡•á ‡§ï‡§æ ‡§∏‡§Æ‡§Ø ‡§Ü‡§ú ‡§∏‡•á ‡§´‡§ø‡§ï‡•ç‡§∏ ‡§ï‡§∞‡•á‡§Ç (11 PM - 7 AM).

3. **Promise:** ‡§∂‡•Ä‡§∂‡•á ‡§ï‡•á ‡§∏‡§æ‡§Æ‡§®‡•á ‡§ñ‡§°‡§º‡•á ‡§π‡•ã‡§ï‡§∞ ‡§ñ‡•Å‡§¶ ‡§∏‡•á ‡§µ‡§æ‡§¶‡§æ ‡§ï‡§∞‡•á‡§Ç:
* *"‡§Ö‡§ó‡§≤‡•á 7 ‡§¶‡§ø‡§® ‡§Æ‡•à‡§Ç ‡§ï‡•ã‡§à ‡§®‡§à ‡§ï‡§ø‡§§‡§æ‡§¨ ‡§®‡§π‡•Ä‡§Ç ‡§ñ‡§∞‡•Ä‡§¶‡•Ç‡§Ç‡§ó‡§æ‡•§"*
* *"‡§Æ‡•à‡§Ç ‡§Ö‡§™‡§®‡•Ä ‡§∏‡•á‡§π‡§§ ‡§ï‡§æ ‡§ñ‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ‡§≤ ‡§∞‡§ñ‡•Ç‡§Ç‡§ó‡§æ‡•§"*
* *"‡§Æ‡•à‡§Ç ‡§è‡§ï Officer ‡§ï‡•Ä ‡§§‡§∞‡§π ‡§∏‡•ã‡§ö‡•Ç‡§Ç‡§ó‡§æ‡•§"*
